Frontend-first, modular youth football talent management system for a single club.

== Changelog ==

= 4.20.23 — Persona dashboard: `ActivePlayersTotal` KPI deep-links with `filter[status]=active` so the destination row count matches the headline (closes #1209). Audit 6 (#1180) flagged the parity gap: `ActivePlayersTotal::compute()` filters `p.status = 'active'`, but the destination players list applies only `filter[archived]=active` and does NOT filter by `status` — so trial / released / inactive players with `archived_at IS NULL` show in the list but not in the count. #478 surfaced the same drift class as a 30/29 mismatch in demo mode; the demo-scope was threaded through then, the status-parity gap was missed. **Fix — two pieces, one PR.** (1) `PlayersRestController::list_players` extends its filter whitelist to accept `filter[status]=<value>`, mirroring the existing `tt_players.status` column. The param is optional; default behaviour (no `filter[status]`) is unchanged. (2) `ActivePlayersTotal::linkUrl()` overrides the base implementation to append `filter[status]=active` to the destination URL. Lands live in the dominant `kpi_card` placement courtesy of v4.20.22's `KpiCardWidget` → `linkUrl()` routing fix (#1207). **Acceptance.** Operator with 12 active + 5 trial players sees KPI "12 active players" → clicks → lands on a 12-row list, not 17. Sibling status filters (trial, released, inactive) are now reachable via direct URL too — useful for future per-status KPIs. Patch bump. (closes #1209) =


= 4.20.22 — Persona dashboard: `KpiCardWidget` now honours per-KPI `linkUrl()` overrides via a shared `AbstractWidget::kpiHrefFor()` helper (closes #1207). Audit 6 (#1180) surfaced a structural defect: `KpiCardWidget::render()` only consulted the legacy `linkView()` builder, so every per-KPI `linkUrl( $ctx )` override added in #771 / #481 (carrying filter query-strings for date windows + team scope) was dead code in the dominant `kpi_card` slot — used by `CoreTemplates::addKpiCard()` for every persona's default template. The overrides only fired when the same KPI was placed in a `kpi_strip`, which is the HoD top-hero exception. Coaches clicking "My team attendance %" from their default dashboard landed on bare `?tt_view=activities` instead of the prefiltered list. **Fix.** New `AbstractWidget::kpiHrefFor( $source, $ctx ): string` resolves the deep-link URL with the right builder — prefers `linkUrl( $ctx )` when the data source overrides it (carries filter query-strings), falls back to `linkView()` when only the legacy view-slug builder is available, returns empty when the KPI is inert. Both `KpiCardWidget::render()` and `KpiStripWidget::render()` now route through this helper so the linkUrl-first lookup is structurally shared — no future widget surfacing KPIs (`RateCardHeroWidget` etc.) can repeat KpiCardWidget's omission. Inline comments reference the audit + the bug history so subsequent edits don't reflex-revert. **Unlocks dead code.** Five sibling KPI overrides (#1209-#1213 in audit 6) become live the moment this lands — until now those overrides existed in the KPI classes but never fired from the kpi_card slot. They drain next in dependency order. **No behaviour change for inert KPIs.** KPIs that declare neither `linkUrl()` nor `linkView()` continue to render as non-clickable cards, exactly as before. Patch bump. (closes #1207) =


= 4.20.21 — Architecture: LookupTranslator into Pdp repositories — module-by-module rollout (closes #1080; closes #806's first-round sweep). **Final** slice in the #806 series after #1081 (Evaluations), #1077 (Goals, v4.20.18), #1078 (Activities, v4.20.19), and #1079 (Players, v4.20.20). All four module-specific follow-ups (#1077-#1080) and the worked-example slice (#1081) now ship. **Mechanical shape.** Pdp differs from the prior slices in that two existing repositories already cover the relevant tables — `PdpFilesRepository` for `tt_pdp_files.status` and `PdpVerdictsRepository` for `tt_pdp_verdicts.decision`. Rather than creating a new wrapper, this slice adds a `hydrate()` static helper to each existing repo and runs all read methods through it. **`PdpFilesRepository` hydration.** Every read (`find`, `findByPlayerSeason`, `listForCoach`, `listForSeason`) now decorates rows in place with `status_localised` resolved via `LookupTranslator::byTypeAndName( 'pdp_status', $raw )`. Falls back to the canonical English label switch (`PdpStatus::OPEN → 'Open'` etc.) when the lookup row isn't seeded yet (fresh install pre-migration 0112). Raw `status` stays for back-compat — the upsert gate validates against `PdpStatus::ALL` and filter dropdowns key off the canonical codes. **`PdpVerdictsRepository` hydration.** `findForFile` now decorates rows with `decision_localised` via the repository's existing static `label()` helper (which already routes through `LookupTranslator::byTypeAndName( 'pdp_verdict_decision', $code )` with a canonical English fallback). **`FrontendMyPdpView` refactor.** `renderVerdictCard()` now echoes `$verdict->decision_localised` directly; the inline `decisionLabel()` switch helper at the bottom of the view (a stale duplicate of `PdpVerdictsRepository::label()`) is deleted along with the now-unused `PdpVerdictDecision` import. **#806 series complete.** All five slices now hydrate at the repository boundary. The remaining consumer-callsite cleanup (FrontendPdpManageView, FrontendPdpPlanningView, REST verdict surface, KPI sources) happens incrementally as each is touched; the CI lint allow-list tightens module-by-module once those land. Patch bump. (closes #1080) =

= 4.20.20 — Architecture: LookupTranslator into Players repository — module-by-module rollout (closes #1079; refs #806 / #1080). Fourth slice after #1081 (Evaluations), #1077 (Goals, v4.20.18), and #1078 (Activities, v4.20.19). View code echoes `$player->status_localised` + `$player->preferred_foot_localised` rather than calling `LabelTranslator::playerStatus( $player->status )` / `LookupTranslator::byTypeAndName('foot_options', $player->preferred_foot)` inline; bypass impossible at the view layer for any future site that goes through the repository fetch. **New `Infrastructure\Players\PlayersRepository`.** One read method this slice: `find( int $id )` returns the active (non-archived) player row hydrated with `status_localised` (via `LabelTranslator::playerStatus`) and `preferred_foot_localised` (via `LookupTranslator::byTypeAndName`). The hydration tries the canonical seeded slug `foot_options` first, falls back to the historic singular `foot_option` slug that one legacy callsite used (FrontendMyProfileView line 108 pre-refactor) — operators with either seed shape get the right Dutch label. Raw `status` + `preferred_foot` stay on the row for back-compat (KPI joins, filter dropdowns, JSON exports). **`FrontendPlayersManageView::loadPlayer` refactor.** The view's private fetch helper now delegates to `PlayersRepository::find()`; inline SQL + per-row LabelTranslator/LookupTranslator calls remain in the existing view render code where they were — same module-by-module discipline as #1077 / #1078. New consumers that go through `loadPlayer` get pre-localised fields by construction. **Position labels deliberately not hydrated.** `preferred_positions` is a JSON array on `tt_players`; per-element translation belongs to a helper, not a row-level field. Same scoping discipline as the previous slices that left adjacent translation paths untouched. **What this is NOT.** Not a sweep of every Players callsite (FrontendPlayerDetailView's hero pill, REST list endpoint, FrontendMyProfileView's Playing details card, exporters) — those keep their existing inline translation calls until each is touched separately. CI lint allow-list tightens for Players once those land. **Refs remaining slice.** #1080 (Pdp) — last in the #806 series. Patch bump. (closes #1079) =

= 4.20.19 — Architecture: LookupTranslator into Activities repository — module-by-module rollout (closes #1078; refs #806 / #1079-1080). Third slice after #1081 (Evaluations, v4.17.2) and #1077 (Goals, v4.20.18). View code echoes `$row->activity_type_localised` and `$row->attendance_status_localised`; bypass impossible at the view layer. **New `Infrastructure\Activities\ActivitiesRepository`.** Single read method this slice: `findForPlayer( int $activity_id, int $player_id )` returns the activity row with the player's `tt_attendance` row JOIN'd onto it (one query instead of the previous two — activity fetch + separate attendance lookup). Hydrates `activity_type_localised` via `LabelTranslator::activityType()` (which routes through LookupTranslator for operator-added rows per #1121) with a humanise-fallback for custom types lacking translation; hydrates `attendance_status_localised` via `LabelTranslator::attendanceStatus()` when an attendance row exists, `null` otherwise. Raw `activity_type_key` + `attendance_status` stay for back-compat — KPI joins + filter dropdowns key off the canonical codes. **`FrontendMyActivitiesView::renderDetail()` refactor.** The `?tt_view=my-activities&id=N` detail surface routes through the repository. Inline activity SQL + separate attendance fetch + per-section LabelTranslator calls in the render path are replaced by the localised fields. The back-compat `$att` synthetic object built from the join fields keeps the rest of the render block (notes section) reading unchanged. **`plan_state` deliberately not pre-localised.** It's an engine-internal workflow state, not a user-facing pill on any surface today; the issue's "lookup-backed fields" list is aspirational on that field. **What this is NOT.** Not a sweep of every Activities callsite (FrontendActivitiesManageView, FrontendTeamDetailView, REST list endpoint, Planner cards, exporters) — same module-by-module pattern as #1077 / #1081 which each refactored one canonical view. The CI lint allow-list tightens for Activities once those callsites land. **Refs remaining slices.** #1079 (Players), #1080 (Pdp). Patch bump. (closes #1078) =

= 4.20.18 — Architecture: LookupTranslator into Goals repository — module-by-module rollout (closes #1077; refs #806 / #1078-1080). Second slice after #1081 shipped the Evaluations module under v4.17.2. Same shape: view code echoes `$row->status_localised` / `$row->priority_localised` instead of calling `LabelTranslator::goalStatus( $row->status )` inline, so bypass becomes structurally impossible at the view layer. **Mechanical difference vs. #1081.** Evaluations had a FK to `tt_lookups` so the precedent hydrated via `LookupTranslator::name()` after pulling the full lookup row. Goals store `status` + `priority` as code strings directly on `tt_goals` (no FK), so the per-row hydration calls the existing `LabelTranslator::goalStatus()` / `LabelTranslator::goalPriority()` switches. The contract is identical — repository returns pre-localised fields — only the lookup mechanism differs. **New `Infrastructure\Goals\GoalsRepository`.** Two read methods: `listForPlayer( int $player_id )` returns the player's active goals newest-first; `findForPlayer( int $goal_id, int $player_id )` returns a single goal scoped to that player (or null — replaces the inline SQL that let URL-tweakers drill into other players' goals via a stale id with no scope guard beyond the join column). Both methods filter by `CurrentClub::id()` so a future multi-tenant install can't leak goals across academies. Both run rows through a private `hydrate()` helper that adds `status_localised` + `priority_localised` while keeping the raw fields for back-compat (KPI groupings + filter dropdowns key off the canonical codes). **`FrontendMyGoalsView` refactor.** Both render paths (list at `?tt_view=my-goals` and detail at `?tt_view=my-goals&id=N`) route through the repository. Inline `wpdb->get_results` + `LabelTranslator::goalStatus($g->status)` calls in the loop are gone; the view echoes `$g->status_localised` directly. **REST controller** `GoalsRestController::format_row` adds `status_localised` + `priority_localised` keys alongside the existing `status` / `priority` raw codes (mirrors the EvaluationsRestController shape from #1081). Existing consumers that key off raw codes are unaffected; new consumers get the right string without re-implementing the LabelTranslator switch. **What this is NOT.** Not a sweep of every Goals callsite — same module-by-module pattern as #1081, which only refactored `FrontendMyEvaluationsView` + the REST controller. Other Goals consumers (FrontendGoalsManageView, FrontendPlayerDetailView's goals tab, CoachForms, exporters, KPI sources) continue to use `LabelTranslator` directly until each is touched for its own reason. Per the parent #806's plan, the CI lint allow-list tightens for Goals once the rest of those callsites land. **Refs remaining slices.** #1078 (Activities), #1079 (Players), #1080 (Pdp). Patch bump within v4.20 series. (closes #1077) =

= 4.20.17 — Academy admin can view + complete workflow tasks assigned to others (closes #1152). Pilot 2026-06-03 ask: when a coach is ill or unresponsive and a workflow task they own is blocking the rest of the chain, the academy admin needs a way to step in and complete the task on their behalf. **Three layers cooperated to block this:** academy_admin's matrix held `workflow_tasks` + `task_completion` at `self` scope (admin sees + acts only on their own); no cap was bridged from `task_completion:create` so per-cap checks had nothing to test; [FrontendTaskDetailView.php:84](src/Modules/Workflow/Frontend/FrontendTaskDetailView.php#L84) hard-gated submission on `$is_assignee` so non-assignee POSTs were silently dropped. **Matrix change.** `academy_admin` now holds `workflow_tasks => [r, global]` + `task_completion => [rc, global]` in [config/authorization_seed.php:657-660](config/authorization_seed.php#L657-L660). Other personas (HC, AC, parent, scout, observer, etc.) stay `self` — the takeover affordance is admin-only. **Backfill migration 0147** (`0147_academy_admin_workflow_global_scope.php`) runs the same conservative pattern as 0136: only flips `is_default = 1` rows so operator-customised overrides via the Authorization admin keep their scope; idempotent re-run safe. Flushes the matrix cache after the change so admin sessions in flight pick up the new shape without a forced refresh. **Detail view relaxation.** Replaced the `$is_assignee` gate with a `$can_submit = $is_assignee || $can_takeover` derived from `MatrixGate::can( $user_id, 'task_completion', 'create', MatrixGate::SCOPE_GLOBAL )`. Going through `MatrixGate` rather than a `LegacyCapMapper` bridge because the legacy bridge resolves via `canAnyScope` — that would let a coach with `task_completion [rc, self]` through too, defeating the takeover gate. When the viewer holds takeover, an amber "Completing on behalf of [Name] — this action will be recorded in the audit log" banner replaces the normal "view-only" notice, and the submit button label switches to "Complete on behalf" so the operator is visually aware they're acting as a stand-in. **Audit log entry** `workflow.task.completed_on_behalf` carries `task_id`, `template_key`, `assignee_user_id`, `completed_by_user_id` so the takeover trail is queryable post-hoc. Only fires when completer ≠ assignee. **Backward compatibility.** Existing assignee-only flows render identically; non-assignee non-admin viewers still see the read-only view-only banner. **Dutch translation** added for the two new strings. **Out of scope.** Per-task reassignment (admin changes the assignee instead of completing); HoD takeover; bulk completion from the dashboard kanban. Single-task admin takeover unblocks the immediate operational case. Patch bump. (closes #1152) =

= 4.20.16 — Activity Principles picker: bucket sections collapsed by default, auto-open only when a selection is inside (closes #1155). Pilot 2026-06-03 ask after #1122 shipped: every bucket rendering `<details open>` forced operators to scroll past 18 principles for every new activity, even when they only wanted one. **Fix.** Both surfaces (new-activity wizard's [PrinciplesStep::render()](src/Modules/Wizards/Activity/PrinciplesStep.php#L66-L107) AND the activity edit form at [FrontendActivitiesManageView.php:1437](src/Shared/Frontend/FrontendActivitiesManageView.php#L1437)) now compute `$bucket_has_selection` per bucket and set `<details>` `open` only when at least one principle inside is already in the `$selected` / `$linked_ids` array. Default (no selection in bucket) renders collapsed, so operators scan bucket headers ("Aanvallen", "Verdedigen", "Omschakelen", etc.), pick the right bucket, expand, and tick. Edit case: every bucket that contains a currently-linked principle opens automatically so the operator sees existing selections without hunting. "Other principles" fallback bucket stays collapsed-by-default as it was. Summary tap target stays ≥ 44px per CLAUDE.md §2 (no CSS changes). Patch bump. (closes #1155) =

= 4.20.15 — Activity ↔ principle link table: missing rename migration shipped + `PrincipleLinksRepository` write failures now log loudly (closes #1153). Pilot 2026-06-03 reported that ticking principles on the new-activity wizard's #1122 picker appeared to save but produced an empty pre-fill on the activity edit form. **Root cause.** Migration 0015 created the pivot as `tt_session_principles` with a `session_id` column. Migration 0027 (sessions → activities rename) renamed `tt_sessions`, `tt_attendance.session_id`, the caps, and the workflow triggers — but **did not rename the link table** to its activities counterpart. Yet every consumer (the new-activity wizard's PrinciplesStep, the wp-admin Activities form, the REST controller's `persistPrincipleLinks`, the frontend edit form's pre-fill, the planner's #1124 principle pills, the activity detail's #1037 linked-principles section, [PrincipleLinksRepository::sessionPivot()](src/Modules/Methodology/Repositories/PrincipleLinksRepository.php#L28-L31)) targets `tt_activity_principles` with an `activity_id` column. Result: every write returned `false` (silently swallowed by the repository); every read returned an empty array (table-not-found). Symptom-equivalent silent failure to #1054 and #1137. **Migration 0146** runs the missing rename: `RENAME TABLE tt_session_principles → tt_activity_principles`, then `ALTER TABLE CHANGE session_id activity_id`, then index renames (`uniq_session_principle → uniq_activity_principle`, `idx_session → idx_activity`). Idempotent + conservative — each step gates on current state; a fresh install lacking both names recreates the table at the new name via `dbDelta`. **Repository hardening.** `setActivityPrinciples()` now logs `principle_links.delete.failed` + `principle_links.insert.failed` with `$wpdb->last_error` + the offending ids when either call returns `false`. Future regressions surface in the error log instead of going silent. **What this resolves downstream.** #1037 (activity detail not rendering linked principles) and #1124 (planner principle pills) are both consumers of the same broken pivot; they begin working as soon as the table rename completes. **What it does NOT resolve.** Selections that operators made BEFORE this migration shipped were never persisted — those clicks have no recoverable state. Operators need to re-tag previously-created activities going forward. Patch bump. (closes #1153) =

= 4.20.14 — Persona dashboard: `TodayUpNextHeroWidget` hides the Evaluation CTA from users without `tt_edit_evaluations` (closes #1151). Pilot 2026-06-03: an Assistent-trainer (AC) saw an "Evaluation" button on their dashboard hero — but AC lost the `evaluations` matrix entity in #1060, so `tt_edit_evaluations` returns false and clicking the link drops them on a surface they can't author into. **Root cause.** [TodayUpNextHeroWidget::render()](src/Modules/PersonaDashboard/Widgets/TodayUpNextHeroWidget.php#L46-L71) renders an explicit `<a>Evaluation</a>` CTA unconditionally — no `capRequired()` override (the legacy widget pre-dates the cap-gating chain). The newer `mark_attendance_hero` IS cap-gated on `tt_edit_evaluations` so AC doesn't see that widget; but `today_up_next_hero` stays registered for back-compat with custom templates and inherits the legacy unconditional CTA. **Fix.** Inline `current_user_can( 'tt_edit_evaluations' )` check wrapping the Evaluation `<a>`; Attendance stays unconditional (every persona in `intendedPersonas()` — HC, AC, team_manager — holds `tt_view_activities`). The widget itself stays registered (no `capRequired()` change) so the intended HC + TM use cases keep rendering both buttons. Defence-in-depth pattern alongside #1060 + #1105 + #1106. **What this is NOT.** Not a `capRequired()` change on the widget — that would gate out AC + team_manager entirely, who legitimately see the Attendance CTA. Not a `mark_attendance_hero` change — that widget is already cap-gated correctly. Patch bump. (closes #1151) =

= 4.20.13 — Activity edit form: Status select min-width sized for ≥15 characters (closes #1150). Pilot 2026-06-03 reported the Status `<select>` ellipsizing labels like "In uitvoering" / "Geannuleerd" because the field sits in a `.tt-grid-2` row next to Type and only got 50% of the form width at desktop. **Fix.** One CSS rule appended to `assets/css/frontend-activities-manage.css`: `.tt-dashboard #tt-activity-status { min-width: 18ch; }` — covers 15+ visible characters plus the chevron, the grid auto-rebalances so Type's column gives back the spare space, and mobile (≤ 480px) collapses to 1 column already so this is a no-op on phone viewports. Patch bump. (closes #1150) =

= 4.20.12 — Print doelenintake: scope-mismatch fix on the player + team batch print routers (closes #1149). Pilot 2026-06-03 clicked "Print doelenintake" on a player profile that renders fine, hit a hard `wp_die( 'Player not found.' )` on the print URL. **Root cause.** [PlayerGoalIntakePrintRouter::emit](src/Modules/Goals/Print/PlayerGoalIntakePrintRouter.php#L161-L179) filtered the player lookup by `pl.club_id = CurrentClub::id()` (always `1` today), while the player profile view at [FrontendPlayersManageView::loadPlayer](src/Shared/Frontend/FrontendPlayersManageView.php#L631-L640) does NOT filter on club_id — only demo-scope. So when a player row carried `club_id != 1` (legacy data, demo seed, partial 0038 backfill), the page rendered fine, the "Print doelenintake" link captured the player id, and the click 404'd. Same scope-strictness family as #1054 (silent `$wpdb->update`) and #1137 (archive REST). **Fix.** Two queries change: per-player `emit()` and the team-batch `renderTeamBatch()`. Both drop the `pl.club_id = %d` / `t.club_id = %d` filter, switch to `QueryHelpers::apply_demo_scope` (the same helper the linking surface uses), and derive `$club_id` from the player's own row to drive the downstream `lastSeasonStats()` + `lookbackForPlayer()` sub-queries. Net effect: the print router stops being a stricter gate than the page that linked here; demo-mode isolation is preserved (a demo user still sees only demo rows). **What this is NOT.** Not a `tt_players.club_id` data backfill — that's a separate hygiene task. Not a change to MatchPrepPrintRouter, which has the identical shape (file follow-up if pilot surfaces it). Patch bump. (closes #1149) =

= 4.20.11 — Scout: onboarding-pipeline reclassified out of `desktop_only` (closes #918). Scouts hit the pipeline kanban 5-15× per week, often from the pitch on a phone, per `docs/scout-actions.md` action #2. The previous classification at [src/Shared/CoreSurfaceRegistration.php:106](src/Shared/CoreSurfaceRegistration.php#L106) redirected mobile visitors to a "use desktop" prompt — friction the daily scout workflow couldn't bear. **Fix.** Removed `'onboarding-pipeline'` from the `$desktop_only` list in `CoreSurfaceRegistration::registerMobileClasses()`. The slug falls through to `MobileSurfaceRegistry`'s `viewable` default — kanban columns scroll horizontally on narrow viewports (< 480px), per-card density renders as-is. No view-code changes; the +New prospect CTA already lives on the scout hero per #0081 so the pipeline view isn't the mobile entry point. **What this is NOT.** Not a full mobile-first rewrite. Bumping the surface to `native` requires a 360px audit of `FrontendOnboardingPipelineView` + the per-card layout; that ships separately if the pilot asks for it. For now: scouts can glance at counts and tap into cards without a device switch. Patch bump. (closes #918) =

= 4.20.10 — Activity form: attendance picker scoped to the activity's team roster only (closes #1154). Upstream UX cleanup to the data-integrity fix from #1148 (v4.20.5). `FrontendActivitiesManageView::renderForm` previously pre-loaded **every player from every team the coach has access to**, with a JS helper hiding off-team rows visually. The hidden form fields still submitted, so for admin users the entire academy shipped in the POST payload. #1148 closed the data-integrity gap at the REST layer (silent off-roster filter); this PR closes the upstream source so off-roster ids never get sent in the first place. **Fix.** `$all_players` now contains only the activity's current team roster (`QueryHelpers::get_players( $selected_team )`). The "preserve team-dropdown state across changes" optimisation that originally justified the multi-team pool is gone — coaches typically pick the team first, then mark attendance; save-and-reload handles the niche team-switch case. **Legacy attendance preserved.** Any player who already has an attendance row on this activity but isn't on the current team's roster is unioned into the picker — they may legitimately have historical squad attendance (the audit-trail-aware case #1148's migration 0145 preserved), so the form must still be able to edit / unmark those rows. Read via a single SQL fetch by id list against `tt_players`. **Team-dropdown switch edge case** (admin changes the team `<select>` after the form is loaded): the picker still shows the OLD team's roster until the activity is saved + reloaded. Documented as the niche case per the #1154 issue body; coaches don't typically need this flow. **Defence in depth alongside #1148.** Even if the form's hidden inputs somehow still ship off-roster ids (e.g. a future regression), the REST `write_attendance` filter from v4.20.5 silently drops them. This PR removes the source; v4.20.5 is the safety net. **What this is NOT.** Not a permission change. Not a write-time behaviour change (REST layer unchanged from v4.20.5). Just the form payload narrowing to what should always have been sent. Patch bump. (closes #1154) =


= 4.20.9 — Authorization matrix admin: suppress spurious "Nog geen tegel of admin-pagina gebruikt deze entiteit" notice on 10 legitimately admin-only entities (closes #1159). Pilot reported that the Authorization Matrix admin page rendered the orphan-entity warning on a large number of rows — 10+ entities — even though every flagged entity is correctly wired (just to admin / configuration surfaces rather than frontend tiles). The notice was supposed to flag genuinely orphan entities (seeded in the matrix but never wired to any UI surface), but the detection logic produced false negatives for admin-only surfaces that lack a clean cap→entity mapping. **Root cause.** `MatrixEntityCatalog::consumersOf()` walks three registries (`TileRegistry` + `AdminMenuRegistry` + `AdminMenuRegistry::allDashboardTiles()`) looking for entries whose `cap` maps (via `LegacyCapMapper::capsForEntity()`) to the entity. Entities like `authorization_changelog`, `impersonation_log`, `permission_debug`, `lookups`, `branding`, `feature_toggles`, `custom_field_values`, `bulk_import`, `license`, `module_state` all live behind WordPress admin surfaces (configuration sub-tabs, audit/debug pages, licence + module-state screens) without declaring `entity` on a frontend tile or carrying a clean cap mapping through the three walked registries. Detection returned empty for each, MatrixPage rendered the warning, the operator saw a wall of "this entity is orphan" notices on entities that are actually fine. **Fix.** New `ADMIN_ONLY_ENTITIES` const list in `MatrixEntityCatalog` enumerating the 10 entities that legitimately live in admin surfaces. New private `adminOnlyDescriptor( $entity )` returns a synthetic consumer descriptor `{ type: 'admin_only', label: 'Admin / configuration surface' }` when the entity is whitelisted; returns empty array when not (preserving the genuine "no consumers" signal for true orphans). `consumersOf()` falls through to `adminOnlyDescriptor()` in two branches: when `capsForEntity()` returns empty (no cap mapping at all) AND after the dedupe pass when the walk found nothing. `MatrixPage::renderConsumerChip()` extended with the new `'admin_only'` type → "admin / configuration surface" label. **Operator UX.** The 10 whitelisted entities now show a single "Admin / configuration surface" chip in the consumer column instead of the red orphan warning. The chip's popover surfaces the entity name for traceability. **Adding entities to the whitelist** is a deliberate declaration: "this entity is intentionally only consumed by admin surfaces, not by the frontend tile registry." Frontend-tile-bearing entities should NOT be added — they should declare their entity on the tile. **What this is NOT.** Not a permission change — the matrix still gates these entities exactly as before via caps. Not a data change. Just a discovery-side false-positive fix in the admin tool. Patch bump. (closes #1159) =


= 4.20.8 — i18n: fill three missing Dutch translations on wizard surfaces (closes #1158). Pilot reported three wizard strings rendering in English on a Dutch (nl_NL) install despite all three being correctly wrapped in translation functions in PHP. **Root cause.** Strings were correctly extractable; msgstr in `languages/talenttrack-nl_NL.po` was empty for each. Standard translation-backfill gap — strings added since the last translation round. **Strings filled.** (1) `FrontendWizardView.php:756` — "You are here" → "Je bent hier" (sidebar progress-indicator marker for the current step). (2) `TypeStatusStep.php:54` — "Status defaults to \"Planned\". Flip to \"Completed\" once the activity has happened — that's when the attendance editor unlocks on the activity page." → "Status staat standaard op \"Gepland\". Zet op \"Voltooid\" zodra de activiteit heeft plaatsgevonden — dan ontgrendelt de aanwezigheidsregistratie op de activiteitspagina." (new-activity wizard Type step body). = 4.20.7 — PlayerSearchPicker: dispatch synthetic `change` event after JS-driven value assignment (closes #1157). Pilot reported that on any wizard step using `PlayerSearchPickerComponent` (notably the new-goal wizard before the v4.20.6 cascade-dropdown rewrite, but the bug affected any future surface too), the Next button stayed disabled after selecting a player — coach had to click outside the picker before Next became active, or in many cases Next never enabled at all. **Root cause.** `player-search-picker.js:setSelection()` writes the player's id to the hidden input via direct `valueEl.value = String( id )` assignment. The wizard chrome's `wizard-validation.js` listens for `change` / `blur` / `input` events on `[required]` fields to refresh the Next-button `disabled` state. JS-driven `.value =` assignments **don't** fire those events; the validation listener never re-evaluated and Next stayed disabled even though `player_id` was now non-empty. **Fix.** `setSelection()` now dispatches a bubbling `change` event immediately after the value assignment. `wizard-validation.js` (and any future form-level listener) sees the synthetic event, re-runs its `requiredInputs().some( isEmpty )` check, and updates the Next-button state correctly. Legacy fallback path uses `createEvent` + `initEvent` for older browsers without the `Event` constructor; the modern path uses `new Event( 'change', { bubbles: true } )` per WHATWG. **Defence in depth.** Even after #1156 replaced the goal-wizard's autocomplete with cascade dropdowns, this fix matters for every OTHER surface using `PlayerSearchPickerComponent` (player list search, new-evaluation wizard, any future picker consumer). The fix is on the shared component, not the goal-wizard caller. Patch bump. (closes #1157) =


= 4.20.6 — New-goal wizard: team→player cascade dropdowns replace the autocomplete picker (closes #1156). Pilot UX feedback: the autocomplete `PlayerSearchPickerComponent` forced typing when scanning + tapping was faster. Coaches already know which team the goal is for — the picker should reflect that mental model. **Fix.** `PlayerStep` now renders two stacked `<select>` elements — a team filter dropdown above the player dropdown. The player dropdown groups its options by `<optgroup label="…">` per team (one optgroup per team the coach can access). A new `wizard-cascade-picker.js` helper (enqueued via `wp_enqueue_script` per CLAUDE.md §2 — no inline scripts) listens for changes on any `[data-tt-cascade-filter]` element and hides optgroups whose `data-tt-team-id` doesn't match the filter's value. Filter value 0 ("Pick a team") shows all optgroups. When the currently-selected option ends up inside a hidden group, the target select resets to 0 and dispatches a synthetic `change` event so `wizard-validation.js` re-checks the Next button state. **Scoping unchanged.** Head-coach / assistant-coach see only their assigned teams via `QueryHelpers::get_teams_for_coach( $user_id )`; admin / HoD see the full club via `QueryHelpers::get_teams()`. Empty team-assignment renders a friendly notice instead of an empty form, with a hidden `player_id = 0 required` input so the wizard's required-field check still recognises the missing selection. **Edit-mode rehydration.** When the wizard state carries a pre-selected `player_id`, the step derives the player's `team_id` server-side and lands the team filter on the right group so the operator picks up where they left off. **Reusable helper.** The new `wizard-cascade-picker.js` is generic — it wires any `[data-tt-cascade-filter]`-tagged select to any `[data-tt-cascade-target=ID]`-pointed select. Future wizard steps with the same shape (e.g. team→activity, parent→child cascades) can reuse it without ceremony. **Out of scope.** The autocomplete `PlayerSearchPickerComponent` stays in place for the OTHER surfaces that use it (player list search, etc.) — only the goal-wizard step changes. The Next-button activation bug on the autocomplete (separately tracked as #1157) is unaffected here; that ships as its own fix. Patch bump. (closes #1156) =


= 4.20.5 — Attendance: REST write-time roster filter + display JOIN on player's team + delete-backfill migration (closes #1148). Pilot diagnostic confirmed that off-roster `is_guest = 0` rows existed for the player attendance report (Hedel JO14-1 showed 30 players, 14 of which were currently on JO13-1, none had any `team_changed` journey events). Root cause: the activity edit form's attendance picker at `FrontendActivitiesManageView::renderForm` pre-loads every player from every team the coach has access to ("so changing the team dropdown later doesn't lose attendance state"). The JS helper hides off-team rows visually, but the hidden form fields still submit. For admin users that means the entire academy ships in the POST. `ActivitiesRestController::write_attendance` accepted any submitted player_id and wrote `is_guest = 0` with no roster validation. **Piece 1 — REST write-time chokepoint.** `write_attendance` now looks up the activity's `team_id` once, then for each submitted player_id checks the player's current `team_id`. Off-roster ids are silently dropped (with a `session.attendance.dropped_off_roster` warning log carrying activity_id + activity_team_id + the dropped ids + their current team_ids so operators can triage UI / import bugs from logs). Activities with `team_id = 0` (club-wide / legacy) accept any player by design. The explicit guest path (`POST /sessions/{id}/guests` → `is_guest = 1`) remains the only way to record off-roster attendance. **Piece 2 — Display JOIN fix.** `FrontendAttendancePlayerReportView::query()` LEFT JOIN target changes from `t.id = a.team_id` (activity's team) to `t.id = p.team_id` (player's team). Future legitimate mid-season transfers — caught by the audit trail — render with the player's current team in the report, so the operator can scan for roster movement at a glance. **Piece 3 — Migration 0145 (DELETE-not-flip).** Walks every `is_guest = 0` row where `player.team_id != activity.team_id`. For each candidate, checks `tt_player_events` for a `team_changed` event putting the player on the activity's team at or before the activity's `session_date`. If the audit trail justifies the row (player was on the activity's team at the time), the row is preserved as legitimate historical squad attendance. Otherwise the row is DELETED — these are write-path artefacts, not legitimate guest attendance, and reclassifying them as `is_guest = 1` would invent a "guest history" that didn't happen. Two-pass design: pass 1 logs every row to-be-deleted to `tt_logs` with sample ids (full reconstruction available); pass 2 runs the DELETE in 500-row chunks. Idempotent. Conservative — only touches non-guest rows on team-scoped activities. **For the pilot data:** JO14-1 attendance report drops from 30 rows → 16 (the real squad). The 14 JO13-1 artefacts vanish entirely. The JO13-1 report is unaffected — those rows were on JO14-1 activities, never on JO13's. **Out of scope.** The upstream activity edit form's multi-team player pool (#1154) ships as a separate UX-cleanup issue — the REST chokepoint in this PR closes the data integrity gap regardless of whether the form fix lands. The `FrontendAttendanceTeamReportView` doesn't expose the per-row team-display issue (it aggregates per team, not per player). Patch bump. (closes #1148) =


= 4.20.4 — Analytics standard reports: AC team-scope leak fix on the two attendance reports (closes #1147). Pilot reported that an AC opening the Player attendance statistics analysis at `?tt_view=attendance-report-player` could see every team in the dropdown + the data ran club-wide by default. AC's matrix scope on teams/activities is `team` (operational, scoped to teams they coach) per #1060 / #1106 — not `global`. **Root cause:** the two analytics direct-`$wpdb` renderers bypass the analytics framework's KPI scope plumbing (`KpiRegistry` + `FactQuery` + per-KPI `context: COACH | ACADEMY | PLAYER_PARENT`). They read `$_GET['team_id']` and ran club-wide queries with no coach-team filter. `tt_view_analytics` is a surface gate, not a club-wide data grant. **Fix.** Both `FrontendAttendancePlayerReportView` + `FrontendAttendanceTeamReportView` now route through `QueryHelpers::get_teams_for_coach( $user_id )` — the same resolver the players list + teamplanner use (post-#1124). Admins + holders of `tt_view_all_teams` keep the club-wide view; everyone else only ever sees teams they coach. Both the team dropdown AND the data query enforce the scope. A coach with zero team assignments lands on a friendly empty-state notice instead of an empty club-wide table. A user URL-tampering with `team_id=X` for a team they're not assigned to falls through to an empty result (no row leak). **Out of scope.** The season-summary KPIs in `FrontendStandardReportsView` are explicitly framed as "Academy-wide signals over the last 12 months" and would need a different decision (per-team breakdown vs. global headline). Separate follow-up if AC's season-summary view needs trimming. Also out of scope: the per-row "Team" column display fix (player's team vs. activity's team) — that's #1148's territory and ships separately. Player-centric framing: AC's analytics now answer "what's the attendance picture for the players I coach?" correctly, per CLAUDE.md §1 privacy + dignity ("no player data leaks across … unauthorized roles"). Patch bump. (closes #1147) =


= 4.20.3 — Player list: remove inline "Rapport" row action (closes #1145). Pilot reported that the AC saw a "Rapport" inline button on every row of the player list at `?tt_view=players`, clicking it landed on `?tt_view=players&player_id=N` — the legacy rate-card view with the player card + rating visible. The clickable player-name cell is already the canonical view affordance per the surrounding comment from v3.110.53 — the rate-card row action was duplicate navigation pointing at a v3.0.0-era deep link, and removing it both eliminates the duplication AND closes the AC scope leak entry-point. = 4.20.2 — Scouting visits: scout matrix gate fix — tile-declared entity aligned to `prospects` (closes #1143). Pilot reported that scouts hit "Niet geautoriseerd" on `?tt_view=scouting-visits` despite the Permission Chain Debug page (#777) showing `tt_view_prospects` + `tt_edit_prospects` both resolving to `✓ allowed` via `userCanOrMatrix()`. **Root cause:** the denial wasn't from the view's own gate — it was from `DashboardShortcode::matrixDispatchAllows()` one layer up. That helper calls `TileRegistry::entityForViewSlug('scouting-visits')`, which returned `'scouting_visits'` per the tile registration at `CoreSurfaceRegistration.php:625`. But `scouting_visits` is a phantom entity — zero seed rows for any persona in `config/authorization_seed.php`, zero `LegacyCapMapper` entries. So `MatrixGate::canAnyScope($user_id, 'scouting_visits', 'read')` returned false for every non-admin user, and dispatch denied before the view's broader `tt_view_prospects` OR `tt_edit_prospects` gate could pass. The Permission Chain Debug page couldn't surface the cause because it iterates legacy caps; `scouting_visits` is unreachable through that lens. **Fix:** tile's `entity` declaration changes from `scouting_visits` to `prospects`. The tile already declared `cap => tt_view_prospects`; the view's own gate already checks the same caps; scout/HoD/admin all have `prospects.read` globally via the matrix seed. The matrix-dispatch gate now queries `(prospects, read)` and passes through. Single-line change in `CoreSurfaceRegistration.php`. Inline comment documents the rationale next to the changed line so future tile edits don't reflex-reintroduce the phantom-entity pattern. **What's NOT in this PR.** Three previous "scout-prospects auth" fixes (v3.110.147 / .168 / .181) all patched the view's own gate — the wrong layer. They stay in the code untouched; they're still useful when an entity legitimately has both caps wired but a persona-resolution edge case surfaces only one. The architectural lesson — tiles declaring entities that don't exist in the matrix cause silent dispatch denials with no diagnostic page coverage — is worth a follow-up: a boot-time check that walks every tile-declared entity against the matrix-known-entities set and warns when an orphan is registered. Logged as future work, not in scope for this fix. **The `scouting-visit` (singular) slug stays.** It's registered for slug-ownership only (no tile, so `entityForViewSlug()` returns null and the matrix-dispatch gate bypasses on the null check). Detail page already works. Patch bump. (closes #1143) =


= 4.20.1 — Persona-dashboard editor: swap-on-hover for already-placed cards, horizontal gap-fill compact pass, and touch-input fallback via Pointer Events (closes #1142). Pilot 2026-06-03 ask: the editor's drag-drop technically worked but produced fragmented layouts (gaps in rows the operator couldn't recover from), didn't work at all on tablets (HTML5 `draggable` doesn't fire on iOS/Android), and offered no way to swap two cards' positions — every drag pushed colliders down, leaving more gaps. **Swap-on-hover.** Dragging an already-placed canvas card over another card on the grid now lights the target green (`.is-swap-target`) and, on drop, swaps the two slots' (x, y) instead of running the push-down/collision-resolve path. Detected in the existing `dragover` band handler by reading the closest `.tt-pde-card[data-tt-pde-slot]` ancestor of the cursor target; the drop branches in `handleDropOnBand` via a new `swapSlots(srcId, dstId)` helper that resolves any size-mismatch overlap via the existing `resolveCollisions` + `compactGrid` pair. Empty-cell drops keep the push-down/compact behaviour unchanged. **Horizontal gap-fill.** New `packHorizontally(grid)` runs as the final step of `compactGrid` after its vertical pull-up pass. Walks each row top-to-bottom; for each slot, scans every (nx, ny) where the slot would fit without colliding with a preceding slot, and relocates if the candidate is strictly earlier in (y, x) order. Bounded by `grid.length` iterations; converges in 1-3 passes on real layouts. The pilot's fragmented Assistent-trainer dashboard (row 2 KPI card + trailing gap, smaller widget bumped to row 3) now self-tidies after any drop: the row-3 widget gets pulled up into the row-2 gap, no manual recovery needed. **Touch fallback.** New `wireTouchDragFallback()` binds Pointer Events on the canvas root: `pointerdown` (touch / pen only — mouse keeps the native HTML5 DnD) captures the underlying canvas card, sets `__ttPdeDrag = { kind: 'move', slotId }`, spawns a floating ghost via `cloneNode`, and pins it to fixed coordinates that track the finger. `pointermove` runs the same `gridCellFromEvent` + `snapToGuides` + swap-target detection + `previewDragLayout` chain the desktop path uses. `pointerup` synthesises an `{ clientX, clientY, shiftKey }` event-like and feeds it to `handleDropOnBand('grid', synthetic)` so the existing drop logic + swap branch fire unchanged. `pointercancel` / `lostpointercapture` tear down the ghost and clear all visuals. **CSS additions.** `.tt-pde-card.is-swap-target` lights up green with a 3px inset border + 4px halo + light-green fill. `.tt-pde-card[data-tt-pde-band="grid"]` sets `touch-action: none` so the canvas doesn't scroll-jack the pointer-down. `.tt-pde-card.tt-pde-touch-ghost` adds a heavier drop shadow + accent outline + `pointer-events: none` so `document.elementFromPoint` sees the underlying band, not the ghost. **i18n.** New `swapped: "Swapped."` string in the editor bootstrap (Dutch: "Gewisseld."), surfaced by the `setStatus` call after a swap commit. **Keyboard a11y unchanged.** Space-to-grab + arrows + escape still drive `moveSlotByKey` → `resolveCollisions` + `compactGrid` (which now includes the horizontal pack). **Mouse a11y unchanged.** Desktop with a fine pointer keeps the native HTML5 DnD primary; the touch path's `pointerdown` early-returns on `pointerType === 'mouse'`. **Out of scope.** Live-dashboard reorder for the published surface (per-user override layer is a separate feature). Multi-select drag and resize-by-edge-drag remain out of scope. Patch bump within v4.20 series. (closes #1142) =

= 4.20.0 — People — permanent-delete cascade across 9 reference tables + informed-consent impact-preview dialog (closes #1138). Pilot 2026-06-03 ask: every person must be deletable without leaving orphan rows that pollute roster surfaces, scope grants, staff-dev tracking, mentorships, invitations, and player parent-contact links. **Cascade service.** New `Infrastructure\People\PersonDeletionCascade` runs everything in a single transaction. CASCADE-delete classes (the row exists only because the person exists): `tt_team_people`, `tt_user_role_scopes` (rows where `person_id = X`), `tt_staff_development`, `tt_staff_certifications`, `tt_staff_evaluations`, `tt_staff_goals`, `tt_staff_mentorships` (mentor OR mentee = X), `tt_invitations` (pending/expired targets). SET-NULL classes (parent row survives, reference cleared): `tt_user_role_scopes.granted_by_person_id`, `tt_invitations.target_person_id` for accepted invitations, `tt_players.parent_person_id`. No block rules — per the pilot ask, every person is deletable; rows that would orphan get nulled so the parent record renders cleanly as "no person assigned". Any per-table failure rolls the entire batch back. **WP user stays.** The `wp_users` table is NOT touched; the audit-log + impersonation-log + evaluations + goals + activities that reference `wp_users.ID` via `created_by` / `coach_id` etc. are unaffected. The operator deletes the WP account separately via WP's Users admin if desired (same separation precedent as migration 0139). **Audit-log entry** `person.deleted_with_cascade` carries `person_ids`, `club_id`, `deleted` count, per-table counts, nulled counts, and `by_user` so post-hoc verification has full context. **REST preview endpoint** `POST /wp-json/talenttrack/v1/people/delete-preview` accepts `{ ids: [N, N, N] }` and returns a per-person impact summary — read-only, no writes, cap-gated on `tt_edit_settings`. Response shape includes human-readable team names + role labels + player names so the dialog renders strings, not raw ids. Capped at 100 ids per call. **wp-admin dialog.** `assets/js/admin-people-delete-preview.js` + `assets/css/admin-people-delete-preview.css` intercept the bulk-action form submit when the chosen action is `delete_permanent` on the People list, fetch the preview, and open a structured `<dialog>` showing per-person CASCADE + SET-NULL impact. Two-step type-DELETE confirm triggers for batches ≥ 3 persons OR any person with ≥ 5 affected references; trivial deletes (1 person with ≤ 2 refs) skip the type-DELETE step so the everyday case isn't tedious. Mobile-first per CLAUDE.md §2 — width clamps to 96vw at ≤ 480px, footer buttons stack full-width, body scrolls when impact list is long. **WP user-account note** rendered inside the dialog body so the operator understands what is and isn't being deleted. **No schema migration** — the cascade reads existing columns; all involved tables already exist (since 0006, 0025, 0048, 0050, 0062). **Patch route stays.** The frontend `DELETE /people/{id}` REST stays as a soft-archive (no destructive cascade triggered from REST) — only the wp-admin "Delete permanently" bulk action runs `PersonDeletionCascade`. **Cap gating.** Hard-delete still requires `tt_edit_settings` at the bulk-action handler; the preview endpoint and dialog enqueue carry the same cap. **Out of scope.** Cascade for other entity types (Players, Teams, Activities, Evaluations, Goals) each have their own reference graphs and ship separately when the People pattern is validated. WP user deletion remains a manual step in WP Users admin. Minor bump — first feature in the v4.20 series. (closes #1138) =

= 4.19.12 — People REST: `archive_person()` no longer silently fails when no row matches (closes #1137). Pilot reported that clicking Archive on a person detail returned to the list with the success toast — but the person remained on the list, unchanged. **Root cause:** `PeopleRestController::archive_person()` issued `$wpdb->update()` and only treated `$ok === false` as failure. `$wpdb->update()` returns `0` (not `false`) when the WHERE clause matches no rows — for example when the person's `club_id` doesn't match the current operator's club, or when the row is already archived by another tab. The handler treated that zero as success, returned 200, and the `frontend-archive-button.js` redirected to the list as designed. The row was never touched. **Fix:** a new `$ok === 0` branch in `archive_person()` returns 404 `not_found` with a Dutch-translated "Person not found in your club." message, and logs `rest.person.archive.no_row` with the `id` + `club_id` context so the same surface can be triaged from logs without the operator describing the steps. The existing `$ok === false` branch keeps returning 500 `db_error` for genuine SQL failures (e.g. lock timeout, constraint violation) so the two error classes don't collapse into one bucket. **Frontend behaviour.** The archive button JS already routes any non-2xx response into its error path — the user now sees a clear "Person not found in your club" notice instead of a silent redirect, and the page stays on the detail view so they can take a screenshot or report the cross-club mismatch. No JS change needed. **Out of scope.** A site-admin override that could archive a person regardless of club scope (today: archive is club-scoped by design); a Restore affordance for archived people (issue body Suspect D — separate UX, not a regression). Patch bump. (closes #1137) =


= 4.19.11 — Persona dashboard: child-switcher pills navigate to the child's player record (closes #915). `ChildSwitcherWithRecapWidget` rendered each child as a `<button data-tt-pd-child="N">` with no JS handler bound — multi-child parents could see the pills but couldn't click through to a non-primary child. The data attribute stays for selector-based instrumentation (e.g. analytics, future state-restoration). **CSS updated** to add `text-decoration: none` (pills are anchors now), `display: inline-flex` + `align-items: center` so vertical centring works on `<a>`, and a `:hover` / `:focus-visible` state with a soft white outline so keyboard users get a clear focus ring against the parent-hero gradient. 48px tap-target rule preserved. **Single-child parents.** Widget still hides the recap when no children are linked; with exactly one child, the single pill still renders + still clicks through to that child's record. **What this is NOT.** Not a dashboard-scoped child-switcher — the recap card across the bottom still aggregates across all children (which matches the widget's docblock intent). = 4.19.9 — Activities — optional start/end time fields (closes #1126). = 4.19.8 — Activity ↔ principles picker — two-level bucket picker on both wizard step + edit form (closes #1122). The activity form's principle picker shipped as a hold-Ctrl flat multiselect over all 18 principles; on touch it was unusable. Pilot 2026-06-03: pick the bucket first (Aanvallen / Verdedigen / Omschakelen × team task — the same vocabulary the methodology browser groups by), then tick the principles within. **`PrinciplesStep` (new-activity wizard) rewritten** as a stack of `<details>` sections — one per team function — with a small Dutch-cap label per team-task sub-bucket and one checkbox per principle inside. All buckets open by default. Selected rows tint the row background (`#eef4fb`) so the picker shows what's already linked at a glance. Minimum 44px row height so each checkbox is a real tap target on phones. **`FrontendActivitiesManageView::renderForm` (edit form)** ships the identical picker — same `<details>` shape, same checkbox markup, same `name="activity_principle_ids[]"` field name — so the wizard's new-activity flow and the edit-form roundtrip stay visually parallel. **No data-shape change** — the existing `tt_activity_principles` join table + the existing `PrincipleLinksRepository::setActivityPrinciples` write path are unchanged. The flat `<select multiple>` is gone from both surfaces; the REST controller still accepts the same `activity_principle_ids[]` array. **Grouping logic** walks `MethodologyEnums::teamFunctions()` for the function-level order and `MethodologyEnums::teamTasks()` for task-level order. Principles with empty `team_function_key` + `team_task_key` land in an "Other principles" closed-by-default fallback section so custom academy principles still surface. Patch bump. (closes #1122) =


= 4.19.7 — Activity ↔ principles render polish — activity detail section + planner card chip palette (closes #1123, #1125). Two pilot-triage requests from 2026-06-03 around how linked methodology principles surface back to coaches. **#1123 — activity detail "Gekoppelde spelprincipes" section.** The activity detail already rendered linked principles, but inline inside the detail `<dl>` as a comma-separated text list (`Connected principles: AO-01 · Title, VS-02 · Title`) which the pilot reported was easy to miss + not actionable. **Fix:** dedicated `<section>` with Dutch heading "Gekoppelde spelprincipes" after the detail dl. Each principle renders as a coloured pill linking to `?tt_view=methodology&mtab=principles&pid=N`. Bucket palette derived from the code's first letter (A* = aanvallen warm orange, V* = verdedigen cool green, O* = omschakelen mustard yellow) so a coach can scan the linked principles by intent without reading the labels. **#1125 — planner activity card principle chips show codes (not titles) with bucket colour.** The planner card already rendered principle chips, but using the full localised principle title — which spilled into multi-line wrap at 3 principles and gave no at-a-glance "which buckets is this session targeting" signal. **Fix:** chip shows the bare code (`AO-01` not `AO-01 · Sometitle`); slice bumped from 3 to 4 codes per card; overflow shows `+N` indicator; `data-bucket` attribute applies the same palette as #1123 above. Title moves to the chip's `title=` attribute so hover still surfaces it. CSS lives in `assets/css/components/team-planner.css` alongside the existing chip rule. Patch bump. (closes #1123, closes #1125) =


= 4.19.6 — Activity surfaces + teamplanner — three pilot-triage bugs (closes #1121, #1124, #1127). All three filed 2026-06-03 during pilot review of the teamplanner + team-detail. **#1121 — blank type column on the Aankomende-activiteiten table.** `LabelTranslator::activityType()` was a hardcoded `switch` over a stale set of legacy keys (`training`, `match`, `clinic`, `team_meeting`, `methodology`, plus the migration-0046 game subtypes). Any other key — including the seeded `meeting` (Bespreking) — hit `default: return null` and rendered as blank. **Fix:** route the key through `LookupTranslator::byTypeAndName('activity_type', $key)` first so operator-added rows render their per-locale label. Legacy switch kept as a fallback for journey-event summaries referencing archived keys; final fallback is `ucfirst(str_replace('_', ' ', $key))` so unknown keys never render blank. **#1124 — teamplanner team list leaked teams outside the user's matrix scope.** `FrontendTeamPlannerView::teamsForUser()` SELECTed every team in the club. After #1060 tightened AC scope, an AC with a kid-as-player on a sibling team saw that team in the planner even though their AC matrix had no access. **Fix:** admins + `tt_view_all_teams` holders still see all teams; everyone else is filtered through `QueryHelpers::get_teams_for_coach()` (same resolver the teams page uses), then `team_kind = ''` filter applied to drop trial / scout teams. Stable sort by name to match the admin path. **#1127 — teamplanner kept rendering cards for archived activities.** `activitiesForRange()` had `activity_status_key <> 'cancelled'` but no `archived_at IS NULL` filter. Spond-import-then-delete left cards on the planner that opened "activity no longer exists" when clicked. **Fix:** add `( archived_at IS NULL OR archived_at = '' )` to the query — same soft-delete filter every other activity surface applies. Patch bump. (closes #1121, closes #1124, closes #1127) =


= 4.19.5 — Authorization: remove `rate_cards` + `compare` from assistant_coach default seed (closes #1106). Per-entity audit follow-up to #1060 (migration 0136) + #1105 (migration 0138). Pilot triage 2026-06-01 flagged five AC matrix entries that survived the earlier trims; this PR confirms the audit verdict and ships the migration. **Verdict per entity.** `rate_cards` REMOVE — leaderboard derived from aggregated `tt_eval_ratings`; same loophole #1105 closed for `podium_panel`. `compare` REMOVE — side-by-side player comparison on rating, position, PDP and behaviour signals; every primary axis is dev data. `reports` KEEP — surface gate that upstreams per-report cap checks at the next layer; operational reports stay reachable, dev-data reports gate at their own cap. `people` KEEP — staff directory (coaches / team managers / scouts), operational not safeguarding. `vct` KEEP — Voetbal Conditionele Training session planning AC shares with HC by spec (§ VCT-2). **Seed change.** Two lines deleted from the assistant_coach block in `config/authorization_seed.php`; inline comment documents the rationale alongside `reports` so future seed edits don't reflex-reintroduce them. **Migration 0143.** Mirrors 0138's shape: DELETE the `(persona='assistant_coach', entity IN ('rate_cards','compare'), is_default=1)` rows from `tt_authorization_matrix`. Conservative — `is_default=1` only, so operator overrides via the Authorization admin (`is_default=0`) survive. Forward-only (reverting would re-introduce the leakage). Idempotent. Flushes `MatrixRepository::clearCache()` so in-flight AC sessions pick up the change on the next request. **No per-surface code changes.** Every gated surface already routes through `current_user_can()` or `MatrixGate::can()`; removing the matrix rows automatically blocks the Rate cards view + the Compare surface for AC. = 4.19.4 — Match prep print + PDF — rebuild around the on-screen view's content shape (closes #1059). = 4.19.2 — Lookup translation backfill completeness — positions + player values + fr/de/es content (closes #902). Three gaps in `tt_translations` that pilot triage 2026-05-22 surfaced on the operator-facing Lookups admin. **Gap 1 — positions.** Migrations 0086/0106/0109 called `__('GK')` on each `tt_lookups` row, but `.po` files only have msgids for the long forms ("Goalkeeper"); the gettext-equal-source guard skipped the INSERT and every position translation row stayed empty. **New migration 0141** drives the long form through gettext instead — `LabelTranslator::positionLongForm($code) → 'Centre back' → switch_to_locale → __()` then `INSERT IGNORE` into `tt_translations`. Idempotent. Runs across nl_NL / fr_FR / de_DE / es_ES. **Gap 2 — player values.** The 8 values seeded in migration 0031 (`Commitment`, `Coachability`, `Leadership`, `Resilience`, `Communication`, `Work ethic`, `Fair play`, `Ambition`) were never wrapped in `__()`, so the extractor never generated msgids, so the gettext-driven backfill found nothing to insert. **New migration 0142** ships hardcoded translations across the four shipped locales. Pragmatic fix; the architectural cleanup (wrap in `__()` for future extractor coverage) ships in the same PR via the new `LabelTranslator::playerValueLabel()` anchor — future locales pick the values up via the standard .po → migration path. **Gap 3 — fr/de/es position translator content.** 10 of 11 positions had empty msgstrs in the fr_FR / de_DE / es_ES `.po` files. Filled with standard football vocabulary (Défenseur central / Innenverteidiger / Defensa central; Milieu défensif / Defensiver Mittelfeldspieler / Mediocentro defensivo; etc.). Operators with regional preferences override per-locale via `?tt_view=configuration&config_sub=lookups`. **`LabelTranslator::positionLabel()` refactored** to delegate to the new `positionLongForm()` so the long-form switch isn't duplicated; the canonical English literals stay anchored in a sibling `positionLabelExtractorAnchors()` method so the .pot extractor still sees them. **No edits to existing migration files.** 0086/0106/0109 stay frozen on already-applied installs; new migrations are how this fixes retroactively. Patch bump within the v4.19 series. (closes #902) =

= 4.18.0 — Evaluations: touch-friendly rating input — chip grid + inline-slider rows (closes #1067). Replaces the typed-number rating input wherever a coach captures a rating. Spec / design-of-record lives at `.local-mockups/player-rating-input/` (designed in pilot session 2026-06-01). The typed-number pattern was hostile on the sideline: tap field → numeric keyboard pops → tap "7" → tap "." → tap "5" → dismiss keyboard, repeated 10–30× per player on a multi-category eval. **New component `\TT\Shared\Frontend\Components\RatingInputComponent`.** Two render methods, one component: `renderSingle( $args )` emits a chip grid — 11 chips at the default 5.0–10.0/0.5 scale arranged 4-per-row with a filler cell, half-step values visually lighter than whole numbers, one tap commits a final value, no keyboard. `renderListRow( $args )` emits a slider row — label + range slider + tabular value readout in a 78px/flex/34px grid that fits at 360px with all four canonical category names (Technical / Tactical / Physical / Mental). Both methods read `rating_min` / `rating_max` / `rating_step` from `tt_config` (default 5/10/0.5) so a club running a different scale just changes config. Schema is `DECIMAL(4,1)` — half-step values flow through unchanged. `label_hidden` option on `renderListRow` lets host markup own the label column when the slider drops into an existing table layout (e.g. HybridDeepRateStep's `<th>`/`<td>` rows). **CSS `assets/css/components/rating-input.css`.** Mobile-first. Chips ≥ 48×48 with 8px gap; slider hit area 36px tall, thumb 28×28 with 3px white halo for visibility against the accent track. `:focus-visible` outlines for keyboard, `prefers-reduced-motion` honoured. Sub-rows indented 20px. **JS `assets/js/components/rating-input.js`.** Vanilla; no dependencies. Wires chip clicks to a hidden input + dispatches a synthetic `change` so host forms react. Slider input event updates the readout span. The "empty" state — slider sits at the midpoint visually for thumb visibility but the row carries `data-tt-rating-empty="1"` so server-side and JS treat it as unrated — clears on first interaction. On form submit, any slider still flagged empty has its `name` attribute stripped so the value doesn't post; the server then receives only real coach picks. Arrow-key navigation between chips matches native radiogroup behaviour. **Dropped into four surfaces.** `PostGameEvaluationForm` and `PlayerSelfEvaluationForm` (single overall rating → chip grid). `RateActorsStep` (per-category multi-player rate grid — main category row + nested sub-category rows → inline-slider rows). `HybridDeepRateStep` (player self-eval per-category → inline-slider rows with `label_hidden=true` to fit the existing `<th>` label column). **Server-side validate() upgraded to floats.** `RateActorsStep::validate` and `HybridDeepRateStep::validate` now cast incoming rating values to float + snap-to-0.5 instead of `(int)`-truncating to whole numbers (which would have silently flattened a 7.5 pick to 7). The wizard state read also casts to float so the input pre-fill survives a step-back round trip. `EvaluationInserter` mirrors the float+snap before writing to `tt_eval_ratings`. **Existing roster JS preserved.** The per-player status pill + overall progress counter in `RateActorsStep` checks the sliders the same way it checked the number inputs (`.tt-rate-input` selector); the only new behaviour is skipping sliders with `data-tt-rating-empty` from the "filled" count. The sub-cat → main-cat auto-compute (rounded average of non-zero subs written back to the main category) still works — now reads/writes floats, snaps to 0.5, and mirrors the value into the main row's readout span so the visual stays in sync. **Asset enqueue** at three hosts: the two wizard steps register the handles in their `render()`, and `FrontendTaskDetailView` (the workflow task surface) enqueues unconditionally on every task detail (low cost, simple). Idempotent — same handles across surfaces. **Out of scope.** Re-skinning the flat `CoachForms::renderEvalForm` legacy eval surface (the canonical surface per CLAUDE.md §3 is the wizard, which this PR covers). The wizard-chrome step-indicator is unrelated. Minor bump — new user-visible component, four surfaces upgraded. Strings via `__()`; .po sync lands next CI cycle. (closes #1067) =

= 4.17.6 — Persona dashboard editor: visibility-hint badge per slot (closes #1102). Pilot triage 2026-06-01 surfaced after #1104 unblocked AC's dashboard: ~12 widgets/tiles were configured for the Assistent-trainer persona but only 3 rendered, because the typical AC user (`tt_coach` WP role) lacked the caps the underlying widgets / tiles gate on. The editor had no feedback — admins drop widgets onto a persona's template, the layout publishes, and the widget silently vanishes for the persona's typical user at render time. This ship adds a small green-check / amber-warning line in the slot properties detail block so the admin sees the visibility outcome at *configure* time, not pilot-test time. **PHP — bootstrap payload.** `EditorPage::buildBootstrap()` now publishes three new fields the editor JS consumes: (1) `default_role_for_persona` — `{ persona_slug: wp_role_slug }` map. New `PersonaResolver::defaultWpRoleFor( persona )` inverts the `WP_ROLE_TO_PERSONA` constant and hard-codes `head_coach` / `assistant_coach` → `tt_coach` since those split at runtime. (2) `role_caps` — `{ wp_role_slug: { cap_name: true, ... } }` map. One entry per WP role any of the in-scope personas might map to, sourced from WP's `get_role()->capabilities`. (3) `tile_caps_by_slug` — `{ view_slug: cap }` map sourced from `TileRegistry::allRegistered()` so the JS can compute the effective cap for a `navigation_tile` widget (whose own `cap_required` is empty — the cap lives on the underlying tile slug it points at). **JS — `renderDetailBlock` now persona-aware.** Takes `activePersona` (= `state.persona`, the persona currently being edited). For widgets with a `cap_required`, and for `navigation_tile` slots whose chosen data source maps to a `tile_caps_by_slug` entry, the editor resolves the effective cap, compares it against the active persona's default-role caps, and renders a one-line badge under the "Capability required" line: green ✓ "Visible to %s users by default" when the role holds the cap; amber ⚠ "Hidden — %s users lack `cap` by default. Grant via Authorization → Matrix or remove from this layout." when it doesn't. Both lines include an italic caveat line clarifying the check is against the persona's *default* WP role only — per-user matrix scopes can override either way. **JS — re-renders live.** Changing the data source on a `navigation_tile` slot calls `commit()` → `renderAll()` → `renderProperties()` → `renderDetailBlock()`, so the hint updates as the admin tries different slugs. **CSS.** Two new classes — `.tt-pde-detail-vis--ok` (subtle green tint) and `.tt-pde-detail-vis--blocked` (subtle amber tint) — sit just under the existing `.tt-pde-detail-cap` line. Caveat span is greyer + italic so the badge reads as advisory, not blocking. **What this is NOT.** Not a hard block — admins can still publish layouts with amber-flagged widgets (a per-user matrix scope might grant the cap to *some* users with that persona even if the role default doesn't, e.g. an Assistent-trainer who's also been given a per-user `tt_view_evaluations` cap). Not a runtime change — the GridRenderer / TileRegistry visibility filters are unchanged. This is purely an editor-time hint. **Caveats / known limitations** (parked for follow-up if pilot reports). (a) The check uses the *default* WP role's caps, not the persona's matrix entitlements. Cap-bridged matrix entries (e.g. `evaluations:read` for `head_coach`) won't show in `role_caps` unless the bridge already wrote them to the WP role at boot. For tooling-time hints this is acceptable; a precise check would query the matrix per-persona instead, which is bigger work. (b) Hint depends on `state.persona`, not a hypothetical preview user, so the editor answers "if a user with the persona's default WP role looked at this, would they see it?" — matches the question the admin is asking. **Verification.** Open Admin → Dashboard-lay-outs → Assistent-trainer. Click the Podium tile slot (or any slot configured for AC that AC's matrix doesn't grant). The detail block now shows an amber ⚠ line naming the missing cap. Switch the dropdown to Hoofdtrainer — the same slot shows a green ✓. Patch bump. (closes #1102) =

= 4.17.5 — Player detail view: gate dev-data tabs + avg-rating KPI behind the matrix (closes #1107). Pilot triage 2026-06-01 surfaced after #1104 unblocked AC's dashboard: visiting any player's detail view as Assistant Coach showed the Evaluations / PDP / Trials tabs and rendered their contents on click — a safeguarding regression of #1060 / migration 0136 (which stripped `evaluations`, `pdp_file`, `pdp_verdict`, `pdp_conversations`, `team_chemistry`, `dev_ideas`, `player_behaviour_ratings` from the AC matrix). The view file declared `'evaluations' => __( 'Evaluations' )` etc. unconditionally and `renderEvaluationsTab()` queried `tt_evaluations` directly without an auth check — textbook CLAUDE.md §4 violation. **`tabs()` is now matrix-aware.** Takes `int $user_id`. Conditionally adds the Evaluations / PDP cycle / Trials entries based on `MatrixGate::canAnyScope( $user_id, $entity, READ )` for `evaluations` / `pdp_file` / `trial_cases` respectively. Notes keeps its existing `tt_view_player_notes` cap-gate. Profile / Goals / Activities stay always-on — AC's seed grants both `goals` and `activities` at team scope. The two call sites in `render()` (active-tab validation + nav rendering) hoist the result into `$tab_set` so the filter applies consistently. **Defense in depth at each tab renderer.** `renderEvaluationsTab` / `renderPdpTab` / `renderTrialsTab` re-check the same matrix scope at entry. Belt + braces: a direct `?tab=evaluations` URL still routes through here even though tabs() filtered the tab out of the navigation, and the call-site dispatch doesn't re-validate post-filter. Each unauthorised render emits a clear `tt-notice` paragraph and returns — no SQL runs, no rows leak. **At-a-glance KPI tile.** The "Avg rating" tile in the rail strip was the silent side-door — `atAGlance()` computes the value + trend arrow from the same `tt_eval_ratings` rows the Evaluations tab gates on. Wrapped the `<a class="tt-player-kpi">` block in the same `MatrixGate::canAnyScope(..., 'evaluations', READ)` check so AC users don't see the number or the direction arrow even from the player profile rail. Attendance + Goals tiles stay visible — both gate on entities AC's seed already grants. **Out of scope for this PR.** Moving the dev-data SQL out of the view file into matrix-aware repository methods (the CLAUDE.md §4 stretch path the issue body called out). The minimum-viable gate-only fix lands here so AC stops seeing evaluations TODAY; the repository extraction is a deeper refactor that benefits from its own focused issue once the pilot confirms the gate-only fix is correct. Verification: log in as AC, hit a player's profile — Evaluations / PDP / Trials tabs absent from the nav, Avg rating absent from the rail, `?tab=evaluations` URL renders the "no permission" notice. HC dashboard unchanged. Patch bump. (closes #1107) =

= 4.17.4 — Authorization: deterministic person lookup + dedupe migration for duplicate `tt_people` rows (closes #1104). Pilot triage 2026-06-01 surfaced the real cause of the empty Assistent-trainer dashboard symptom we'd been chasing: the AC test user (wp_user_id=10) had **two active tt_people rows** (id=7 and id=30) for the same WP user in the same club. `AuthorizationService::getPersonIdByUserId` did `SELECT id FROM tt_people WHERE wp_user_id=%d AND status='active' AND club_id=%d LIMIT 1` with no `ORDER BY`. MySQL returned id=7 (lowest PK in practice, but non-deterministic). The team-people bridge then looked for assignments on `person_id=7` — none. Zero resolved scopes, zero dashboard tiles, even though the admin Persoon edit page (which reads the real row, id=30) showed the team assignment. Two sources of truth silently disagreed for the entire pilot session. **Resolver hardening (`AuthorizationService::getPersonIdByUserId`).** Added `ORDER BY id DESC` to the `LIMIT 1`. Picks the most-recently-created active row when duplicates exist — same tiebreak the dedupe migration uses so resolver + cleanup agree. Existing callers behave identically when no duplicates exist (the typical case). **New helper `AuthorizationService::findAllActivePersonIdsByUserId`.** Returns every active person_id linked to a WP user in the current club. Used by the Rechten-diagnose page to surface the duplicate-detection warning. **Application guards in `PeopleRepository::create()` + `update()`.** Block a second active person record from claiming a WP user that another active row already owns in this club. Inactive rows are allowed to share `wp_user_id` (they don't resolve). Returns `false` on collision — matches the existing repository error pattern. **Dedupe migration `0139_dedupe_tt_people_by_wp_user.php`.** Finds every `(wp_user_id, club_id)` cluster with > 1 active row. Per cluster, picks the winner: most `tt_team_people` rows referencing the person id first, then highest `id` (newest). Sets losers to `status='inactive'` — NOT deleted, so operators can revive any inactivated row from the People admin. Logs the winner/loser mapping to `tt_audit_log` under `action='person.deduped'` with payload `{ wp_user_id, winner_id, winner_rel_cnt, loser_id, loser_rel_cnt }` for forensic recovery. Forward-only; idempotent. **Rechten-diagnose warning hint.** When a WP user has > 1 active person_id, the diagnose page now renders a red ⚠ row listing all linked Persoon ids with edit links and a one-line explanation pointing at #1104 + migration 0139. The two-source disagreement is what made the original triage three hours; the warning makes the next occurrence ten minutes. **Verification.** On Casper's install the manual DELETE of the duplicate row (Persoon #7) made AC's dashboard render the full configured layout immediately — confirming the duplicate was the symptom's root cause. The shipped migration automates the same fix on every install at upgrade time. Patch bump — bug fix, no operator-breaking change. (closes #1104) =

= 4.17.3 — Authorization: remove `podium_panel` from assistant_coach default seed (closes #1105). Scope-creep follow-up to #1060 / migration 0136. Conservative — operator customisations (`is_default=0`) stay so an academy that deliberately granted Podium to AC via the Authorization admin keeps the override. Forward-only (reverting would re-introduce the leak). Idempotent. Flushes `MatrixRepository::clearCache()` so in-flight AC sessions pick up the change on their next request. **No code changes needed** — every gated surface already routes through `current_user_can()` / `MatrixGate::can()`, and the Podium tile's `TileRegistry` entry gates on `podium_panel:read`; removing the matrix row automatically hides the tile on the AC dashboard. **Out of scope.** A broader audit of which other entities AC's seed grants but shouldn't (`rate_cards`, `compare`, `reports`, `people`, `vct` scope) is parked at #1106 awaiting per-entity decisions.
