= 4.17.2 — Architecture: LookupTranslator-into-repository pattern, Evaluations module as worked example (closes #806 first slice; refs follow-ups #1077-#1080). Today ~30 sites across the codebase echo raw `tt_lookups.name` directly without translating — the bypass problem #806 is built to close. The architectural fix is to **pre-localise lookup-backed fields at the repository boundary** so view code that does `echo $row->type_name_localised` gets the localised string by construction (bypass becomes structurally impossible). **Evaluations module — first slice shipped here.** `EvaluationsRepository::recentForCoach()` now pulls the full lookup row (id + name + lookup_type) in its SELECT, then after fetch hydrates every result row with `type_name_localised` via `LookupTranslator::name( $lookup_stub )`. The raw `type_name` field stays for back-compat (consumers that need the canonical key for grouping / filtering). Updated consumers: `FrontendMyEvaluationsView::renderForCoach()` echoes `$e->type_name_localised` with a fallback to raw, and `EvaluationsRestController::recent_for_coach()` exposes both keys in the JSON response (`type_name` + `type_name_localised`). **Other 4 modules tracked separately.** #1077 Goals (status / priority / link_type), #1078 Activities (activity_type_key / plan_state / attendance status), #1079 Players (status / preferred_foot / position), #1080 Pdp (file status / verdict decision). Each ships as its own focused issue with the Evaluations repo as the pattern reference. After all four ship, the CI lint allow-list (#804) can be tightened: the "bypass" IS the translation now, so a future raw-echo regression is caught at lint time. **No behaviour change for pilot users** — the localised string was already rendered correctly via the legacy `LookupTranslator::name()` calls in the view layer; this just moves the translation point one layer earlier so future regressions can't slip through. Patch bump — architectural refactor. (closes #806 first slice, refs #1077, #1078, #1079, #1080) =

UNIQUE on `(club_id, eval_type_id, eval_category_id)` so duplicates are impossible; indexed on both ends. If empty, all categories render (back-compat). **Server-side validation.** `ReviewStep::submitPlayerFirst` now rejects ratings for categories outside the type's allowlist with a clear `category_not_allowed_for_type` error — closes the "dev-tools form editing" bypass the issue flagged. **Admin matrix.** New `TalentTrack → Eval Type Categories` admin page (`?page=tt-eval-type-categories`) lists every eval_type with checkboxes for each main category. = 4.17.0 — Printable season-start goal-setting intake + selectable methodology reference (closes #1064). Ships the design-of-record from `.local-mockups/player-goal-intake/`. **Per-player intake** (`?tt_goal_intake_print=1&player_id=N[&season=YYYY/YY]`) — 3 A4 portrait pages emitted by `PlayerGoalIntakePrintRouter`: page 1 is the speler-snapshot (identity + last-season stats pulled from `tt_attendance` + average eval rating from `tt_eval_ratings` + 4 pre-printed lookback cards drawn from the player's recent evaluation medians + prior goals + a placeholder for trainer notes); page 2 is the doelen 1 + 2 panel with full-width Doelomschrijving fields + principle/action code boxes + waarom/hoe meten/eigenaar rows; page 3 is the doel 3 + afsluitende reflectie + 3-up signatuur row + reminder-to-transfer-into-TalentTrack CTA. **Team-batch** (`?tt_goal_intake_print=1&team_id=N`) — same router, iterates the team's active roster in jersey-then-surname order and concatenates each player's 3 pages into a single print job (browser's "Save as PDF" produces one multi-page PDF). **Methodology reference card** (`?tt_methodology_ref_print=1&sections=…`) — emitted by `MethodologyReferencePrintRouter`. Up to 3 pages: **Spelprincipes** (grouped by team-function + team-task buckets), **Voetbalhandelingen** (3-column layout by `category_key`), **Leerdoelen** (2-column by side, sub-grouped by team-task). The `sections` query param accepts any subset of `principles,actions,leerdoelen` so the operator can print just the slice they need. Content pulled verbatim from the seeded methodology tables — academy edits flow through automatically on the next print. **Entry points.** Player detail row gains "Print doelenintake" (cap-gated on `tt_edit_goals`); team detail page-actions gains "Print seizoens-intakes" (same cap, single multi-page job); methodology view page-actions gains "Print referentiekaart" (cap-gated on `tt_view_methodology`). All three open the standalone print document in a new tab so the originating view is preserved. **`FrontendViewBase::pageActionsHtml()` extended** with optional `target` key so page-action anchors can open in a new tab when appropriate (used by all three new print actions; backward-compatible — `target` is omitted by default). **CSS.** Print-tuned styles embedded in each router (`@page { size: A4 portrait; margin: 0 }`, mobile/tablet preview chrome stripped via `@media print`); `page-break-inside: avoid` on goal boxes + leerdoel entries so they never get sliced mid-field; deep-teal `#155a57` accent stays readable in B/W copies; no dompdf / wkhtmltopdf dependency added — the existing `MatchPrepPrintRouter` browser-print pattern handles the PDF rendering via the user's local print dialog. **Fully Dutch on a Dutch site** — every visible string runs through `__()` so the .pot/.po sync (next CI cycle) picks them up. **Out of scope**: a server-rendered PDF via dompdf so the file is downloaded directly without the user clicking "Save as PDF" in the print dialog — defer to a follow-up if pilot wants it; the browser-print path matches every other printable surface in the plugin today and works on every modern browser. Minor bump — new feature epic affecting two persona-facing surfaces. (closes #1064) =

= 4.16.1 — Evaluations: FrontendMyEvaluationsView SQL extracted to a repository + new REST endpoint (closes #920). Per CLAUDE.md §4 (SaaS-readiness smell test: "if you deleted every file under `src/Shared/Frontend/`, could the REST API still return correct data?"), the coach-context "My evaluations" feed was failing — the view ran an inline `$wpdb->get_results()` join across `tt_evaluations` + `tt_lookups` + `tt_players` and nothing equivalent existed via REST. **What ships.** New `TT\Infrastructure\Evaluations\EvaluationsRepository::recentForCoach( int $coach_user_id, int $days = 30 ): array` holds the single source-of-truth query. Filters by `e.coach_id = %d`, `e.archived_at IS NULL`, `e.eval_date >= cutoff` (default 30-day trailing window), and `( e.club_id = CurrentClub::id() OR e.club_id IS NULL )` for SaaS-readiness. Returns row objects in the shape the view template already expects (`id`, `eval_date`, `opponent`, `game_result`, `type_name`, `first_name`, `last_name`). **View refactor.** `FrontendMyEvaluationsView::renderForCoach()` now calls the repo (one-liner) instead of the inline SELECT — no behaviour change for the user-facing widget. **REST endpoint.** New `GET /wp-json/talenttrack/v1/evaluations/recent` registered on `EvaluationsRestController`. Defaults `coach_id` to the current user; explicit `coach_id` query param is allowed only when the requester also holds `tt_view_all_teams` (so an HoD can audit their staff — otherwise 403 with `forbidden_coach_override`). `days` capped to 90 to keep the query bounded; defaults to 30. **Cap gating aligns with #1060.** The endpoint gates on the `my_evaluations` matrix entity at `SCOPE_SELF` (via `MatrixGate::can()`) — assistant coaches keep this entity even after losing the broader `evaluations` entity, so the self-scoped "what did I author?" feed remains operational for AC users. Response shape: `{ coach_id, days, count, rows }` where each row carries `id`, `eval_date`, `opponent`, `game_result`, `type_name`, and a nested `player: { first_name, last_name, display }` object. **Pilot impact.** Zero — the user-facing widget renders the same content. The win is structural: a future non-WordPress front end can consume the same data via the new endpoint without re-deriving the SQL. The sibling-audit follow-up flagged in the issue (`FrontendMyGoalsView`, `FrontendMyActivitiesView`, `FrontendMySessionsView`) stays open — each becomes its own issue if found to repeat the anti-pattern. Patch bump. (closes #920) =

= 4.16.0 — Authorization: Assistant Coach scope tightened to operational-only (closes #1060). Pilot need surfaced 2026-05-31: an assistant coach who is also a parent of a player on the team (or a sibling team) shouldn't see other players' development data; more broadly, AC inherited too much of HC's read access. Per the locked 2026-05-31 design: **AC is operational, HC is development.** The AC-with-kid case is then handled naturally by the existing parent path — AC sees no per-player dev data on any kid (including their own), and as parent of their own kid they see that kid's evaluations / PDP / behaviour the same way every parent does. **Matrix changes** (`config/authorization_seed.php`): the AC persona block loses the per-player development-data entities — `evaluations`, `pdp_file`, `pdp_verdict`, `pdp_conversations`, `team_chemistry`, `dev_ideas`, `player_behaviour_ratings`, plus the matching tile-visibility panels (`evaluations_panel`, `team_chemistry_panel`, `pdp_panel`). AC keeps `team`, `players` (identity-only), `people`, `activities`, `goals`, `attendance`, `methodology`, `football_actions`, `reports` (team aggregates), `rate_cards`, `compare`, `documentation`, `pdp_calendar_export` (self-scoped — exports own calendar slots), `workflow_tasks`, `task_completion`, `my_evaluations` (self-scoped — operational signal of WHEN they rated, not what's in the eval), `player_status`, `trial_inputs`, `player_timeline`, `invitations`, `player_notes`, `vct`, and every staff-development entity. **Backfill migration** (`0136_assistant_coach_scope_tightening.php`): on existing installs, DELETEs the 10 removed AC rows from `tt_authorization_matrix` — **conservatively** scoped to `is_default = 1` so any operator who deliberately granted broader AC access via the Authorization admin keeps that override. Flushes `MatrixRepository::clearCache()` so AC sessions pick up the change on their next request. **No per-surface code changes needed** — every gated view already routes through `current_user_can()` or `MatrixGate::can()`, both of which consume the matrix at runtime; removing rows automatically blocks the corresponding surfaces (Evaluations tab, PDP tab, Behaviour ratings, Team chemistry sandbox, rate-actors wizard via the upstream `tt_edit_evaluations` gate on `NewEvaluationWizard`). **Match-prep / match-execution surfaces unchanged** — those gate on the `match_prep` / `match_execution` entities (kept for AC); HC's per-player notes still flow through to AC inside those operational windows. **AC-with-kid path unchanged** — the parent role grants the AC-also-parent visibility to their own kid's evaluations / PDP through the existing `'parent'` persona block, independent of the AC matrix. **Verification**: use `wp-admin/admin.php?page=tt-auth-chain-debug`, pick an AC user, confirm each removed cap returns false (`tt_view_evaluations`, `tt_view_player_behaviour`, `tt_view_pdp`, `tt_manage_team_chemistry`). **Out of scope for this PR**: the per-tab visibility on the player profile when AC reaches a player's page (Goals tab still renders since `goals` entity stays operational for match-prep flow) — flagged as a follow-up if pilot reports the tab feeling out of place. The wider analytics-drill cap (`tt_drill_analytics`) per the issue's §3 also defers to a follow-up; current behaviour is the explorer view already gates on the `analytics` entity (kept HC-only). Minor bump — visible behaviour change for every existing AC. (closes #1060) =

= 4.15.9 — Player dashboard: mobile-first CSS extraction (closes #916). Per CLAUDE.md §2 (mobile-first by default) — the player dashboard's overview tab was rendering with an inline desktop-first `<style>` block that started at the 2-column layout and patched downward via `@media (max-width: 820px)`. Two violations: (a) `max-width` downward patch instead of `min-width` upward scale, (b) `820px` is a non-standard breakpoint (canonical set is 480 / 768 / 1024). **What ships.** New stylesheet `assets/css/frontend-player-dashboard.css` enqueued via `wp_enqueue_style( 'tt-frontend-player-dashboard', … )` parallel to the existing `tt-frontend-mobile` enqueue. Base CSS targets ~360px (single column, FIFA card stacked below info), `@media (min-width: 768px)` upgrades to the two-column grid with the card on the right. The 820px breakpoint is gone; rounded to the canonical 768px. Inline `style=""` attributes on `.tt-overview-grid`, `.tt-overview-card`, the print-row container, and the print-link `<a>` all extracted into the stylesheet (`.tt-overview-print-row` + `.tt-overview-print-link` classes added). The render path stays the same shape — just emits class names instead of inline declarations. **Pilot impact.** Overview at 360px (player landing on a phone) no longer renders with desktop-first proportions. Tap targets and content order match the mobile-first contract every other surface follows. Patch bump. (closes #916) =

= 4.15.7 — Blueprint editor: picking a player no longer silently fails (closes #1054). Pilot bug surfaced 2026-05-31: coach picks a player from the slot picker, page reloads, slot stays empty, no error shown. The end-to-end trace was: JS PUT to `/blueprints/{id}/assignment` carried a perfectly valid `{ slot_label, tier, ref: { kind: 'player', player_id: 52 } }` body — but the slot stayed empty on every browser. Root cause was three-layered: (1) `TeamBlueprintsRepository::setAssignment` called `wpdb->insert/update/delete` and never checked the return value — when the INSERT collided on a UNIQUE constraint the failure was swallowed and `true` was returned anyway, (2) `set_blueprint_assignment` REST handler then returned `200 OK` to the client, (3) the JS reloaded the page believing the assignment had landed. **The underlying INSERT collision** was rooted in migration 0129's UNIQUE constraint `uniq_slot_tier (blueprint_id, slot_label, tier)` — no `club_id` — combined with `setAssignment`'s SELECT-before-INSERT that DID filter by `club_id`. Any stale row for the same `(blueprint_id, slot_label, tier)` but a different `club_id` made the SELECT miss it and the INSERT collide. **The fix.** Migration 0135 widens the UNIQUE to `uniq_slot_tier_club (club_id, blueprint_id, slot_label, tier)` so the constraint matches how the repo logically scopes assignments (and stays correct under future SaaS multi-tenancy where `CurrentClub::id()` returns ≠1). `setAssignment` now checks every `wpdb` return value, captures `wpdb->last_error`, and returns `false` on DB-layer failure; new `lastError()` accessor exposes the message. The REST controller calls `setAssignment`, returns `500` with the captured error when persistence failed, and turns malformed-player-ref payloads (caller sent `kind=player` but no usable `player_id`) into a `400` via a new `\InvalidArgumentException` path in `coerceAssignmentRef` — previously these were silently coerced to `null` and triggered a slot DELETE. The JS `refForRosterEntry` guard returns `null` rather than building `{ kind: 'player', player_id: NaN }`; `saveAssignment` short-circuits with a localised alert when the ref is malformed, reads the server's error message out of the response body on `!ok`, and verifies the response payload contains the persisted ref before reloading (so a regression that returned 200 OK + ref:null would no longer silently "succeed"). New i18n string `bad_ref`. **Pilot impact**: blueprint editor's primary interaction works again on every install where stale rows might exist; on installs where the silent-fail wasn't surfacing, every layer is now defensive enough that a future regression would surface as a visible alert instead of a vanishing pick. Patch bump. (closes #1054) =

= 4.15.6 — Methodology seed top-up: Omschakelen leerdoelen + Spelinzicht/Communicatie sub-actions (closes #1061). Two seed-content gaps surfaced during the 2026-05-31 pilot review against the source PDF `07. Voetbalmethode.pdf`. **Football actions** — sheet 3 (Introductie) decomposes `Spelinzicht` and `Communicatie` (the two "Ondersteunend" buckets) into sub-items. Source: migration `0134_methodology_leerdoelen_omschakelen_and_action_subitems.php`. Patch bump. (closes #1061) =

= 4.15.5 — REST: `BaseController::isPositiveInt()` must be public, not protected (closes #1057). Saving any lookup value returned HTTP 500 with `Uncaught TypeError: call_user_func(): Argument #1 ($callback) must be a valid callback, cannot access protected method TT\Infrastructure\REST\LookupsRestController::isPositiveInt()`. Four controllers (LookupsRestController, InvitationsRestController, LookupNormalisationRestController, PushSubscriptionsRestController) register routes with `'validate_callback' => [ self::class, 'isPositiveInt' ]` against URL segments that need positive-integer validation. The validator lives on `BaseController` as `protected static`, which works fine for internal calls but breaks when WP REST invokes the callback via PHP's `call_user_func()` — that runs outside the class hierarchy and cannot reach protected methods even on a subclass. The route-arg validation step 500s before the handler ever runs. One-line fix: promote `BaseController::isPositiveInt()` to `public`. Every PUT / DELETE on `/lookups/{type}/{id}`, every invitation endpoint that takes an id, and the push-subscriptions endpoint all start working again. Pilot impact: any operator who tried to edit a lookup value on a live install since v4.11.0 (when this validator pattern was introduced) would have hit the 500 — surfaced today during the post-drain pilot pass on the Posities lookup admin. Patch bump. (closes #1057) =

= 4.15.4 — Match execution: late-event affordance — retroactive goal + sub UI in PENDING_REVIEW (closes #1049, #1033 follow-up D). Pilot ask: "I forgot to log the goal at 31'" / "I logged the sub but at the wrong minute." Today's PENDING_REVIEW state (v4.15.0) accepts the writes via the existing goal-event / substitution endpoints, but the view had no UI for inputting them at retroactive minutes. v4.15.4 adds the UI. **Late-event panel.** New `tt-mexec-late-event` section renders only when state = PENDING_REVIEW. Dashed warn-orange border so it reads as a corrective surface, not a primary action. Header: "Add late events" + the minute range (`Minute 0–{half_length+10}` per the locked validator default). Two collapsible `<details>` panels inside: **+ Add late goal** (player picker · half picker · minute input · Log goal button) and **+ Add late substitution** (off-player · on-player · half · minute · Log substitution button). All inputs hit the 48px touch-target floor; minute input uses `inputmode="numeric"` + `min=0 max=half_length+10` per the locked validator default; numeric inputs at 16px to prevent iOS auto-zoom. Reuses `QueryHelpers::player_display_name()` for the picker options; lists every player in the match's availability roster (`$players_by_id`), keyed sort. **POSTs.** Inline IIFE wires the two forms to the existing v4.15.0 endpoints — `/goal-event` and `/substitution` — building the payload with a client-generated `event_uuid` (uses `crypto.randomUUID()` with a Math.random fallback for older browsers, matching the offline-queue replay contract from #847). On success → `window.location.reload()` so the v4.15.1 recompute side effect can re-derive attendance + minutes from the new event. On failure → `window.alert()` with the server's error message. Client-side guard refuses negative minutes and identical off/on players before sending. **Out of scope.** Editing existing events (e.g. "I logged the sub at minute 30 but it was actually 28"). Today's workflow: reverse via the existing `route_goal_event_delete` path then re-add via the new late-event form. A "edit timestamp on existing event" affordance is a separate quality-of-life follow-up. Server-side minute validation (HTTP 400 for out-of-range) is also deferred — client-side `max` attribute + the existing assertEditable guard cover the common cases. No new endpoint, no new cap. Patch bump. (closes #1049) =

= 4.15.2 — Match executions listing surface at `?tt_view=match-executions` (closes #1047, #1033 follow-up A). Per the locked default (2026-05-30): all states by default. State pills use the v4.15.0 colour conventions — green for live, amber for pending review, grey for finalized. **Scope.** Cap-gated on `tt_view_activities`. Persona scoping: coach sees executions on teams they have a `tt_user_team_link` row for; HoD/Admin (and anyone with `tt_view_all_teams` or `tt_edit_settings`) sees club-wide. **Entry point.** New "Match executions" page action on `?tt_view=activities` next to "+ New activity" — visible to anyone with `tt_view_activities`. = 4.15.1 — Match execution: attendance + minutes recompute on PENDING_REVIEW edits and on Finalize (closes #1048, #1033 follow-up C). v4.15.0 introduced PENDING_REVIEW with editable score / sub / goal endpoints, but `tt_attendance` (status + minutes_played per player) was only written once during `route_finish`. Any subsequent edit in PENDING_REVIEW left the derived attendance totals stale until... nothing, because the one-shot write never re-fired. **Recompute extracted to the repository.** New `MatchExecutionRepository::recomputeAttendanceAndMinutes( $execution_id )` owns the attendance + minutes write loop that used to live inline in `route_finish`. Reloads the prep snapshot, runs `computeMinutes()` against the current substitution log, reconciles stale rows (the #1032 sweep), and writes status + `minutes_played` for every player in the prep's availability list. Idempotent — same prep + same sub log → same attendance rows. **Trigger pattern.** Per the user's "both" decision (2026-05-30): the recompute fires (a) on every PENDING_REVIEW edit (substitution log changes, goal-event add / delete) via a new `recomputeIfPendingReview()` helper that gates by the current state, AND (b) on Finalize as a belt-and-braces pass before the FINALIZED flip closes the window for missed writes (offline-queue replay, transient DB errors). Live writes during the match still skip the recompute — they happen too often, and `route_finish` covers the transition. Score edits also skip (a score change doesn't touch any input to `computeMinutes`). **Failure handling.** Per the locked default: on recompute exception the method swallows the error, logs at warn level via `Logger::warn( 'match_execution.recompute_failed', … )` with the execution_id, and returns false. The caller's primary action (the edit, the finalize) has already succeeded — aborting an edit because a side effect failed would be hostile, and the next edit or finalize will re-fire the recompute. **route_finish refactor.** The inline attendance + minutes write block (76 lines) is replaced with a single `$repo->recomputeAttendanceAndMinutes( $exec_id )` call. Behaviour-identical for the End-match tap path. **Out of scope.** Async / background recompute — inline is fine, ~20 attendance rows max per execution. Recompute on live-trio writes — preserved as today's behaviour. No schema, no REST surface change, no new caps. Patch bump. (closes #1048) =

= 4.15.0 — Match execution: pending-review state + Finalize action (partial #1033, MVP). Pilot ask: "after the match when I complete the match the match execution should move to a separate place where they all are stored and where they can be viewed and adjusted when needed." Today, tapping "End match" makes the execution immediately read-only — no opportunity to fix a missed goal, a wrongly-timed sub, or a missed score-tap. **State machine extended.** `MatchExecutionState` enum gains two values: `PENDING_REVIEW` (post-match, editable) and `FINALIZED` (terminal, read-only). The legacy `FINISHED` constant is kept as a deprecated alias for one release; migration `0133_match_execution_state_pending_review` backfills any existing `state='finished'` row to `'finalized'` (safe interpretation — those rows were closed at a time without the new edit affordance). New `EDITABLE` set (live trio + PENDING_REVIEW) drives the write-guard. **REST.** Tapping "End match" (`route_finish`) now lands the execution in `PENDING_REVIEW` instead of `FINISHED`, but still writes attendance + minutes + flips the activity to completed — every existing post-match consumer keeps working. New `route_finalize` (`POST /match-execution/{activity_id}/finalize`) transitions PENDING_REVIEW → FINALIZED. Score / substitution / goal-event / goal-event-delete endpoints gain a single-line `assertEditable()` guard that returns HTTP 409 when the execution is FINALIZED. NOT_STARTED still accepts writes (offline-queue replay tolerance). **View.** A new post-match status section renders above the existing footer when state ∈ {PENDING_REVIEW, FINALIZED}: an amber pill ("Match ended · pending review") or grey pill ("Finalized — read-only"). PENDING_REVIEW additionally shows a red "Finalize match" button + a one-line warning "Locks the match. Goals, subs, and score cannot be edited after." A tiny inline IIFE wires the button to the new `/finalize` endpoint with a confirm prompt and a reload on success. **Out of scope for this MVP (filed as #1033 follow-ups for the next analyst pass).** Dedicated listing surface (`?tt_view=match-executions`) so coaches can find every pending-review or finalized match without going through activity detail; "Matches needing review" widget on the coach hero; auto-recompute of attendance + minutes when subs are edited in PENDING_REVIEW (today's behaviour: attendance/minutes write once at `route_finish` and don't recompute on later edits); explicit "late-event" affordance with a retroactive minute picker; mockup additions for the pending-review + finalized states. v1 ships the spine of the feature (state machine + Finalize + edit-guards) — the surfaces around it follow in scoped follow-ups. **Why a minor bump.** New state, new endpoint, new visible UI affordance. Migration 0133 is additive only (no schema change — just data backfill). No new caps. (partial #1033) =

= 4.14.1 — Standard report: minutes played per team / player (closes #1034). New curated analytics report at `?tt_view=minutes-report-team&team_id=N&from=YYYY-MM-DD&to=YYYY-MM-DD&type=all|League|Cup|Friendly`. Pre-built answer to "how is game-time distributed across the squad?" — the question the pilot academy asked for explicitly and that today can only be answered via CSV export. **Layout.** Per the locked mockup at `.local-mockups/standard-reports/minutes-played/index.html` (Option A — squad table). One row per player who actually got on the pitch in the window; columns: Player | Total | Matches | Starts | Subs in | Subs off | Avg / match | League | Cup | Friendly | % available. Sortable. Default sort: total minutes desc. Defaults to a 365-day window (one season), filterable via the toolbar's date pickers + team picker + match-type chip (All / League / Cup / Friendly). When a match-type filter is on, the Total and Avg columns reflect that bucket; per-type columns stay informational for one-glance comparison. Player names link to the player profile (with a `tt_back` pill back). Cap-gated on `tt_view_analytics`, scope matches the existing Attendance reports. **Data source.** New `TT\Modules\Analytics\Reports\MinutesQuery::forTeam( team_id, from, to )` domain service. For each match-type activity in the window, pulls the lineup from `tt_match_prep_lineup`, the substitution log from `tt_match_execution_substitutions`, and the half-length from `tt_match_prep.half_length_minutes`; runs the same `MatchExecutionRepository::computeMinutes()` helper the match-finish endpoint uses to derive per-player minutes. Aggregates per player: total minutes, distinct matches on the pitch, starts (counted once per activity even if started both halves), subs-in (came on via the log), subs-off (started but came off before full time), minutes bucketed by `game_subtype_key`. Squad-wide `available_minutes` total is summed once and reused per row for the % available column. Matches with a prep but no execution row credit starters with the full half length so plan-only weeks don't disappear from the report. **Routing.** Registered in `DashboardShortcode::dispatchAnalyticsReportView` and surfaced as a new card on `?tt_view=analytics` "Standard reports" next to the existing Team / Player attendance reports. Back-label resolver entry added ("Back to Minutes played"). **Out of scope for v1 (deferred follow-ups in #1034).** A player-detail variant (the Option C spotlight from the mockup) — same `MinutesQuery` data, different surface. REST endpoint (`GET /talenttrack/v1/teams/{id}/minutes`) so a future non-WP front end can consume the same data. Registering a `minutes_played` fact + matching KPIs in the `Analytics\FactRegistry` so the explorer + entity Analytics tabs auto-surface this signal. Friendly / Tournament / Indoor lookup expansion if the canonical seed grows beyond League / Cup / Friendly. No schema, no new caps, no REST yet — patch bump. (closes #1034) =

= 4.14.0 — Wizard chrome — V3 sidebar timeline (closes #1036). The v3.110.102 wizard chrome read too heavy in pilot use: completed steps were solid dark-green pills that pulled the eye off the form; the action row had no visual hierarchy (Cancel in a red-bordered outlined button competed with Save / Back / Next); and on mobile the action row wrapped unpredictably as 3-4 ~120px pills don't fit a 360px row. V3 chrome (from `.local-mockups/wizard-chrome/index.html`, "Sidebar timeline" variant) replaces this with a vertical rail + reorganised action row. **Step indicator.** Desktop ≥720px: a 220px vertical rail on the left of the form, dot + label + optional caption per step. Done = filled teal dot with `✓`. Current = outlined teal dot with a filled inner + 4px soft ring, bold teal-deep label, "You are here" caption. Pending = outlined grey dot, muted label. NA = dashed dot, muted label with line-through, "Not applicable" caption. Vertical line between dots fills teal between done steps. Mobile <720px: rail collapses to a single teal-tinted disclosure (`Step X of Y · {current label} ▾`) that expands on tap. **Action row.** Desktop: Cancel left (white outline that hover-tints to danger), Save · Back in a quiet middle group (text-buttons), Next far right (teal pill with `›` chevron that nudges on hover), all inside a tinted container with a 1px separator above. Mobile: 3-row grid via `grid-template-areas` — Next full-width on top (thumb spot), Back full-width below (subordinate outline), Save · Cancel text-link row at the bottom. Buttons carry `data-role="next|back|save|cancel"` so the grid mapping is DOM-order-independent; the middle wrapper goes `display: contents` on mobile so its children participate in the parent grid directly. **Implementation.** `FrontendWizardView::renderProgress()` rewritten to emit the vertical rail markup + a mobile disclosure toggle; preserves the existing state classes (`is-done`, `is-current`, `is-pending`, `is-na`). The action bar wraps Save + Back in `.tt-wizard-actions-middle` and adds `data-role` to every button. The whole form area is wrapped in `.tt-wizard-layout` (CSS Grid 1fr on mobile, 220px+1fr ≥720px). Existing inline IIFE script gains a small rail-toggle handler that flips `data-rail-open` on the layout container and `aria-expanded` on the toggle button. CSS replaces the prior `.tt-wizard-progress*` block with the new `.tt-wizard-rail*` rules and the prior `.tt-wizard-actions` block with V3 actions + the mobile button grid. Live mandatory-field validation, help drawer, autosave-status placement, and the Next-button loading state preserved. `prefers-reduced-motion` honoured. **Out of scope.** Functional "Edit" jump-back per step (mockup convention) needs `WizardState` to be multi-step-back capable; v1 omits the Edit link and renders the rail with dot + label + caption only. Three new English strings ("Step %1\$d of %2\$d", "You are here", "Not applicable") land in the next `chore(i18n)` sync. **Why a minor bump.** Visible visual rework affecting every wizard; no behaviour change. (closes #1036) =

= 4.13.4 — Lookup admin: master-detail side-panel layout (closes #1039). The list-first lookup admin (`FrontendConfigurationView::renderLookupCategoryEditor`, design from #985) used three full-width views toggled by `data-state` (list / add / edit). Clicking a row hid the list and showed the form full-width; returning to the list lost the operator's spot. With the small list (typically 5-20 values) + small form, the right pattern is **master-detail**: list on the left, panel on the right of the same view. **PHP** — the two existing renderers (`renderLookupListView` + `renderLookupFormViews`) are now wrapped in a `.tt-lkp-md` grid container inside the admin root. The form section moves inside a new `.tt-lkp-panel` `<aside>` alongside an empty-state ("Tap a row to edit…") and a back-to-list pill (mobile only). The `+ Add value` button moves out of the list-header and into a right-aligned actions row beneath the list card. **CSS** — `.tt-lkp-md` is `grid-template-columns: 1fr` on mobile and `minmax(0,420px) minmax(0,1fr)` at ≥880px with `position: sticky` on the right panel so it stays in view as the list scrolls. The view-state map gains an empty-state slot (visible when `data-state="list"`); the form section is visible at `data-state="add"` or `data-state="edit"`. On mobile (<880px), the list collapses out of view when a row is clicked or `+ Add` is pressed — the panel uses the full viewport — and the back-to-list pill becomes visible. Desktop keeps both columns in view. The 48px touch target and mobile-first base CSS (CLAUDE.md §2) are preserved; the existing translations grid (one locale per row from #1038) sits cleanly inside the narrower panel column. **JS** — no changes. The state machine still maps list → add | edit via the existing `[data-tt-lkp-go]` buttons and row-click handlers; the back-to-list pill is just another `data-tt-lkp-go="list"` button. **Out of scope** — the list rendering (columns, coverage dots, drag-to-reorder) is unchanged; REST + save flow unchanged; caps unchanged. Three new English strings ("Tap a row to edit", "or click + Add value to seed a new one.", "← Back to list", "Edit lookup value" aria-label) land in the next `chore(i18n)` sync. No schema. Patch bump. (closes #1039) =

= 4.13.3 — Rate-players step pulls from the actual on-pitch set (closes #1032). After a match-execution finished, the rate-players wizard step surfaced too many people in the roster — bench / unused subs (`minutes_played = 0`), players from other teams via stale attendance rows, and the existing v4.3.20 linked-guest support gave no visual cue why "another team's player" appeared. Root cause: `RateActorsStep::ratablePlayersForActivity()` read `tt_attendance` — club-scoped only, with no team filter, no minutes filter, and downstream of the match-finish endpoint that INSERTs an attendance row for every available player including bench (`MatchExecutionRestController.php:246-272`). Stale rows from prior runs were never reconciled. **The rate-step now pulls from the actual on-pitch set for match-type activities.** New `ratablePlayersForMatch( $activity_id, $team_id )` collects the `DISTINCT player_id` set from `tt_match_prep_lineup` (starting XI per half) UNION `tt_match_execution_substitutions.player_on_id` (excluding `reversed_at` events), then SELECTs the resolved player rows with an `is_guest` flag derived by comparing `pl.team_id` against the activity's team. Bench-only players are excluded by construction. Already-rated guard preserved. For training and any non-match activity (`activity_type_key NOT IN ('match','game')`), the legacy attendance-based query stays — there is no lineup data to derive from. **Guest pill on rate-step rows.** Rows where `pl.team_id` differs from the activity's `team_id` carry a `Guest` pill between the player name and the status pill, with a tooltip "On loan from another team for this match." Answers the "why is this other-team player here?" surprise the user surfaced. **Stale-attendance reconciliation in finish endpoint.** Before the per-availability INSERT/UPDATE loop, the finish endpoint now DELETEs any `tt_attendance` row for the activity whose `player_id` is NOT in the prep's availability list — when match-execution finishes, availability is the source of truth. Eliminates the cross-list contamination from prior mark-attendance runs. **Out of scope.** Wizard-loop symptom (bug 3 in the issue) is downstream of the wizard-restart fix #1006 and gets re-tested after that lands; the rate-step → behaviour-step transition itself is unchanged. The lineup / subs schema doesn't carry an `is_guest` column, so guest detection is derived from `tt_players.team_id` instead of a per-event flag — works for the pilot's model where guests are players from sibling teams already in the club. No schema, no REST, no new caps. Patch bump. (closes #1032) =

= 4.13.2 — Match prep print: dedicated route so admin bar + theme chrome stay off paper (closes #1031). Printing the on-screen match-prep view (`?tt_view=match-prep&activity_id=N`) leaked the WordPress admin bar plus the active theme's header / nav / footer onto every printed page — the v4.12.15 `@media print` block only hid TalentTrack's own dashboard chrome. Chasing theme selectors via `@media print` is fragile (breaks on theme switch) and can't suppress the admin bar (a logged-in DOM injection). **Fix mirrors the existing `PdpPrintRouter` pattern.** New `TT\Modules\MatchPrep\Print\MatchPrepPrintRouter` hooks `template_redirect` / `admin_init` at priority 1, intercepts `?tt_match_prep_print=1&activity_id=N`, suppresses the admin bar via `add_filter('show_admin_bar', '__return_false')`, and emits a standalone `<!doctype html>` document with embedded landscape-A4 styles. The dashboard shortcode never runs; the active theme's template hierarchy never loads — so no chrome can leak. Body layout mirrors the existing `MatchPrepPdfExporter` landscape-A4 sheet (lineup per half + bench, match goals, per-player attention with `!` / camera markers) so the on-screen print matches what the PDF exporter already produces. Cap-gated identically to the on-screen view (`tt_edit_activities`). A small toolbar at the top of the print view offers Print + Close buttons, hidden via `@media print` so they don't appear on paper. Registered in `MatchPrepModule::boot()`. The on-screen "Print (landscape A4)" toolbar button in `FrontendMatchPrepView` becomes a `target="_blank"` anchor pointing at the new route; the previous `data-tt-mp-print` JS handler that called `window.print()` directly is dropped (it was the workaround that caused the leak in the first place). The v4.12.15 `@media print` block in `assets/css/frontend-match-prep.css` stays untouched — kept as a fallback for users who hit Cmd/Ctrl+P from the on-screen view without using the Print button. No schema, no REST, no new caps. Patch bump. (closes #1031) =

= 4.13.1 — Lookup admin: internal-key now populates on row click, locales render one-per-row (closes #1037, #1038). Two related bugs on the list-first lookup admin (`?tt_view=lookups&type=<…>`), bundled because they share the same file and the same root design pattern. **#1037 — Internal-key field empty on row click.** `FrontendConfigurationView::renderLookupFormViews()` rendered TWO `<form data-tt-lkp-form>` elements when the page loaded without `?edit=N` — one inside `tt-lkp-view-add`, one inside `tt-lkp-view-edit`. `lookup-admin.js` used `querySelector('[data-tt-lkp-form]')` which returns the first match, so it bound to the form inside `view-add` (hidden by default). Clicking a row populated the hidden form; the visible form (in `view-edit`) stayed blank — internal key, sort order, translations all empty. Fix: collapse to ONE form inside a single `tt-lkp-view-form` section. CSS now maps both `data-state="add"` and `data-state="edit"` to `view-form`. The form's heading + hint flip between "Add new value" / "Edit value" via new `data-tt-lkp-form-title` and `data-tt-lkp-name-hint` hooks driven by `clearForm()` / `populateFromRow()`; four new i18n keys (`title_add`, `title_edit`, `hint_add`, `hint_edit`) carry the strings through to JS. **#1038 — Translation locales render in messy grid.** When `show_desc=false` (positions, evaluation categories, etc.), the desktop ≥640px breakpoint set the translations grid to 3 columns and hid the empty `<span class="tt-lkp-tx-cell-desc">` spacer with `display:none`. `display:none` removes the element from grid auto-flow, so the next locale badge fell into the empty third column instead of starting a new row — five locales of two visible cells each wrapped into a 3-column grid produced badges and inputs in the wrong places. Fix: drop the desktop 3-column variant entirely and the empty-spacer span at the source. The grid is now always 2 columns (locale | input); description spans columns 2/-1 on its own row when present. Mobile-first compliant, one-locale-per-row at every viewport. **Out of scope**: side-panel master-detail layout (#1039) — builds on this clean single-form base. No schema, no REST, no caps change. Patch bump. (closes #1037, closes #1038) =

= 4.13.0 — Team chemistry page rework, single-tier blueprint port (closes #1002, supersedes #1007). Full surface rework of `?tt_view=team-chemistry`. Ports the design-of-record mockup at `.local-mockups/team-chemistry/index.html` onto the live surface: three-column shell with a roster sidebar on the left, the pitch in the centre, and a stacked KPI scoreboard plus coach-marked pairings panel on the right. The chemistry surface is single-tier — the chemistry engine scores primary cells only, so the secondary / tertiary tier stack the blueprint editor exposes is irrelevant here. Each pitch position renders one slot card. **PHP** — `FrontendTeamChemistryView` rewritten end-to-end: `renderToolbar()` emits a CSP-friendly auto-submitting formation picker plus the Suggested / Try-a-lineup segmented toggle and a Save-as-blueprint action; `renderRosterSidebar()` renders a searchable, fit-sorted roster (best team-fit score per player, computed once from the aggregator's depth chart so no extra query); `renderPitchCard()` hands off to `PitchSvg` for the actual pitch + chemistry-link SVG (unchanged, still emits the data-attributes the JS picker binds to); `renderRightColumn()` stacks a headline `Link chemistry / 100` card on top of composite / formation / style / depth / coverage sub-cards plus the coach pairings panel with a collapsible add form. The v1 depth-chart "1st / 2nd / 3rd choice" table is dropped — the same data still flows to the picker via the localised payload. CSS assets enqueue on every entry path (team picker + board + error states), not only inside the cap-gated sandbox enqueue. **JS** — `frontend-team-chemistry.js` retargets selectors from `.tt-chem-sandbox*` to `.tt-tc-sandbox*`, adds `wireSegmentedToggle()` (binds both Suggested + Try-a-lineup segments), `wireRosterFilter()` (live case-insensitive substring filter on the sidebar) and `wireFormationAutosubmit()` (replaces the v1 inline `onchange="this.form.submit()"` so CSP-strict installs work). Sandbox + bottom-sheet picker + save-as-blueprint modal behaviour is unchanged from v3.110.174 / v3.110.184; only the surface they bind to has moved. **CSS** — `frontend-team-chemistry.css` rewritten on the mockup's token system (`--tt-tc-bg`, `--tt-tc-panel`, `--tt-tc-line`, `--tt-tc-accent`, `--tt-tc-accent-2`, `--tt-tc-strong`, `--tt-tc-weak`, etc.). Mobile-first base CSS for ~360px; tablet at 768px (two-col with right column going full-width below); desktop at 1180px (three columns, right column sticky). Touch targets ≥ 44px on every interactive surface; 16px input font-size for iOS no-zoom; `prefers-reduced-motion` honoured on the picker + sandbox-on slot animations. Bottom-sheet picker + save-as-blueprint modal styles preserved from v3.110.174 / v3.110.184 with the new token names. **v1 bugs caught + fixed (supersedes #1007).** Four investigation-grade defects folded in alongside the layout port: (1) inline `onchange="this.form.submit()"` on the formation dropdown broke under CSP `script-src 'self'` and produced a console warning on stricter dashboard themes — replaced with `data-tt-tc-autosubmit`; (2) the v1 team picker had no stylesheet enqueued because the CSS file was loaded only inside the cap-gated `enqueueChemistrySandboxAssets()`, so read-only viewers landing on the team picker saw unstyled `<a>` cards — CSS now enqueues from the top of `render()`; (3) no styled empty-state for installs without `tt_formation_templates` rows — v4.13.0 renders a `.tt-tc-emptystate` card with a clear "Configure one in Settings → Team development" pointer; (4) help-link button "How does this work?" stacked above the board, pushing the toolbar + pitch down 60px on phones for no benefit — moved below the board so the chemistry score is the first thing on screen. **Out of scope** — chemistry algorithm unchanged (`BlueprintChemistryEngine::computeForLineup()` / `computeForSuggested()`, `ChemistryAggregator::teamChemistry()`); REST contracts unchanged (`GET /teams/{id}/chemistry`, `POST /teams/{id}/chemistry/preview`, pairings CRUD, blueprint create + assignments PUT); no schema; same caps (`tt_view_team_chemistry` for read, `tt_manage_team_chemistry` for sandbox + pairings); multi-team chemistry comparison + per-player drilldown deferred; the mockup's "Why?" reasoning panel with Default / Slot / Link states is shape-only and deferred — the JS state machine needs server-side explanation strings the engine doesn't currently emit. **Why minor bump** — meaningful surface rework + restored functionality on a previously-broken page (#1007). Patch bump would understate the visual + interaction change. (closes #1002, supersedes #1007) =

= 4.12.15 — Match prep print polish + short player names (closes #1023). Two scopes ship together because they share files (the match-prep view + CSS) and the on-screen short-name change is what the print CSS inherits. **A. Print polish (6 items).** (1) Dashboard brand banner / DEMO strip / breadcrumbs no longer leak onto paper — `@media print` block now hides `.tt-dash-header`, `.tt-dash-brand`, `.tt-dash-actions`, `.tt-dash-demo-pill`, `.tt-dash-help`, `.tt-user-menu`, `.tt-back-pill` alongside the existing breadcrumbs / back-link / toolbar / picker / drawer rules. The shared chrome rendered by `DashboardShortcode::render()` was previously the first thing the coach saw on every printed page. (2) Page title `Wedstrijdvoorbereiding — <Activity> · <date>` is now the first visible printed line — source string changed from `Match prep — %1$s · %2$s` to `Match preparation — %1$s · %2$s` so the Dutch translation lands at 12pt bold (~16px CSS), no top margin (`.tt-match-prep-title { font-size: 12pt !important; margin: 0 0 3mm !important; }`). (3) Pitch slot labels — both the number circle AND the player-name pill — now render on paper: print block forces `color: var(--tt-mp-ink) !important; background: #fff !important; print-color-adjust: exact;` on `.tt-mp-slot .tt-mp-slot-num` and `.tt-mp-slot .tt-mp-slot-name`. Empty slots keep their muted colour. (4) Restore `!` (red) and camera (green) icon colours on print — `.tt-mp-dps tbody td.tt-mp-col-spec.tt-mp-on` forces `color: var(--tt-mp-danger)` and `.tt-mp-dps tbody td.tt-mp-col-cam.tt-mp-on` forces `color: var(--tt-mp-success)`, both with `print-color-adjust: exact;` so they survive the browser's "Background graphics off" default. (5) Compact Wedstrijddoelen so the whole spreadsheet fits on one landscape-A4 page at 100% print scale on Chrome / Edge / Firefox: goal-box font 9pt → 7.5–8pt; row padding halved (`0.25mm 1mm`); section heading padding halved (`0.5mm 2mm`); `.tt-mp-goals-row` forced to two columns so attacking + defending sit side by side; grid columns tightened from `50mm / 1fr / 70mm` to `48mm / 1fr / 64mm`; body font 10pt → 9pt; line-height 1.25 → 1.2. (6) Empty goal lines print as a clean horizontal rule with no placeholder dots — placeholder text (`…`, `Goal 1…`) is forced `color: transparent !important; opacity: 0 !important;` on every print-time goal-line input via `::placeholder` / `::-webkit-input-placeholder` / `::-moz-placeholder`. **B. Short player names (whole match-prep surface).** New `TT\Shared\Util\PlayerShortName::resolve( iterable $players ): array` helper resolves a list of players into a `[ player_id => short_name ]` map. Default: first name only (`Daan`, `Senna`, `Javi`). Disambiguation: when two players in the input set share a first name, both render as `<firstName> <lastInitial>` (`Daan P`, `Daan A`); the disambiguation scope is the input set, not the whole club. Graceful fallback for players with missing first or last names (returns the available part, or `—`). v1 assumes Western "first last" order — East-Asian "last first" conventions deferred. `FrontendMatchPrepView::render()` computes the map once from the team roster and threads it into every render site: the roster column (`Selectie · Minuten`), the Doen per speler column, the Rollen & standaardsituaties column, the pitch slot labels (via the bootstrap payload's `players[].name` which the JS `renderPitches()` / `renderRoster()` / `renderDps()` / `renderRoles()` paths consume unchanged), and the availability drawer (same `state.players[].name` source). Full name is still passed on the bootstrap as `players[].full` so a future variant can opt back into the long form. **Out of scope**: other surfaces (Player profile, Activities list, Team detail) keep full names; the short-name helper is `Shared\Util` so future call sites can adopt it but this PR is match-prep only per the spec. **Mobile-first preserved**: the print block sits at the end of the file; the base on-screen CSS is unchanged. Patch bump — UX defect bundle (six print items + one vocabulary change), no schema, no REST, no behavioural change beyond the listed items. (closes #1023) =

= 4.12.10 — PHPStan rule — vocabulary constants enforcement (PR-set 8 of 8, closes #988 umbrella). Final PR-set in the #988 umbrella migration. Lands the custom PHPStan rule that flags raw string-literal comparisons against any value already enumerated under `TT\Domain\Vocabularies\Lookups\*` or `TT\Domain\Vocabularies\Enums\*` — the regression gate that prevents PR-sets 1-7's work from silently un-doing itself as new code lands. Rule class `TT\Tests\PhpStanRules\VocabularyConstantsRule` walks `BinaryOp\Identical` / `NotIdentical` / `Equal` / `NotEqual` AST nodes plus `in_array($value, [...], $strict)` calls; for each string literal it cross-references against the `const ALL` arrays in the 29 vocabulary classes (built lazily via reflection so new vocabularies land in subsequent PR-sets without rule edits) and emits an error suggesting the typed constant (`AttendanceStatus::PRESENT` instead of `'present'`). Out of scope by design: switch / match arms, SQL string literals, array keys, default-parameter literals, migration-seed values — those are either canonical-stored-value contexts (DB layer is the source of truth) or refactors better handled as a separate sweep. Per #988's locked decisions (2026-05-28), the rule ships as **infrastructure but disabled by default** — the backwards-compat allowlist (REST endpoints accept BOTH the raw literal AND the typed constant for one release) keeps the raw literals legal until the deprecation window closes; flipping the rule into the default analyse run today would flood the build with errors on the same call sites the allowlist deliberately tolerates. Wire-up is via the opt-in overlay `tests/PhpStanRules/vocabulary-constants-rule.neon` — operators include that file from their own `phpstan.local.neon` to run the rule on demand (and CI will flip to it once the allowlist sunsets in the next minor). `composer.json` gains an `autoload-dev` PSR-4 mapping for `TT\Tests\PhpStanRules\` -> `tests/PhpStanRules/` so the rule class is autoloadable to PHPStan without bleeding into the runtime plugin classmap. The two existing files under `src/Domain/Vocabularies/` (`Lookups/` 27 classes + `Enums/` 2 classes) are unchanged — PR-set 8 is pure tooling, no behaviour change, no schema, no REST, no UI. **Approximate impact at error-level today** (rough grep against `src/`, excluding `Vocabularies/` itself): low hundreds of comparison sites would be flagged; PR-sets 1-7 already swapped the highest-traffic ones to constants, so the residual is the long tail of one-off comparisons across the codebase plus the REST-allowlist call sites the deprecation contract explicitly tolerates. Closes the #988 umbrella issue. Patch bump — tooling only. (closes #988 umbrella, PR-set 8 of 8) =

= 4.12.9 — Vocabulary constants — auth + ideas + invitations + behaviour (PR-set 7 of #988). Adds seven typed constants classes — six under `TT\Domain\Vocabularies\Lookups\*` (`IdeaStatus`, `IdeaType`, `InvitationStatus`, `InvitationKind`, `BehaviourRating`, `PotentialBand`) and one under `TT\Domain\Vocabularies\Enums\*` (`ImpersonationEndReason`) — mirroring the PR-set 1 / 2 / 3 / 4 / 5 / 6 precedent with `const ALL` + static `isValid()`. `IdeaStatus` enumerates the nine values stored on `tt_dev_ideas.status` (`submitted`, `refining`, `ready-for-approval`, `rejected`, `promoting`, `promoted`, `promotion-failed`, `in-progress`, `done`) — backs the `idea_status` lookup seeded by migration 0115; `IdeaType` enumerates the four values stored on `tt_dev_ideas.type` (`feat`, `bug`, `epic`, `needs-triage`) — backs the `idea_type` lookup; `InvitationStatus` enumerates the four values stored on `tt_invitations.status` (`pending`, `accepted`, `expired`, `revoked`) — backs the `invitation_status` lookup seeded by migration 0108; `InvitationKind` enumerates the three role variants stored on `tt_invitations.kind` (`player`, `parent`, `staff`); `BehaviourRating` enumerates the five 1..5 anchor values on `tt_player_behaviour_ratings.rating` — backs the `behaviour_rating_label` lookup seeded by migration 0042; `PotentialBand` enumerates the five values stored on `tt_player_potential.potential_band` (`first_team`, `professional_elsewhere`, `semi_pro`, `top_amateur`, `recreational`) — backs the `potential_band` lookup seeded by migration 0042 and consumed by `PlayerStatusCalculator::POTENTIAL_BAND_SCORES`; `ImpersonationEndReason` enumerates the two code-only values stored on `tt_impersonation_log.end_reason` (`manual`, `expired`) — code-only enum (not operator-editable), lives under `Vocabularies\Enums\*` per #988's locked sub-namespace split. The existing `TT\Modules\Development\IdeaStatus` / `IdeaType` and `TT\Modules\Invitations\InvitationStatus` / `InvitationKind` constants are kept as deprecated aliases that delegate to the new canonical `Vocabularies\Lookups\*` values; aliases stay for one release and are removed in the next minor. Replaces PHP-side raw string literals at the call sites — `PlayerStatusCalculator` (`POTENTIAL_BAND_SCORES` map keys), `Infrastructure\REST\PlayerStatusRestController::setPotential()` (allowlist), `FrontendPlayerStatusCaptureView::render()` (potential allowlist + select-option map), `FrontendPlayerDetailView` (potential-popover band map), `PersonaDashboard\Widgets\SystemHealthStripWidget::countPendingInvitations()` (defensive fallback literal), `ImpersonationService::end()` (default-parameter literal), `ImpersonationAdminPost::end()` (Switch-back handler). **CertificationType not in scope this PR-set** — empirical grep on the codebase surfaced zero PHP-side string-literal comparisons against the six `cert_type` lookup keys (`uefa_a`, `uefa_b`, `uefa_c`, `first_aid`, `gdpr`, `child_safeguarding`) seeded by migration 0048; the values are read-only on the operator-facing surface, so a constants class would document them without making any literal-to-constant swap. Deferred to a future PR-set if call sites surface — same shape as PR-set 4's `PlayerValue` / `AgeGroup` / `Position` deferral. **BehaviourRating** is also a documentation-only addition for this PR-set — the column is DECIMAL so the canonical 1..5 anchor values are stored numerically and PHP-side comparison literals don't surface; the class documents the seeded anchor set for future PHPStan rule consumption (PR-set 8). SQL string literals (`SET end_reason = 'expired'` in the ImpersonationService orphan-cleanup UPDATE), migrations, .po / .pot files, test fixtures, and JavaScript stay as literals per the spec. REST endpoints continue to accept BOTH the raw literal AND the constant for one release per #988's locked plan; the deprecation timeline sits in `docs/rest-api.md`. Patch bump per the umbrella's "Patch bump (per PR-set), separate PR each" rule. Seventh of 8 PR-sets. (partial #988) =

= 4.12.8 — Vocabulary constants — player + team (PR-set 4 of #988). Adds two typed constants classes under `TT\Domain\Vocabularies\Lookups\*` for the player-side roster vocabularies — `PlayerStatus` and `PreferredFoot` — mirroring the PR-set 1 / 2 / 3 / 5 / 6 precedent with `const ALL` + static `isValid()`. `PlayerStatus` enumerates the five lifecycle values stored in `tt_players.status` (`active`, `trial`, `inactive`, `released`, `graduated`) per the canonical contract codified across `JourneyEventSubscriber::emitStatusTransition()`, `LabelTranslator::playerStatus()`, the `PlayersPage` status dropdown, and the trials / workflow forms that write the column. The `archived_at` column from migration 0010 is the soft-delete / bulk-archive marker (NULL vs timestamp); `status` is the orthogonal lifecycle marker, so archived players still carry one of the five values. Migration 0061 already back-filled legacy `status='deleted'` rows from v3.89.1-and-earlier delete paths back to `'active'` (with `archived_at` populated), so the five-value vocabulary is the only stored set on every install. `PreferredFoot` enumerates the three lowercase keys stored in `tt_players.preferred_foot` (`left`, `right`, `both`); backs the `foot_option` lookup (operator-editable, seeded by migration 0001 with TitleCase display labels), but the stored player-record value is the lowercase key per `RosterDetailsStep::validate()`'s `sanitize_key()` + allowlist. The empty-string sentinel ("not specified") is intentionally not part of `ALL` — it represents the absence of one of the three options. Replaces PHP-side raw string literals at the high-traffic call sites — `PlayersPage` (status dropdown, form defaults, stub creation), `PlayerCsvImporter` (default status on bulk import), `FrontendPlayerDetailView` (trial-player gate on the trials tab empty state), `FrontendTrialsManageView` (inline player-create on trial-case create + status flip), `JourneyEventSubscriber::emitStatusTransition()` (the three-arm status-transition match — pairs cleanly with PR-set 5's `JourneyEventType::*` swap on the emit-arg side), `LabelTranslator::playerStatus()` (display-label switch), `Tournaments\Wizard\SquadStep` (trial-badge gate on the squad picker), `Wizards\Player\ReviewStep` (status assignment on wizard submit), `Workflow\Forms\RecordTestTrainingOutcomeForm` (status='trial' on prospect-admitted player creation), `Workflow\Forms\AwaitTeamOfferDecisionForm` (status='active' on accepted team offer), `DemoData\PlayerGenerator` (status='active' on seeded players + the `tt_player_created` hook payload), `Wizards\Player\RosterDetailsStep` (preferred-foot allowlist). The `PlayerStatus::GRADUATED` value is intentionally included even though the `PlayersPage` status dropdown currently exposes only four of the five values — the `JourneyEventSubscriber` already emits a `graduated` journey event when the column flips to that value, so the vocabulary documents the canonical five-state set; UI surfacing of the fifth dropdown option is a separate UX task. `LabelTranslator::playerStatus()` adds a `case PlayerStatus::GRADUATED` arm for symmetry; the legacy `'deleted'` arm is preserved as a literal for historical-display safety against migration-0061-pre installs. **PlayerValue / AgeGroup / Position not in scope this PR-set** — empirical grep on the codebase surfaced zero PHP-side string-literal comparisons against the 8 player-value keys, the U7-U23 / Senior age-group codes, or the 11 position abbreviations; the values live in `tt_lookups` and are read-only on the operator-facing surface, so a constants class would document them without making any literal-to-constant swap. Deferred to a future PR-set if call sites surface. SQL string literals (`WHERE pl.status='active'` in `PlayersPage::render_list`), migrations, .po / .pot files, test fixtures, and JavaScript stay as literals per the spec. REST endpoints continue to accept BOTH the raw literal AND the constant for one release per #988's locked plan; the deprecation timeline sits in `docs/rest-api.md`. Patch bump per the umbrella's "Patch bump (per PR-set), separate PR each" rule. Fourth of 8 PR-sets. (partial #988) =

= 4.12.7 — Vocabulary constants — PDP + trial (PR-set 3 of #988). SQL string literals (`status IN ('open','extended')` in the trial-cases active-window queries, `status NOT IN ('completed','archived')` in season carryover), migrations, .po / .pot files, test fixtures, and JavaScript stay as literals per the spec. Form-internal radio-button values in `ReviewTrialGroupMembershipForm` (`offer_team_position`, `decline_final`) stay as form-input literals — they're mapped to canonical `TrialCaseDecision::*` values inside `serializeResponse()` and aren't themselves stored. REST endpoints continue to accept BOTH the raw literal AND the constant for one release per #988's locked plan; the deprecation timeline sits in `docs/rest-api.md`. Patch bump per the umbrella's "Patch bump (per PR-set), separate PR each" rule. Third of 8 PR-sets. (partial #988) =

= 4.12.4 — Match prep: widen on-screen layout + landscape A4 print CSS + save-indicator layout-shift fix + in-place print button (closes #998). Four bundled UX defects on the `?tt_view=match-prep&activity_id=<id>` surface, all visible to the head coach. **(1) Widen on-screen** — the shared `.tt-dashboard` wrapper caps at 1100px, which left the 3-column spreadsheet narrower than the paper coaches print to. Adds a `.tt-dashboard:has(.tt-match-prep)` override that lifts the cap to 1320px on the match-prep route only; every other dashboard view stays at 1100px. Desktop grid columns widen from `12.5rem | 1fr | 20rem` to `14rem | 1fr | 22rem` so the left roster names and the right Player-focus / Roles panes get breathing room. Mobile (≤ 360px) and tablet (768–1099px) breakpoints untouched. **(2) Landscape A4 print CSS** — new `@page { size: A4 landscape; margin: 8mm; }` plus an `@media print` block that drops the dashboard chrome (breadcrumbs, back-pill, page-head actions, toolbar) and every overlay (picker, drawer, backdrops) so only the spreadsheet renders on paper. Selectors verified against the live markup emitted by `FrontendMatchPrepView::render()` rather than guessed: `.tt-breadcrumbs`, `.tt-back-link-wrap`, `.tt-mp-toolbar`, `.tt-mp-picker(-backdrop)?`, `.tt-mp-drawer(-backdrop)?`. The 3-column grid is forced on at print regardless of viewport width — printing from a narrow window must still emit the spreadsheet, not a stacked phone layout. Pitch tints, panel-head shading, and the "on pitch" green cells are kept via `print-color-adjust: exact` because the match-prep is unreadable without them. `break-inside: avoid` on each player row, goal box, and set-piece row prevents a player from splitting across two pages. **(3) Save-indicator layout shift** — the toolbar's continuous-save indicator toggles between "Unsaved changes…" / "Saving…" / "All changes saved." / empty as the coach types. The flip to empty collapsed the indicator's box to 0px height and reflowed the toolbar height every keystroke; coaches lost their cursor / scroll position mid-edit. Fix is purely defensive CSS on `.tt-mp-save-state`: `min-height: 1.4em`, `min-width: 12ch`, `display: inline-flex` so the box reserves one line's worth of vertical space and ~12 chars of horizontal space regardless of content. The textContent flip still happens in JS — only the bounding box is now stable. **(4) Print button** — the toolbar's `PDF (landscape A4)` anchor routed to `?tt_view=exports&exporter=match_prep_pdf&activity_id=N`, dumping the coach onto the central Exports page with two clicks and a full context switch to get a PDF. Replaced with a `<button type="button" data-tt-mp-print>Print (landscape A4)</button>` and a one-line JS handler in `frontend-match-prep.js` that calls `window.print()` in-place. The new print CSS from item (2) handles the layout; the browser's "Save as PDF" within the print dialog covers the file-output case for free. Dropped the unused `$pdf_url = add_query_arg([...])` block from `FrontendMatchPrepView::render()`. The exports page's match-prep PDF exporter route stays available for users who explicitly visit `?tt_view=exports` — it just isn't the primary affordance from inside the match-prep editor any more. Dutch string: `Afdrukken (liggend A4)`. `.local-mockups/match-preparation/index.html` updated in parallel so the mockup remains the design-of-record. Patch bump — UX defect bundle, no schema, no REST, no behavioural change beyond the four items above. (closes #998) =

= 4.12.1 — PlayerAttendanceCalculator queried `tt_attendance.status` with TitleCase literals `'Present'` / `'Absent'` / `'Excused'`, but the canonical contract codified in `TT\Domain\Vocabularies\Lookups\AttendanceStatus` (v4.11.1, #988 PR-set 1) stores the column in lowercase (`'present'` / `'absent'` / `'excused'`) — the calculator's three SQL CASE expressions silently never matched, so attendance score / streak / status verdicts in `src/Infrastructure/PlayerStatus/` were computing against an empty bucketing of the rows the calculator HAD pulled in. The numerator collapsed to 0 on every call; `low_confidence` fired on every player. Pilot symptom: every player's dashboard attendance card showed either 0% or `null` even on players with full attendance history. Fix replaces the three TitleCase literals with `$wpdb->prepare(... %s ...)` placeholders bound to `AttendanceStatus::PRESENT|ABSENT|EXCUSED`; `use TT\Domain\Vocabularies\Lookups\AttendanceStatus;` added at the top of `PlayerAttendanceCalculator.php`. No data migration needed — `tt_attendance.status` is created with `DEFAULT 'present'` lowercase at install time (Activator.php), and the legacy back-fill from the boolean `present` column also writes lowercase, so no legacy rows carry TitleCase values that would need normalising. The other TitleCase call sites surfaced by the same grep (EvidencePacket.php, ActivitiesRestController.php, LabelTranslator.php, MatchExecutionRestController.php, FrontendMatchExecutionView.php, LookupCanonicalSeeds.php, DemoData\Generators\ActivityGenerator.php, Excel\ExcelImporter.php, migration 0093's seed colours) are part of the #988 umbrella's planned PR-sets and stay out of scope for this targeted bug fix. Patch bump — silent-data-miss bug fix. (closes #996) =

= 4.12.0 — Lookup canonical-language drift audit + admin review tool (closes #987). The `tt_lookups.name` column is contractually the stable English internal key; `tt_translations` carries the per-locale display label. Pilot installs ended up with a mixed-language vocabulary in the column because earlier operator workflows let admins type anything into `name` and never populated `tt_translations` — opening any lookup category showed a list that was half Dutch, half English. This release ships the data fix without changing the schema. New `LookupCanonicalSeeds` class is the single source of truth for canonical English values per `lookup_type`, with a reverse map (drifted-NL -> canonical-EN) seeded from migration 0060's English+Dutch pairs and case-insensitive matching for lowercase drifts like `present` -> `Present`. New migration 0132 walks every `tt_lookups` row, cross-checks `name` against the canonical seed map, and writes a `lookup.needs_review` entry to `tt_audit_log` for every drifted row — current value, suggested canonical, detected source locale, full canonical option list. Idempotent: re-running the migration on an already-audited install skips rows whose entity_id already has an open review entry. The migration never auto-renames anything — every accepted rewrite goes through the human-in-the-loop admin tool. New frontend view `?tt_view=lookup-normalisation` (cap `tt_access_frontend_admin`, mirrors `FrontendConfigurationView`'s gate) lists the pending-review queue: one card per row, with the current value, a dropdown of canonical options pre-selected to the migration's suggestion, and a locale dropdown defaulting to the detected source. Per-row Accept rewrites `tt_lookups.name` to the chosen canonical AND upserts the drifted value as a `tt_translations` entry in the selected locale, so dashboards keep showing the operator-visible Dutch/English label via the existing `LookupTranslator` resolution chain. Per-row Skip leaves the row as-is and records the operator's deliberate decision. Both actions write follow-up `lookup.normalisation.applied` / `lookup.normalisation.skipped` audit entries; the queue join filters resolved rows out so the row stops surfacing without mutating the original audit entry (audit log is append-only by design). New REST endpoints `POST /lookup-normalisation/{audit_id}/accept|skip` under the existing `talenttrack/v1` namespace, both gated on `tt_access_frontend_admin`. Accept defensively rejects canonical values that aren't in the per-`lookup_type` allowlist, so an operator can't typo a fresh drift back into the column. New Configuration tile "Lookup canonical-language review" appears only while there are pending rows (with a count in the description) — it disappears the moment the queue empties. Mobile-first per CLAUDE.md §2: 360px base, 640px breakpoint, all interactive targets >= 48px tall, `prefers-reduced-motion` respected via the existing site CSS. No schema change beyond audit-log writes; no breaking REST change; no behaviour change for end users (the translator chain keeps surfacing the correct locale label whether `name` is `Aanwezig` or `Present`). Minor bump — new admin surface + new audit-log workflow. (closes #987) =

= 4.7.0 — Activities list date-bucket redesign + Type filter + past pinned-top toggle (closes #973). Rewrites the `?tt_view=activities` list surface end-to-end as a faithful port of `.local-mockups/activity-list/index.html`. **Filter row**: existing Team picker now sits beside a new Type picker, lookup-backed via `QueryHelpers::get_lookups('activity_type')` so operator-customised vocabularies appear automatically. Side-by-side 2-column grid on mobile (360px), full breakpoint set ramps the frame to 720px at 768px and 880px at 1100px+ so the list breathes on desktop without exploding to full width. **Past pinned to top**: a single persistent button — `N past activities hidden · Show ▼` ⇄ `N past activities shown · Hide ▼` — replaces the chronological interleave. URL state `?include_past=1` preserves the choice across refresh / shared links. Past = `session_date < today AND plan_state IN ('completed','cancelled')`; the toggle stays visible in both states with its chevron rotating 180° on expand. **Date buckets** (top→bottom, empty buckets collapse to nothing): **⚠ Needs attention** (past planned, header + per-row date badge in `--tt-warn` — surfaces past activities the coach forgot to close), **Today** (date badge in `--tt-accent`, header carries day-of-week + date), **This week** (`today < session_date <= upcoming Sunday`), **Next week** (next Mon → next Sun), **Later this month**, **Later** (beyond end-of-month). Existing capability gate `tt_view_activities` unchanged; existing entry points (dashboard widgets, team detail links) continue working at the same URL. **Page header CTA**: + New activity moves into the page header's actions slot (routed through `WizardEntryPoint::urlFor( 'new-activity' )`); no separate CTA row clutters the list. **Mobile-first CSS** rewrite per CLAUDE.md §2 — base styles target 360px viewport, 480px / 768px / 1100px breakpoints scale up. All interactive targets ≥ 48px tall, 8px gap between adjacent cards via `margin-bottom: -1px` border collapse. Tap targets honour `touch-action: manipulation`; `:active` state gives feedback inside 100ms. Minor bump — new surface behaviour visible to every coach. (closes #973) =

= 4.6.0 — Blueprint editor clean rebuild from the in-tree prototype (closes #972, supersedes the partial v4.4.0 implementation). The v4.4.0 ship landed the depth-chart editor markup but the picker was wired against an unhydrated DOM root (a hidden `.tt-bp-editor` legacy anchor sat alongside the new `.tt-bpe-editor`), so clicking a player did nothing on the live site. Rather than chase the bug, this ship replaces the editor surface end-to-end with a faithful port of `.local-mockups/blueprint-editor/index.html`. **Layout**: two-column at >= 820px (220px roster sidebar + flex pitch column); single column below. Toolbar above the layout carries the team display (read-only), formation dropdown populated from `tt_formation_templates`, a Clear all slots button and a save-state hint. **Pitch**: each formation slot renders as a positioned card with a numbered circle (slot number + position abbreviation) and a three-row rounded stack below it; each row is a tier slot (1 / 2 / 3) with a coloured pill (teal / amber / grey) on the left and the player name (or "—") on the right. **Picker**: clicking a tier slot opens an anchored dropdown with a search input + filterable list; "Clear this slot" affordance appears when the slot is filled. **Drag-drop**: roster rows drag onto tier slots; dropping replaces the previous occupant without pulling them from other slots. **Same player in multiple slots / tiers is allowed** — the roster sidebar's xN badge counts placements in the current formation only. **Formation switch** preserves assignments by slot_label; slots dropped from the previous formation are hidden but data is preserved (round-trip restores). **Add guest / cross-team / custom**: inline 3-tab form (Other team / Guest / Custom); cross-team picks persist on placement as `ref_kind=player`, guest as `ref_kind=guest`, custom as `ref_kind=custom`. **Save / Save As / Hide chemistry / status buttons**: the legacy `frontend-team-blueprint.js` Save / Save As / Hide-chem / status-button handlers are lifted into the new editor JS; the legacy `.js` + `.css` are deleted entirely. **Asset cleanup**: `assets/js/frontend-team-blueprint.js` (687 lines) and `assets/css/frontend-team-blueprint.css` (499 lines) are removed; the still-needed CSS rules (chemistry headline, status row, hide-chem toggle, heatmap, tabs) are absorbed into `assets/css/frontend-blueprint-editor.css`. The dead `renderRosterChips` / `renderRosterChip` / `overlaySlotDropTargets` / `renderDepthChart` / `loadTrialPlayers` helpers in `FrontendTeamBlueprintsView.php` are deleted. The legacy `TT_BLUEPRINT` localised payload is gone; only `TT_BLUEPRINT_EDITOR` remains. **Untouched**: the read-only share link view (`tt_view=team-blueprint-share`), the squad-plan heatmap (`renderHeatmapPitch`), the schema (`tt_team_blueprint_assignments` with `ref_kind`) and the REST endpoints (`PUT /blueprints/{id}/assignment(s)`, `POST /blueprints/{id}/clone`, `PUT /blueprints/{id}/status`). Capability gate stays on `tt_manage_team_chemistry`. Mobile-first per CLAUDE.md §2; the editor renders at 360px without horizontal scroll. Minor bump — behaviour-replacement epic. (closes #972) =

= 4.5.1 — Match prep roster query + wizard activity_id round-trip (#940 / #965 follow-up). Two related defects on the match-prep flow, one architectural class. **(1)** `AvailabilityStep::rosterForActivity()` and `FrontendMatchPrepView::loadTeamRosterById()` both queried a `tt_team_players` junction table that doesn't exist in the schema — `tt_players.team_id` is the canonical FK (verified across 8+ call sites in `Infrastructure/Stats`, `Infrastructure/Security`, `Infrastructure/REST`, etc.). The query returned an empty roster regardless of how many players the team has, so the wizard fell into the "No players on this team yet" early-return branch (pilot symptom on a U14 with a full roster). Same defect class in the main `?tt_view=match-prep` form's roster lookup. Fix: replace the junction join with a direct `SELECT FROM tt_players WHERE team_id = ? AND club_id = ? AND archived_at IS NULL ORDER BY last_name, first_name`. **(2)** Because the wizard's empty-roster branch `return`s before emitting the hidden `<input name="activity_id">`, every subsequent form POST landed at `AvailabilityStep::validate()` with `$post['activity_id']` missing. The wizard also lacked an `initialState()` seed hook, so the URL's `?activity_id=N` was never persisted to wizard state. Result: clicking Create on a wizard with the empty-roster fallback yielded a "Missing activity_id" error — exactly the pilot symptom. Fix: `MatchPrepWizard` now implements `WizardInterface::initialState()` mirroring the mark-attendance pattern; `FrontendWizardView::render()` calls it on first hit and stows `activity_id` in state. After this fix the wizard is resilient even if a future regression takes the empty-roster branch again — the activity_id survives the round-trip. **Why this regressed now**: the #940 admin-post.php switch made the round-trip dependent on `state`, not `$_GET`, because the wizard's POST is processed at admin-post.php (which doesn't carry the original entry URL's query string). Pre-#940 the form POSTed to the dashboard URL itself, so `$_GET['activity_id']` survived. The roster-table bug is older and was masked by the working `$_GET` fallback. Patch bump — bug fix completing the #940 admin-post switch's coverage of the match-prep wizard. (closes follow-up to #940) =
