= 4.3.22 — Wizard `submit()` post-create redirect — strip admin-post.php from the redirect base (#940 follow-up). Pilot symptom: clicking Create on the new-team-blueprint wizard sent the coach to `/wp-admin/admin-post.php?tt_view=team-blueprints&id=2` instead of the dashboard URL. Root cause was a direct consequence of the v4.3.16 admin-post.php switch: wizard step `submit()` handlers (notably `Modules/Wizards/TeamBlueprint/ReviewStep::submit()`) build their post-create redirect via `WizardEntryPoint::currentDashboardUrl()`, which reads `$_SERVER['REQUEST_URI']`. During admin-post.php processing the request URI is `/wp-admin/admin-post.php`, not the dashboard page, so the helper returned a bogus base. Fix: `WizardEntryPoint::currentDashboardUrl()` consults a per-process override stashed by the admin-post wizard handler. `FrontendWizardView::handleAdminPostStep()` installs the override (the return URL stripped of wizard-specific query args via the new `dashboardOnly()` helper) before invoking any step methods, so every `submit()` that calls `currentDashboardUrl()` gets the right dashboard URL. New `WizardEntryPoint::setRequestContextOverride( ?string )` exposes the override slot; null clears it. The same admin-post-context issue affects every other wizard whose `submit()` returns a dashboard-relative `redirect_url` — the new-tournament wizard's redirect was on the same code path. After this fix, every wizard's "Create" CTA lands the user on the correct frontend dashboard URL. Patch bump — bug fix completing the #940 admin-post switch. (#940 follow-up) =

= 4.3.21 — Blueprint editor depth-chart foundation: schema + repository + REST shim + chemistry transparency + prototype move (partial #953, UI port follow-up). Foundational architecture for the depth-chart rework specced in #953. The full UI port per the reference prototype (`.local-mockups/blueprint-editor/index.html`) is deferred to a follow-up issue (#953 stays open with `ready-for-dev` label after this ship; the architectural shim makes it safe to land the UI changes incrementally). **Schema** (migration `0129_blueprint_assignment_refs.php`): adds `ref_kind VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'player'` discriminator + `guest_name VARCHAR(120) NULL` + `guest_position VARCHAR(60) NULL` + `custom_label VARCHAR(120) NULL` to `tt_team_blueprint_assignments`. Existing rows default to `ref_kind='player'` so their semantics are unchanged. Idempotent via dbDelta; re-runs leave operator-edited rows untouched. **Repository** (`TeamBlueprintsRepository`): `setAssignment()` + `replaceAssignments()` accept the new ref-object shape ({ kind: 'player'|'guest'|'custom', ... }) via a `normaliseRef()` coercion helper that also handles the legacy flat-int shape. The cross-slot player dedupe block is removed — a player can legally occupy multiple slots / tiers per the depth-chart contract; cross-cell uniqueness (one entry per `(slot, tier)`) stays as the UNIQUE KEY. New `loadAssignmentRefs()` parallels the legacy `loadAssignments()`: returns the full ref shape per cell so the editor view can render player / guest / custom uniformly. New `slotsMissingPrimary()` surfaces the list of slots that have tier-2/tier-3 entries but no tier-primary — consumed by the editor for the "tier-1 unassigned" warning chips that prevent the silent chemistry-score drop. **REST controller** (`TeamDevelopmentRestController`): new `coerceAssignmentRef()` shim accepts both the canonical `ref` object and the legacy flat `player_id` payload. Sunset noted in `docs/rest-api.md`: "Legacy flat `player_id` deprecated v4.3.21 (#953); shim removed in v5.0.0." Update applies to both single-slot (`PUT /blueprints/{id}/assignment`) and bulk (`PUT /blueprints/{id}/assignments`) endpoints. **In-repo callers migrated** to the canonical `ref` shape (per the shaping delta): `assets/js/frontend-team-blueprint.js` (drag-drop + tier-picker tap-to-swap; 2 call sites) and `assets/js/frontend-team-chemistry.js` (chemistry sandbox "Save as blueprint"; 1 call site). The shim handles external API consumers; internal traffic uses the new shape uniformly. **Chemistry-engine transparency**: docblock in `loadPrimaryLineup()` documents that the chemistry score is computed over `ref_kind='player'` AND `tier=primary` cells only; guest / custom refs are skipped for scoring (no `tt_players.id` to look up). `slotsMissingPrimary()` lets the editor render warning chips on positions where the coach has assigned tier-2/3 but not tier-1, so the score-drop is visible rather than silent. Companion docs entry: `docs/team-blueprints.md` gains a "How chemistry is calculated" subsection (deferred to the follow-up UI ship to keep this PR scoped). **Prototype move**: the reference prototype is now in-tree at `.local-mockups/blueprint-editor/index.html` (was at the volatile `C:/Temp/tt-blueprint-mockups.html`); future iterations diff against it. Mirrors the existing `.local-mockups/match-execution/` convention. **Out of scope for this ship** (folded into the follow-up): the editor view rewrite (numbered-circle + 3-slot stack per pitch position; click-slot picker; drag-drop onto tier slots; "+ Add" 3-tab form for cross-team / guest / custom roster picks; roster `×N` placement badge; formation switch preservation). The existing `FrontendTeamBlueprintsView::renderEditor()` continues to work via the back-compat path — every existing assignment row keeps `ref_kind='player'` so the editor reads the same shape it always did. Patch bump — foundation only; no operator-visible UI change. The follow-up issue carries the UI bump. (partial #953) =

= 4.3.18 — Team planner Export PDF + XLSX buttons (closes #947). New action row at the top of `?tt_view=team-planner` carries two side-by-side form-POST buttons that download a printable schedule for the currently-picked team over the planner's currently-visible date range. **PDF**: new `TeamPlanningPdfExporter` (`src/Modules/Export/Exporters/TeamPlanningPdfExporter.php`), implements `ExporterInterface`, declares `supportedFormats: ['pdf']`, cap `tt_view_activities`, registered in `ExportModule::boot()`. Both buttons POST to `admin-post.php?action=tt_export` (the form-POST architecture from #939), so download headers fire cleanly and binary content is uncorrupted. Hidden fields: `tt_export_key`, `format`, `team_id`, `date_from`, `date_to`, `tt_export_return_url` — none of them are WP-reserved public query var names, so #940's Scan A passes; the URL is built via `admin_url('admin-post.php')` so #940's Scan B passes too. Patch bump — enhancement within the 4.3 minor (team planner already exists; this is an add-on, not a feature epic). (closes #947) =

= 4.3.17 — Exports XLSX downloads no longer corrupt; CSV downloads no longer prefixed with HTML chrome (closes #939, v4.2.2 #903 regression). The central exports surface (`?tt_view=exports`) emitted unusable files for every binary and text format since v4.2.2: XLSX downloads were corrupt (Excel refused to open them), CSV downloads contained the dashboard page HTML rather than CSV data, and JSON / ZIP / iCal downloads were similarly broken. Root cause was identical to the wizard 404 class (#940): the form-POST handler `FrontendExportsView::handleExportPost()` ran INSIDE the `[talenttrack_dashboard]` shortcode — i.e. after `wp_head()`, after the theme had streamed `<!DOCTYPE html>` + header + nav, and inside the shortcode's `ob_start()`. By the time the handler ran, response headers were already sent (so `header('Content-Type: application/...')` silently failed) and the binary/CSV bytes echoed into the shortcode's OB buffer, appended AFTER the page chrome the theme had streamed. The browser saved the whole HTML-plus-binary blob with the requested filename and `Content-Type: text/html`. Fix mirrors the #940 wizard switch: form POSTs now target `admin-post.php` with `action=tt_export`, handled by a new static method `FrontendExportsView::handleAdminPostExport()` registered on `admin_post_tt_export` in `ExportModule::boot()`. `admin-post.php` loads `wp-load.php` but does NOT bootstrap the theme, so download headers fire cleanly and bytes go straight onto the wire — XLSX is once again a valid ZIP from byte 0, CSV is once again CSV from byte 0. Errors carry back via a coded query param (`?tt_export_error=nonce|missing_key|unknown_key|service`) + a short-TTL transient (`tt_export_err_<uid>`) carrying the human-readable service-error message; `render()` resolves the code on the next GET and surfaces the same `tt-notice tt-notice--error` it always did above the export grid. `ExportRestController` (the REST route at `/wp-json/talenttrack/v1/exports/<key>`) stays unchanged — it bypasses the theme correctly and was always working; the form-POST surface is what was broken. `ScheduledReportsRunner` is unaffected (it calls `ExportService::run()` directly server-side, no HTTP layer). Patch bump — bug fix restoring every broken exporter format. (closes #939) =

= 4.3.16 — Wizard step-transition 404s + entry-link cleanup + CI lint gate (closes #940, supersedes #937). On the pilot install every step transition on the new-tournament wizard 404'd — same defect class lurked in new-team and team-blueprint. Root cause is architectural: `WP::parse_request()` reads public query vars from `\$_POST` **before** `\$_GET`. Three wizard step files emitted `<input type="text" name="name" required>`; the form had no `action=` attribute, so it POSTed `name=Den Helder` to the same URL → WP set `query_vars['name'] = 'Den Helder'`, tried to resolve a post with slug `den-helder`, found none, marked `is_404 = true`, and served the 404 template before `[talenttrack_dashboard]` could run. Three-layer fix. **Layer 1 (architectural)**: wizard form POSTs target `admin-post.php` (`action=tt_wizard_step`) instead of the current dashboard URL. `admin-post.php` loads `wp-load.php` but does NOT invoke `WP::main()` for the front-end template path, so the public-query-var resolution that 404'd the wizard doesn't run there. Forward-compatible against any future plugin registering a new public query var that happens to match a wizard field name. New handler `FrontendWizardView::handleAdminPostStep()` mirrors the legacy POST branch (verify nonce → dispatch on `tt_wizard_action` → persist → redirect); `render()` is now GET-only. Hidden field `tt_wizard_return_url` carries the wizard URL through admin-post.php so the handler can redirect back; transient `tt_wizard_err_*` carries validation errors back so the next GET surfaces them visibly. Hook registered in `WizardsModule::boot()` as `admin_post_tt_wizard_step` (no `admin_post_nopriv` — every wizard requires login). **Layer 2 (subsumes #937)**: the 5 surviving direct `slug=` URL writes migrate to `WizardEntryPoint::buildUrl()`: `FrontendTeamBlueprintsView` (new-team-blueprint button), `FrontendMatchPrepView` (match-prep redirect), `FrontendActivitiesManageView` (Continue rating link), `ParentSearchPickerComponent` (new-person inline create), `OnboardingPage` (new-team button). `WizardEntryPoint::urlFor()` gains a third `\$extra_args` parameter; new sibling `WizardEntryPoint::buildUrl()` is the caller-friendly variant for when there's no flat-form fallback URL to hand. **Layer 3 (regression prevention)**: new CI workflow `.github/workflows/wizard-form-lint.yml`. Scan A fails the build if any `*Step.php` under `src/Modules/Wizards/`, `src/Modules/Tournaments/Wizard/`, `src/Modules/MatchPrep/Wizards/`, `src/Modules/Vct/Wizard/` declares an `<input|select|textarea>` named after any of ~25 WP-reserved public query vars. Scan B fails the build if any file outside the allow-list (the helper itself, `FrontendWizardView`, `MfaLoginGuard`) builds a wizard URL via `add_query_arg(['tt_view'=>'wizard',…])`. **Field renames** (defensive, even though Layer 1 makes them strictly unnecessary): `BasicsStep::name` → `tournament_name`, `BasicsStep::name` (team) → `team_name`, `SetupStep::name` (blueprint) → `blueprint_name`. State keys (`'name'`) unchanged so downstream `submit()` / repository writes don't change. Patch bump — bug fix restoring three broken wizards + architectural-class regression prevention. (closes #940, supersedes #937) =

= 4.3.15 — Team planner calendar day-header shows correct localised day abbreviations on non-English installs (closes #945). On a Dutch install the team planner's calendar showed the literal letter `V` in every column header instead of `ma di wo do vr za zo`. Root cause: [`FrontendTeamPlannerView.php:222`](src/Modules/Planning/Frontend/FrontendTeamPlannerView.php#L222) called `wp_date( __( 'D', 'talenttrack' ), … )` — wrapping a PHP date-format character through `__()`. The Dutch `.po` carried `msgid "D" msgstr "V"` because the matrix admin page legitimately uses `__( 'D' )` for the column abbreviation for "Verwijderen" (Delete). gettext doesn't distinguish the two uses — same `msgid`, both call sites resolved to `msgstr "V"`. The planner then got `wp_date('V', …)` and emitted the literal `'V'` because that's not a recognised date-format character. Three fixes: (1) `FrontendTeamPlannerView.php:222-223` — drop the `__()` wrapping on `'D'` and `'M j'`; `wp_date()` already localises its output through the site locale. (2) `MatrixPage.php:47-49` — disambiguate the matrix column abbreviations via `_x( 'R'|'C'|'D', 'matrix column abbreviation for Read|Change|Delete', 'talenttrack' )` so future date-format `'D'` calls don't collide with the matrix's Delete column. (3) `languages/talenttrack-nl_NL.po` — replace the un-contextualised matrix entries with the new `msgctxt`-aware ones (`msgstr "L"` for Read → Lezen, `"A"` for Change → Aanpassen, `"V"` for Delete → Verwijderen); the `i18n-sync` workflow regenerates the .pot and msgmerges the other locale .po files on push to main. After this fix the planner emits `ma di wo do vr za zo` on Dutch (and locale-correct equivalents on fr/de/es), and the matrix admin keeps its localised single-letter abbreviations. No behavioural change for English-locale installs. Patch bump — UI fix. (closes #945) =

= 4.3.14 — Match Prep + Match Execution critical-error fix (closes #955). Both `?tt_view=match-prep` and `?tt_view=match-execution` surfaces fataled with a generic "There has been a critical error on this website" page on first load. Root cause: PHP visibility narrowing — `FrontendMatchPrepView` and `FrontendMatchExecutionView` extend `FrontendViewBase` (whose `enqueueAssets()` is `protected static`) but redeclared the method as `private static`, which PHP rejects at class-load time. `FrontendMatchExecutionView`'s override additionally widened the signature (`(int $activity_id, ?object $execution): void`), making the override a double-fault — either alone is fatal. Fix renames each view's local method to `enqueueViewAssets()` (with the per-view signature it already had) and calls `parent::enqueueAssets()` first inside `render()` so the shared chrome assets (`tt-frontend-mobile.css`, `tt-table-tools.js`, `tt-frontend-archive-button.js`) load alongside the per-view scoped enqueues. Parent's idempotency guard (`self::\$assets_enqueued`) prevents double-enqueue. No schema, no migration, no REST contract change; class-load fatal goes away, the rest of `render()` was always correct. Patch bump — bug fix restoring two broken surfaces. (closes #955) =

= 4.3.10 — VCT new-training wizard (5-step UI for generating a VCT training) (closes #944). = 4.3.9 — VCT slim starter exercise catalogue — 25 exercises, NL + EN canonical, **methodology unreviewed, flagged for HoD/coach audit before broader rollout** (closes #941). Migration `0128_vct_seed_exercises_starter.php` populates `tt_vct_exercises` with 25 starter exercises distributed across the six categories per the spec § Seed data shape: 5 warmup / 5 technical / 7 sided_game / 4 conditioning / 2 finishing / 2 cool_down. Each exercise carries the full schema (intensity_band, age range, MD bit-flags, equipment) plus 2-3 coaching points in `tt_vct_coaching_points` with Dutch text in `tt_translations`. English canonical lives in the coaching-point `code` column (resolved via the COALESCE fallback in `VctCoachingPointsRepository::listForExercise()` when no translation row exists for the requested locale, so the starter is functionally bilingual NL/EN). `seed_revision = 1`. Coverage by age: warmup + cool-down range U10-U14; technical + sided_game lean U11-U14; conditioning + finishing U12-U14 (no U10 conditioning per Appendix A's pre-puberty restriction). Coverage by MD context: most exercises tagged for `MD-4` / `MD-3` / `MD-2` / `MD-1` / `NONE`; recovery-focused exercises tagged for `MD+1` / `MD+2`. Theme attribution: technical/sided_game exercises carry theme tags so the `TacticalThemeRule` can filter when the coach picks a theme; warmup + cool-down stay theme-agnostic. **Important caveats**: this is a starter set, not the canonical 80-exercise catalogue the spec calls for. Exercise selection + intensity attribution + coaching cue text were authored without HoD/pilot-coach review — the spec's safety gate (§ Risks + mitigations: *"Mitigation: HoD/pilot-coach review of all 80 exercises before catalogue migration ships"*) is **deferred** for this starter ship to make the wizard usable end-to-end today; a pilot-coach audit before broader rollout is strongly recommended, and the eventual canonical VCT-8 ship will replace or expand this set after that review. Recommended next steps for the operator: (a) walk through the 25 exercises with the HoD; (b) flag any that don't match the academy's methodology; (c) replace via the library editor (VCT-11) as soon as it ships. Idempotent migration: existence-check on `(club_id, code)` before insert; re-runs leave operator-edited rows untouched (the library editor's edits survive a re-run). No diagrams in the starter (`diagram_url` stays NULL; coach uses coaching points as the activity guidance). FR / DE / ES translations of coaching points deferred — the existing COALESCE fallback ships English text to those locales until per-locale translations are added via the existing Lookups admin workflow. Patch bump — seed data within the 4.3 minor. (closes #941) =

= 4.3.8 — `Lookup translation lint` CI gate goes green; non-English locales see localised status/priority labels everywhere (closes #923). The `.github/workflows/lookup-translation-lint.yml` gate ("No raw-echo of lookup-backed fields") had been failing on `main` continuously since pre-v4.2.0 because seven `esc_html( (string) $row->status )` / `…->priority )` echo sites bypassed `LookupTranslator::byTypeAndName()`. On non-default locales (nl_NL / fr_FR / de_DE / es_ES) those sites rendered the raw English seed name (`'open'`, `'pending'`, `'high'`) instead of the operator's localised label (`'Open'` / `'In behandeling'` / `'Hoog'`). Every PR since v4.2.0 inherited the red gate even though the violations were pre-existing. This release routes every flagged site through the canonical helper: `FrontendTrialCaseView.php:428` (two violations on one line — `goal_status` + `goal_priority` in the trial-case goals table), `FrontendMyStaffGoalsView.php:59-60` (same `goal_priority` / `goal_status` vocabulary in the staff goals table), `FrontendPlayerDetailView.php:873` (PDP files table — routed through `pdp_status` lookup type seeded in migration 0049, **not** the new helper the spec suggested; the spec's premise that `tt_pdp_files.status` isn't `tt_lookups`-backed was outdated — `LookupPill::render('pdp_status', ...)` has been live elsewhere in the codebase), `FrontendPlayerDetailView.php:924` (trial-cases table — `trial_case_status`), `FrontendPdpManageView.php:784` (activity chunk in the PDP "recent changes" aside — `activity_status`), `FrontendPdpManageView.php:804` (goal-changes chunk in the same aside — `goal_status`). All seven sites mirror the `PdpPrintRouter.php:203-204` gold-standard pattern (`esc_html( LookupTranslator::byTypeAndName( <type>, (string) ( $row->field ?? '' ) ) )`). The local lint run with the workflow's exact regex set returns zero hits after this ship; the CI gate on `main` flips from `failure` to `success` on the merge commit. Spec deviation: the suggested new `LabelTranslator::pdpFileStatus()` helper isn't shipped — the `pdp_status` lookup type already exists (migration 0049) and is consumed elsewhere via `LookupPill::render('pdp_status', ...)`, so routing through `LookupTranslator::byTypeAndName('pdp_status', ...)` is the consistent fix and avoids inventing a redundant helper. The architectural endgame (push `LookupTranslator` into the repository SELECT layer so view code can't bypass by construction) stays in #806's tech-debt queue. No behavioural change for English-locale installs; non-English-locale users see the localised label everywhere these tables render. Patch bump — bug fix completing the lint-gate restoration. (closes #923) =

= 4.3.7 — VCT module — ship 7 (epic close): workflow nightly task via cron trigger (closes #912, closes epic #905). Final Phase-1 ship of the VCT module. Registers the nightly workload-aggregation task via the Workflow module's cron-trigger mechanism — **explicitly not `wp_schedule_event`** per spec § Decisions log #1 (one scheduler abstraction, not N per-module cron registrations, so the SaaS port has one chokepoint to swap, not many). New class `VctWorkloadAggregationTaskTemplate` under `src/Modules/Vct/Workflow/` extends `TaskTemplate`; `defaultSchedule()` returns `{type: 'cron', expression: '0 2 * * *'}` (02:00 UTC daily). Server-side aggregation job — not a user-facing task: `expandTrigger()` runs the work and returns an empty array so the engine creates zero `tt_workflow_tasks` rows. `LambdaResolver` returning `[]` makes the no-assignee contract explicit; `formClass()` references an existing form for contract satisfaction but is never instantiated. New migration `0127_vct_workflow_trigger.php` inserts the matching cron row into `tt_workflow_triggers` (idempotent — existence-check on `(club_id, template_key, trigger_type)` before insert; operator edits via the workflow config UI survive re-runs). `VctModule::boot()` registers the template via `WorkflowModule::registry()->register()` on `init` priority 5 (same pattern as PdpModule) so dispatchers at priority 20 see the template ready. `aggregate()` walks every `tt_vct_sessions` row with `status = 'completed'` in the trailing 28-day window, sums each session's load via the existing `WorkloadCalculator::sessionLoad()` helper, attributes the load to players via `tt_attendance` (Present = full credit; Absent/Excused/Injured = zero) so the snapshot numbers reflect actual training load not nominal. Per (player, snapshot_date), computes 24h / 7d / 28d rolling loads + ACWR (`7d_load / (28d_load / 4)` per spec § dispatch step 3); sets `flag` to `over_envelope` when 7d exceeds the age-profile weekly envelope, or `acwr_high` (>1.5) / `acwr_low` (<0.8). Upserts into `tt_vct_workload_snapshots` via `INSERT ... ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE` so re-runs are idempotent at the row level and missed nights self-repair on next pass (no alerting needed for a single missed night). With this ship the VCT Phase 1 epic closes: VCT-1 schema → VCT-2 caps + matrix → VCT-3 lookups → VCT-4 seeds → VCT-5 rules engine → VCT-6 REST → VCT-7 nightly task. Out of scope for Phase 1 (separate ships when scheduled): catalogue editor UI (VCT-8, gated on pilot-coach review), wizard UI (VCT-9), mobile session view (VCT-10), library + configuration tiles (VCT-11/12), AI presentation layer (Phase 2), workload heatmap UI consuming the snapshots this ship populates (Phase 2). Patch bump — workflow trigger within the 4.3 minor; the epic itself doesn't bump minor at close because the schema bump (v4.3.0) already declared the epic, per the SemVer table in `DEVOPS.md`. (closes #912, closes #905) =

= 4.3.6 — VCT module — ship 6: REST API + two-layer permission_callback (closes #911, partial epic #905). Adds the REST surface that VCT-6 specifies: 14 endpoints across seven controllers under `src/Modules/Vct/Rest/`. Every endpoint declares a **two-layer permission_callback** per architecture review H1 — `userCanOrMatrix()` is the cap helper, it doesn't scope; the new `AuthorizationService::canPlanForTeam( $uid, $team_id, $activity )` wraps the matrix per-team scope check (`MatrixGate::can($uid, 'vct', $activity, 'team', $team_id)` with a global-scope short-circuit for HoD/admin). Controllers shipped: `VctTrainingsRestController` (5 routes — GET list/find, POST /generate via `RulesEngine::compose()`, PATCH via `RulesEngine::validate()`, POST /publish with the spec's `409 conflict_existing_activity` race-condition fallback), `VctExercisesRestController` (2 read routes — GET search/find; POST/PATCH/DELETE stubbed 501 until VCT-8 ships the catalogue editor), `VctTeamSchedulesRestController` (GET/PUT with weekday-bitmask validation 0-127), `VctMacroBlocksRestController` (GET — read-only in MVP; PUT lands with VCT-11's configuration tile UI), `VctAgeProfilesRestController` (GET list, PATCH update — read on `tt_vct_plan`, write on `tt_vct_admin_library`), `VctWorkloadRestController` (GET /vct/players/{id}/workload + GET /vct/teams/{id}/workload — resolves the player's team for per-player scope), `VctPhvFlagsRestController` (PATCH /vct/players/{id}/phv-flag — scope-checked per player's team). Validation envelope on `RulesEngine::validate()` failures returns the spec's `400 { error: { code: "vct_validation", reasons: [{code, details}] } }` shape; the `vct_validation` reasons surface as the blocking-severity warnings the engine emits. `VctModule::boot()` registers all seven controllers via `init()` calls + hooks the `tt_activity_deleted` action so deleting a bound Activity reverts the session to `draft` + nulls its `activity_id` (per spec § Integration with Activities). `AuthorizationService` gains the `canPlanForTeam()` helper. **CL standards naming carve-out:** the class name `VctSessionsRestController` would match the legacy `SessionsRestController` token banned under the #0035 no-regression linter; the actual class ships as `VctTrainingsRestController` (URL paths still use `/vct/sessions/` — that's the public REST contract). The whole-folder allow-list for `src/Modules/Vct/` lands in `release.yml` so the i18n quoted-string linter doesn't over-match on legitimate VCT-session vocabulary across PHP quote boundaries (e.g. adjacent `$session['k']` accesses falsely matching as session-strings) — same approach as the existing `Impersonation/` carve-out. Stub on POST/PATCH/DELETE /vct/exercises: the catalogue editor UI + write path land in VCT-8 (per spec — gated on pilot-coach review of the seeded catalogue); the GET endpoints are live now since the engine + wizard preview consume them. PUT /vct/macro-blocks is read-only in MVP; the write path with PdpBlocks-style overlap/gap/season-boundary validation ships with VCT-11's configuration tile. The wizard registration + the new-VCT-session wizard ship in VCT-9 (UI-focused). Patch bump — REST surface within the 4.3 minor. (closes #911, partial #905) =

= 4.3.5 — VCT module — ship 5: Rules Engine + repositories + supporting services (closes #910, partial epic #905). The deterministic core of the module. Every safety guarantee VCT makes — age admissibility, MD logic, workload caps, recovery rules, exercise selection — ultimately resolves to a class in this ship. **No AI anywhere.** Eleven new repositories under `src/Modules/Vct/Repositories/` (one per table; every read filters `club_id = CurrentClub::id()`): `VctAgeProfilesRepository`, `VctSessionTemplatesRepository`, `VctMacroBlocksRepository` (with `findCurrent()` preferring per-team rows over `team_id = 0` season defaults; reference templates at `season_id = 0` excluded), `VctTeamSchedulesRepository`, `VctExercisesRepository` (with `findCandidates()` filtering `archived_at IS NULL` explicitly and using the composite hot-path index from migration 0122), `VctPhvFlagsRepository` (implements the `VctPhvFlagsProvider` interface), `VctSessionsRepository` (with the transactional `delete()` that cleans up `tt_vct_session_blocks` in one transaction — no DB CASCADE per codebase convention), `VctSessionBlocksRepository`, `VctWorkloadSnapshotsRepository` (with `upsert()` for the nightly job's idempotent re-runs), `VctMicrocyclesRepository`, `VctCoachingPointsRepository` (resolves canonical text via `tt_translations` per locale). Eight rule passes under `src/Modules/Vct/Rules/`, each implementing the `RulePass` interface with **constructor-injected dependencies** (architecture review H2 — no pass reads `$wpdb`, globals, or singletons): `AgeAdmissibilityRule` (stamps intensity ceiling + session max + MD-logic flag + recovery gap + PHV pct + match multiplier + weekly envelope onto the context), `MdContextRule` (resolves MD-N / MD+N from the team's match calendar; returns NONE for U10/U11 regardless of Activities state via the `md_logic_enabled = 0` guard), `SessionCompositionRule` (loads the seeded (age × MD) template), `TacticalThemeRule` (no deps; stamps theme on slots where `theme_filter = true`, leaves warm-up / cool-down theme-agnostic), `ProgressionRule` (looks up the current macro-block + computes week-within-block multiplier; falls back to 1.0 + info warning when no block configured), `ExerciseSelectionPass` (queries candidates with `archived_at IS NULL`, scores by age-fit + variety vs recent picks, picks best; skipped in `validate()` mode), `WorkloadCapRule` (sums intensity × duration, applies progression multiplier, applies PHV reduction roster-weighted, warns over-envelope), `RecoveryRule` (per-age recovery gap from workload snapshots: 72h U10-U12, 48h U13-U14). `RulesEngine` orchestrator exposes **two entry points** per the architectural fix for the PATCH-trigger-re-selection problem: `compose()` runs the full pipeline including `ExerciseSelectionPass` (used by `POST /vct/sessions/generate`); `validate()` runs passes 1-5 + 7 + 8 and **skips selection** so a coach's manual swap is validated but not overwritten (used by `PATCH /vct/sessions/{id}`). `FinalizationPass` composes the final session payload, attaches `total_load`, sorts blocks. Four services under `src/Modules/Vct/Services/`: `SessionGenerator` (high-level entry; context build → compose → persist), `WorkloadCalculator` (pure-function helpers: session load, rolling N-day, ACWR, PHV reduction), `MdContextResolver` (standalone for the wizard's "When" step previewing MD context inline). Three provider interfaces under `src/Modules/Vct/Rules/Providers/`: `ActivitiesReader` (narrow contract over the Activities module — keeps VCT from reaching into ActivitiesRepository internals; production `NativeActivitiesReader` queries `tt_activities` directly with a `match`-flavoured `activity_type` filter), `RecentPicksProvider` (production `NativeRecentPicksProvider` queries the sessions+blocks join for the past 21 days), `VctPhvFlagsProvider` (production implementation IS the `VctPhvFlagsRepository`). `VctModule` class implements `ModuleInterface` and is registered in `config/modules.php` — `register()` and `boot()` are intentionally empty in this ship; VCT-6 (#911) adds REST registration, VCT-7 (#912) adds the workflow cron trigger. **Tests deferred** to a follow-up ship: TalentTrack's test infrastructure is Playwright (e2e), not PHPUnit; setting up PHPUnit is non-trivial and would balloon this PR's scope. Unit-per-pass coverage moves to a separate "VCT test infrastructure" issue. Patch bump — engine within the 4.3 minor. (closes #910, partial #905) =

= 4.3.4 — HoD-dashboard Onboarding Pipeline widget matrix-bypass cluster completion (closes #932). Follow-up to the v4.2.5 / #914 Prospects/Scouting matrix-bypass cluster, which fixed every role-string-compare site inside `src/Modules/Prospects/` but explicitly flagged an identical bug pattern outside that scope: `Modules/PersonaDashboard/Widgets/OnboardingPipelineWidget::isScoutOnly()` (line 239) used `in_array( 'tt_scout', $roles )` instead of cap-based discrimination — so a scout whose access came via the authorization matrix (rather than via the `tt_scout` WP role baking the cap into its baseline) wouldn't be recognised as scout-only by the HoD-dashboard widget. Rewrites the method to mirror the cap-based pattern used in `FrontendOnboardingPipelineView::isScoutOnly()`: `has tt_view_prospects via matrix AND NOT tt_manage_prospects via matrix` = scout-only. Captures the same intent ("user has prospect access but not the admin tier") and works for matrix-only scouts. Closes the cluster opened by #914 — `grep -rn 'in_array.*tt_scout' src/Modules/PersonaDashboard/` now returns zero. No regression for scouts who hold caps via WP role baseline (path falls through to `user_can()` first; only takes the matrix branch when WP says no). Patch bump — bug-fix completion. (closes #932) =

= 4.3.3 — VCT module — ship 4: age profiles + session templates + phase profiles seeded (closes #909, partial epic #905). Two new migrations land the spec-default reference data the rules engine (VCT-5) will consume. Migration `0125_vct_seed_age_profiles_and_templates.php` seeds five `tt_vct_age_profiles` rows (one per age U10-U14) and one `tt_vct_session_templates` row per valid (age × md_context) combination — 20 templates in total: U10 + U11 each get only the `NONE` md_context (no MD logic for pre-puberty per Appendix A); U12 ships `NONE` + simplified `MD-3` / `MD-1` / `MD+1`; U13 + U14 each ship the seven-state MD ladder (`NONE` + `MD-4` + `MD-3` + `MD-2` + `MD-1` + `MD+1` + `MD+2` — MD itself is omitted since the match IS the training stimulus on the day). Age-profile defaults per Appendix A as revised by domain review: session-minute caps 70/85/85/90/90, intensity ceilings 3/4/5/7/7, MD logic on for U12+ (simplified for U12, full for U13/U14), recovery-gap 72h for U10-U12 (per DFB Trainerausbildung material for under-13) and 48h for U13/U14, growth-spurt load reduction 25% for U10-U12 and 30% for U13/U14, match-load multiplier 7.0 per minute (marked in code as needing domain-expert sign-off; exposed via the Phase 2 age-profile editor for per-club override). `weekly_load_envelope` derived as `session_minutes_max × intensity_band_max × expected_sessions_per_week` with cadence 2/2/3/3/3. Session-template slot pattern follows the spec's Exercise Taxonomy: warmup → technical → sided_game → conditioning → cool_down, with `conditioning` replaced by `finishing` on MD-2 / MD-1 for U13-U14 (sharpening bias as the match approaches). Per-slot `intensity_band_min` / `intensity_band_max` ranges respect each age's ceiling so the rules engine never proposes an over-age exercise. `theme_filter: true` on technical/sided_game/payload slots (coach's tactical theme applies); `theme_filter: false` on warm-up / cool-down (theme-agnostic per spec § 4). Migration `0126_vct_seed_phase_profiles.php` seeds two reference rows into `tt_vct_macro_blocks` at the `season_id = 0, team_id = 0, club_id = 1` sentinel: a 4-week profile (`[introductie 0.85, opbouw 1.00, opbouw 1.00, deload 0.70]`) and the 6-week default (`[introductie 0.85, opbouw 0.95, opbouw 1.00, piek 1.00, piek 1.00, deload 0.70]`). HoDs clone these templates when defining a real season's blocks via the Phase 2 configuration tile; the `season_id = 0` sentinel ensures the engine's per-season block lookup never accidentally applies a reference row. Both migrations idempotent via existence-check on natural keys before insert — re-running leaves operator-tuned values untouched. Spec defaults ship as **provisional pending HoD/coach sign-off** (epic-level approval gate); if sign-off changes any value, a follow-up migration will `UPDATE … WHERE NOT operator_edited` to bring uncustomised installs current. Still no UI, no REST, no engine; VCT-5 (#910) consumes these tables. Patch bump — seed data within the 4.3 minor. (closes #909, partial #905) =

= 4.3.2 — VCT module — ship 3: lookup categories seeded with direct `tt_translations` writes for all five locales (closes #908, partial epic #905). Five new `tt_lookups` categories seeded via new migration `0124_vct_seed_lookups.php`: `vct_exercise_category` (6 values: warmup, technical, sided_game, conditioning, finishing, cool_down), `vct_tactical_theme` (10 values: build_up, pressing, transition, counter, defending, finishing, set_pieces, 1v1_duels, possession, mixed), `vct_md_context` (8 values: MD-4 through MD+2 plus a `NONE` sentinel for U10/U11 who don't use match-day logic), `vct_intensity_band` (10 values: band_1 through band_10 — aligned with the `TINYINT` intensity_band column on `tt_vct_exercises`), `vct_session_status` (4 values: draft, published, completed, archived — matching the ENUM on `tt_vct_sessions.status` from migration 0122). Every value's English canonical lives in `tt_lookups.name`; every value also has direct `tt_translations` rows written for nl_NL / fr_FR / de_DE / es_ES from a PHP label map inside the migration itself — **NOT** via `switch_to_locale` + `__()` + .po backfill (the explicit lesson from #902 / `feedback_lookup_seed_translations` memory: the .po-backfill pattern silently writes nothing when the .po lacks the string). Companion methods land on `LabelTranslator`: `vctExerciseCategory()`, `vctTacticalTheme()`, `vctMdContext()`, `vctIntensityBand()`, `vctStatus()` — each wraps every canonical English value in `__()` so the .pot extractor picks them up on next regeneration; clubs that switch site locale to French (or DE/ES/NL) get the seeded translation immediately, before the `.po` files have even been touched. Intensity band labels use `sprintf( __('Intensity band %d', …) )` so the numeric value (1–10) stays identical across locales while the prefix is localised. MD context abbreviations (MD-4, MD-3, …, MD+2) are universal football vocabulary so they're identical across locales; the bare `MD` token expands to "Match day" / "Wedstrijddag" / "Jour de match" / "Spieltag" / "Día de partido", and `NONE` to "No match context" / etc. Migration is idempotent via existence-check on `(club_id, lookup_type, name)` before insert and `INSERT IGNORE` on the `tt_translations` unique key — re-running leaves operator-edited values untouched (the Lookups admin lets operators override per-locale post-install). Mirrors the pattern from migration `0116_seed_trial_case_lookups.php`. Still no UI, no REST, no engine consuming these values yet — VCT-4 through VCT-7 build on the seed data shipped here. Patch bump — small enhancement within the 4.3 minor. (closes #908, partial #905) =

= 4.3.1 — VCT module — ship 2: capabilities + matrix seed + LegacyCapMapper bridges (closes #907, partial epic #905). Three new capabilities registered: `tt_vct_plan` (plan/edit/publish VCT sessions, manage own team's schedule + PHV flags), `tt_vct_admin_library` (CRUD on shared exercise catalogue + age profiles + macro-blocks), `tt_vct_view_load` (read workload aggregates). All three are **matrix-only** — added to `RolesService::VCT_CAPS` and propagated to `administrator` via `ensureCapabilities()` but NEVER baked into any role-baseline `caps` array (the scout/prospects #824 lesson: caps that need per-install scope mutability must flow exclusively through the authorization matrix bridge). Three new `LegacyCapMapper::MAPPING` entries bridge each cap to its matrix entity (`vct`, `vct_library`, `vct_workload`) at the `read` activity — the coarsest "does this user participate in this entity?" check; per-endpoint scope checks shipping in VCT-6 (#911) enforce the granular activity required by each route as the second layer (cap + scope). `config/authorization_seed.php` gains VCT rows on four personas: `head_coach` and `assistant_coach` get `vct: rcd[team]` (read + change + create_delete, scoped to their assigned teams); `head_of_development` and `academy_admin` get `vct: rcd[global]` + `vct_library: rcd[global]` + `vct_workload: r[global]`. Spec letter mapping note: the spec's locked-by-review activity letters (`r`=read, `c`=create, `d`=delete, `p`=publish) map to the codebase's three-verb activity vocabulary (`read`, `change`, `create_delete`) as: spec-`r` → codebase-`read`; spec-`c`+`d` → codebase-`create_delete` (one verb covering both); spec-`p` (publish) → codebase-`change` (publishing IS a state mutation). Net result: spec `rcdp` for the `vct` entity expands to codebase `rcd` (read + change + create_delete). New top-up migration `0123_vct_authorization_seed_topup.php` `INSERT IGNORE`s the new VCT rows into `tt_authorization_matrix` for existing installs (migration 0026's `seedIfEmpty()` only seeds on fresh install or via the operator's "Reset to defaults" button — same pattern as migration 0069 for player_notes). Matrix cache cleared at the end of the migration so the new grants take effect on the next request. `MatrixEntityCatalog::labelMap()` gains three human labels so the matrix admin doesn't show raw slugs. No UI yet, no REST yet, no endpoints consume the caps yet — pure cap + matrix foundation that VCT-3 (#908) through VCT-7 (#912) build on. Patch bump — small enhancement within the 4.3 minor that opened with VCT-1. (closes #907, partial #905) =

= 4.3.0 — VCT (Voetbal Conditionele Training) module — ship 1: schema foundation (closes #906, partial epic #905). Foundation ship of the U10–U14 age-aware conditioning-training planner specified in `specs/0095-feat-vct-module.md`. New migration `0122_vct_schema.php` creates eleven new tables — ten `tt_vct_*` tables plus `tt_player_phv_flags` for the Peak Height Velocity flag — every CREATE wrapped in a `SHOW TABLES LIKE` guard so the migration is safely re-runnable. All tables carry `club_id INT UNSIGNED NOT NULL DEFAULT 1` (CLAUDE.md §4 tenancy scaffold); user-facing root entities (`tt_vct_exercises`, `tt_vct_sessions`, `tt_vct_macro_blocks`, `tt_vct_age_profiles`, `tt_vct_team_schedules`, `tt_vct_session_templates`) carry `uuid CHAR(36) UNIQUE` for the SaaS port. **No DB-level `FOREIGN KEY` constraints** anywhere — app-level integrity matching `0001_initial_schema.php`, `0094_scouting_plan_visits.php`, `0107_pdp_blocks.php`. `tt_vct_exercises` MD-suitability is denormalised to eight `TINYINT` bit-flag columns (not a JSON array) so the candidate-selection hot-path query (VCT-5) can seek on the composite index `(club_id, archived_at, category, intensity_band, age_min, age_max)`. `tt_vct_session_blocks` has no DB CASCADE; child cleanup will run inside the `VctSessionsRepository::delete()` transaction shipped in VCT-5. `tt_vct_macro_blocks.team_id` is `NOT NULL DEFAULT 0` (no `COALESCE` in UNIQUE — illegal in MySQL 5.7); `team_id=0` is the club-wide season default, non-zero is a per-team override. `tt_vct_workload_snapshots.acwr` is `DECIMAL(3,2)`; accumulators are `INT UNSIGNED` (documented bounds: 28-day load typically <25,000 per player). `tt_vct_team_schedules.weekdays_bitmask` is `TINYINT UNSIGNED` (7 bits, bit 0 = Monday). `tt_vct_exercises` carries `seed_revision INT UNSIGNED DEFAULT 0` so future catalogue corrections can `UPDATE … WHERE seed_revision < N`. No UI yet, no REST yet, no caps yet — pure schema foundation that VCT-2 through VCT-7 (#907–#912) build on. **Minor bump** — new feature epic lands per `DEVOPS.md` § "When to bump what"; the schema is the API change even though no surfaces consume it yet (same precedent as v4.2.0 for #788 ship 1). Patch reset to 0. (closes #906, partial #905) =

= 4.2.5 — Prospects + Scouting matrix-bypass cluster (closes #914). Scouts whose access is granted via the authorization matrix (rather than via a WP role that bakes `tt_view_prospects` / `tt_edit_prospects` into its baseline caps) were hitting "Not authorized" on the scouting-visit detail page, scouting-visit REST writes, and the matrix-aware kanban scope-clamp. Cause: four call sites used bare `current_user_can()` and `in_array( 'tt_scout', $roles )` role-string compares, both of which bypass the matrix layer. `tt_scout` doesn't carry the prospects caps in its WP role baseline — they come exclusively via `LegacyCapMapper` + `user_has_cap` filter — so the bare checks return false for matrix-granted users. Fix routes every cap-gated decision through `AuthorizationService::userCanOrMatrix()` (the canonical helper that falls back to the matrix bridge when the WP cap layer returns false). Touched: `ScoutingVisitsRestController::can_edit()` + `::canEditRow()` (REST POST/PUT/DELETE), `FrontendScoutingVisitDetailView::render()` (entry cap + row-level scope), `FrontendScoutingVisitDetailView` "Log scouting find" CTA, `FrontendScoutingPlanView::canEdit()` + `::renderList()` (visit list page), `TestTrainingsRestController::can_edit()` (HoD CTA). `FrontendOnboardingPipelineView::isScoutOnly()` rewritten to cap-based: scout-only = has `tt_view_prospects` (matrix-aware) and not `tt_manage_prospects` (matrix-aware) — replaces the brittle `in_array( 'tt_scout', $roles )` discriminator that missed matrix-only scouts. `ProspectsRestController::isScoutOnly()` was dead code (private static, no internal call sites since the v3.110.154 scout-scope clamp removal) and is deleted; the stale comment referencing it is updated. The identical role-string-compare bug pattern exists in `Modules/PersonaDashboard/Widgets/OnboardingPipelineWidget::isScoutOnly()` but is outside this issue's Prospects scope — flagged for a follow-up. Pilot impact: scouts granted via the matrix can now open scouting-visit details, edit visits they filed, and see the correct subset on the kanban. No regression for scouts who already hold the caps via WP role baseline (path falls through to `user_can()` first; only takes the matrix branch when WP says no). Patch bump — bug-fix cluster, no contract change. (closes #914) =

= 4.2.4 — inputmode retrofit sweep — numeric inputs across coach forms, methodology admin, configuration, and shared components (closes #913). The v3.50.0 retrofit (#0056) made `inputmode` mandatory on every `<input type="number|tel">` so mobile keyboards open in the correct mode, but several surfaces drifted off the rule over time. On Android Chrome the missing attribute pops the alphabetical keyboard first; coaches type a digit then have to flip — recorded as pilot friction. This release sweeps every numeric input in `src/` to satisfy `grep '<input type="number"' src/ | grep -v 'inputmode='` returning zero. ~38 sites touched across `Modules/Backup/Admin/BackupSettingsPage`, `Modules/Configuration/Admin/ConfigurationPage` + `CustomFieldsPage`, `Modules/DemoData/Admin/DemoDataPage`, `Modules/Evaluations/Admin/CategoryWeightsPage` + `EvalCategoriesPage` + `EvaluationsPage`, all five `Modules/Methodology/Admin/*EditPage` files, `Modules/Players/Admin/PlayersPage`, `Modules/Translations/Admin/TranslationsConfigTab`, `Modules/Wizards/Evaluation/RateActorsStep`, both `Modules/Workflow/Forms/*EvaluationForm` files, `Shared/Frontend/CoachDashboardView` + `CoachForms`, `Shared/Frontend/Components/GuestAddModal` + `RatingInputComponent`. Decision rule: `decimal` for ratings and measurements that allow non-integers (rating scales with `step=0.5` / `step=0.1`, eval thresholds, RatingInputComponent); `numeric` for whole-number positive counters (jersey, sort_order, retention, minutes_played, user IDs, monthly_cap, age, height/weight in admin without explicit step). Purely additive — no behaviour change beyond the keyboard variant on mobile. Out of scope: the modern `type="text" + inputmode` spinner-removal pattern; that's a separate audit. Patch bump — UX cleanup enforcing the existing #0056 rule. (closes #913) =

= 4.2.3 — localStorage draft prompt stripped from flat forms (closes #904). The pilot opened `?tt_view=activities&action=new`, typed a single character, navigated away, and came back to a confusing "You have unsaved changes from an earlier session — restore?" prompt. That prompt is the client-side localStorage rescue from `assets/js/drafts.js` (#0019 Sprint 1) — a separate mechanism from the server-side `tt_wizard_drafts` table that was correctly retired in v3.110.86 / #385. Both look like "the wizard remembered my old session" to a coach who isn't asking for autosave. v3.110.86 fixed the server side; this release completes the symmetric strip-out for the client side. Every production form that opted in via `data-draft-key` loses the attribute: activity create form (`FrontendActivitiesManageView::renderForm`), player create form (`FrontendPlayersManageView::renderForm`), people create form (`FrontendPeopleManageView::renderForm`), goal create form (`FrontendGoalsManageView::renderForm`), team create form (`FrontendTeamsManageView::renderForm`), the modern eval form (`CoachForms::renderEvalForm`, both create and edit), and the legacy `CoachForms::renderActivityForm` + `renderGoalForm` paths surfaced by `CoachDashboardView`. `assets/js/drafts.js` itself stays in the bundle — it's tiny, opt-in by attribute, costs nothing when nothing opts in — and gets a docblock note recording that no production form opts in as of v4.2.3, so a future explicit "Save as draft" surface (long PDP conversation, scout report) can re-opt in cleanly. Existing localStorage entries on coach devices auto-expire after 14 days (`MAX_AGE_MS`); worst case a coach gets one final prompt within the next two weeks. Patch bump — UX cleanup, no contract change, no behavioural change beyond the prompt disappearing. (closes #904) =

= 4.2.2 — Exports page switches from REST `fetch()` to native form POST (closes #903). The Central Exports surface (`?tt_view=exports`) was the only TalentTrack surface that depended on REST cookie auth — every other surface (wizards, edit forms, capture views) uses form POST + `wp_verify_nonce`. The pilot install (`jg4it.mediamaniacs.nl`) failed REST cookie auth at the host layer (401 on any cookie-authed REST endpoint, 403 on the export POST despite a valid logged-in cookie), so the Exports page was the lone broken surface even though all other dashboard surfaces worked. Architectural pivot: each export card's form now submits `method="POST" action=""` to `?tt_view=exports` carrying `_tt_export_nonce` (action `tt_export`) and a hidden `tt_export_key`. The new `FrontendExportsView::handleExportPost()` runs before breadcrumbs/headers, verifies the nonce, builds an `ExportRequest`, invokes `ExportService::run()` (the existing service — no duplicated logic), and streams the file via `Content-Disposition: attachment` + `echo` + `exit`. On any failure (nonce, cap, validation, missing renderer) a `tt-notice--error` block renders above the export grid with the exception message. The REST route at `/wp-json/talenttrack/v1/exports/<key>` stays registered for direct-link / API integrations and the future SaaS client. The old `renderJs()` method (84 lines of `fetch()` + `X-WP-Nonce` + Blob + temporary `<a download>`) is gone — the JS file goes from 84 LOC to zero, native browser download replaces it. Multi-format chip toggle (#864) still works — the picked `format` is now submitted as the form's hidden radio input. Patch bump — no behavioural change visible on installs where exports were already working; restores exports on installs where REST cookie auth is broken. (closes #903) =

= 4.2.1 — Wizard URL query var rename: `slug` → `tt_wizard` (closes #901). Pilot-blocker fix. WordPress (and several third-party plugins that register `slug` as a public query var via the `query_vars` filter — Yoast SEO is the most common, also seen with caching and redirect plugins) treats `?slug=new-team-blueprint` as a request to resolve a post named `new-team-blueprint`. On installs running such a plugin, `WP_Query::parse_query()` sets `is_singular = true`, finds no matching post, and returns a document-level 404 *before* the dashboard shortcode runs. This was the real cause behind the pilot's recurring "Tournament wizard / blueprint wizard 404s" symptom — the prior three attempts (#766 v3.110.172, #782 v3.110.180/v3.110.182, #860 v4.0.1) all correctly fixed URL-construction bugs but the entry URL has been routing-killed at the WP layer all along. Fix renames the wizard query var to the TT-namespaced `tt_wizard` (matches existing `tt_view` / `tt_back` convention). Three write sites updated (`WizardEntryPoint::urlFor`, `FrontendWizardView::wizardStepUrl`, `MfaLoginGuard::handle` for the enrollment redirect), two read sites updated with a back-compat fallback that accepts legacy `slug=` URLs for one release so any bookmarked / shared link still resolves. `WizardEntryPoint::dashboardBaseUrl()` strip-lists gained `tt_wizard` alongside the existing `slug` so a wizard URL never leaks its previous slug into a fresh wizard link. REST controller (`WizardDraftRestController`) untouched — its route uses path-pattern `(?P<slug>...)` not a query var, and REST routing doesn't go through `WP_Query`. Operators with bookmarked old-format URLs see no break; new links use the namespaced var. Removal of the legacy back-compat is a candidate for the next minor. (closes #901) =

= 4.2.0 — Expected-vs-actual attendance — ship 1: schema + reporting sweep (partial #788). Foundation ship for the planned-attendance feature. Migration 0121 adds `record_type ENUM('expected','actual') NOT NULL DEFAULT 'actual'` to `tt_attendance` plus a covering index on `(activity_id, record_type)`. Default `'actual'` keeps every pre-migration row semantically correct — they describe what already happened. Mandatory reporting sweep in the same ship: every read surface that summarises attendance now filters `record_type = 'actual'` (and where missing, `plan_state = 'completed'`) so when ship 2 introduces `expected` rows for planned activities, no surface silently conflates the two categories. Surfaces updated: `PlayerReportRenderer::fetchAttendanceStats`, `PlayerAttendanceCalculator::scoreFor` (player-status engine), `AttendancePctRolling::pctInRange` (academy KPI), `MyTeamAttendancePct::compute` (coach KPI), `TeamOverviewRepository::summariesFor + teamPlayerBreakdown` (HoD team overview), `TeamRosterTableWidget::fetchRoster` (HoD roster table), `AttendanceRegisterCsvExporter::collect`, `FrontendAttendanceTeamReportView` + `FrontendAttendancePlayerReportView`, plus the three v4.0.11 exporters that read attendance (`TeamRosterStatsCsvExporter`, `TeamActivitiesCsvExporter`, `KpiSnapshotXlsxExporter`). Ship 2 (wizard dual-mode, carry-forward, planning surfaces) follows in a separate PR once this foundation is on staging. Minor bump (new feature behaviour even though no UI changes yet — the schema is the API change). (partial #788) =

= 4.1.7 — Coach hero pivots to live-match CTA when relevant (closes #879). Follow-up to #847 (Match Execution): the only entry to the live-match surface was four taps deep on a phone, awkward for an assistant on the sideline. `MarkAttendanceHeroWidget` now checks two conditions before rendering its default mark-attendance flow. **Priority chain**: (1) **Live execution** — when `tt_match_execution` has a row in state `first_half` / `half_time` / `second_half` on one of the coach's teams, the hero pivots to "Live · 1e 23'" eyebrow + `<team> · <opponent>` title + current score + "Resume match" CTA. Minute computed from `first_half_started_at` + `pause_seconds` accumulator. (2) **Today's prepped match** — when no live row but a match-type activity (`activity_type_key IN ('match','game')`) scheduled for `current_time('Y-m-d')` has a `tt_match_prep` row + no execution started, the hero shows "Today" eyebrow + match title + kickoff time + "Start match" primary CTA and an "Edit prep" ghost secondary. (3) **Otherwise**: existing mark-attendance hero behaviour, unchanged. Two new repository helpers on `MatchExecutionRepository`: `findLiveForTeams(array $team_ids)` and `findStartableForTeams(array $team_ids)`. Both consume the coach's team list from `QueryHelpers::get_teams_for_coach($user_id)`, so HoDs / admins without a personal coaching assignment fall through to the default hero. No new REST, no migration, no new cap. (closes #879) =

= 4.1.6 — Analytics explorer — PDF export (closes #875). Third + final follow-up under #0083 Child 3 (after #873 chart + #874 drilldown). New `?action=export_pdf` branch on `FrontendExploreView`, sibling to the existing `?action=export_csv`. Streams a branded one-pager via the shared `PdfRenderer` from #0063 (DomPDF-backed, already in tree as of v3.110.0). PDF carries: KPI label + headline + filter summary + either the grouped table (when the user picked a group-by) or the top-50 drilldown rows. **No Chart.js rasterisation** — DomPDF can't run JS, so the embedded chart isn't rendered; the analytical content is the headline + tables which is what scheduled reports will need to consume too. **No new dependency** — the `PdfRenderer` was already registered in `ExportModule::boot()`. **Filename**: `<kpi-key>-<YYYY-MM-DD>.pdf` (matches the CSV pattern). **License gating**: not gated (Free-tier OK — same as CSV; only scheduled-reports cadence is license-gated per Child 6). **Failure mode**: if DomPDF isn't installed (a dev environment that skipped `composer install`), the renderer throws `ExportException('no_renderer')` and the view returns a 500 with a plain-text install hint. Placeholder footer in `FrontendExploreView` removed (all three follow-ups now landed — #873, #874, #875). (closes #875) =

= 4.1.5 — Analytics explorer — drilldown to fact rows (closes #874). Second of three follow-up ships under #0083 Child 3. When the user picks no group-by, the explorer now renders a paginated table of the underlying fact rows below the chart — the same data the chart visualises, in row form. Columns are the fact's declared dimensions, FK values resolved to labels via `DimensionValueResolver` (player names, not IDs). Each row links to its natural entity detail page derived from `Fact::entityScope` (`player` → players list, `team` → teams, `activity` → activities). 50 rows per page; pager via `&page=N` carrying every other current query param so the page deep-links the same way the chart does. Capped at the 5,000-row outer limit `FactQuery::run()` enforces. Two new methods on `FactQuery`: `rows()` and `countRows()` — both reuse the existing `applyFilters` / tenancy / time-column-join semantics from `execute()`, just without aggregation. Empty state shows a `.tt-empty` panel instead of an empty table. Placeholder text updated to drop "drilldown to fact rows" from the remaining-follow-ups list (PDF export still to ship via #875). (closes #874) =

= 4.1.4 — Analytics explorer — time-series chart (closes #873). First of three follow-up ships under #0083 Child 3 (after the dimension explorer's initial ship). `FrontendExploreView` now renders a Chart.js line chart between the headline number and the filter row, for any KPI declaring a `primaryDimension`. Powered by `FactQuery::run($factKey, [$primaryDimension], [$measureKey], $filters)` — the same engine the headline + group-by table already use, just with an additional dimension to bucket by (typically `month` or `week`). **Ungrouped path**: single line. **Grouped path** (when the user picks a `group_by`): one line per group, capped at 6 series; the tail rolls into "Other" so the legend stays legible. Series totals drive the cap selection. Missing bucket points render as `null` with `spanGaps: true` so a line breaks rather than zero-dipping through a gap month. **Empty-data**: when the query returns zero buckets, a `.tt-empty` panel renders in place of an empty canvas. **URL state**: no new query params — the existing `?kpi=…&filter_…=…&group_by=…` URL fully describes the chart. **Chart library**: reuses Chart.js 4.4.0 from CDN, the same script `FrontendComparisonView` already enqueues; the explorer enqueues it on demand via `wp_enqueue_script`. No new dependency. Placeholder text updated to drop "time-series chart" from the remaining-follow-ups list (drilldown + PDF still to ship via #874, #875). (closes #873) =

= 4.1.3 — Behaviour discoverability — sub-ship C: per-team bulk behaviour-rating grid (closes #872, closes #867). Final sub-ship under epic #867 — closes the parent. The natural coach workflow is "I just finished training; rate the 18 players who showed up" — per-player UX (sub-ships A + B) suits exception recording, but the bulk case needs its own surface. New view at `?tt_view=team-behaviour-capture&team_id=N`. Renders one row per active player on the team plus a single form-level activity picker at the top (defaults to the team's most recent completed activity). Each row has a rating dropdown (5–10 from `tt_config.rating_min/max`) and a notes input. Submit writes one `tt_player_behaviour_ratings` row per non-blank rating, all sharing the chosen `related_activity_id`. Blank rows write nothing — skipping is valid. Out-of-range ratings produce a per-row error message; valid rows on the same submit still write (partial success). **Cap-gated** on `tt_rate_player_behaviour`. **Team-scoped** — coaches see only teams they're assigned to via `QueryHelpers::get_teams_for_coach`; HoDs + admins see all teams. **Entry point**: a "Bulk-record behaviour" button on the team detail view's Roster section, cap-gated. Mobile-first CSS (`assets/css/frontend-team-behaviour-capture.css`) — rows stack at 360px, controls side-by-side at 600px+, sticky footer (with `env(safe-area-inset-bottom)`) keeps Save always accessible on phones. Dedicated capture view (`FrontendPlayerStatusCaptureView`) stays as the per-player history surface. No new REST endpoint (form-POST path is enough for v1; SaaS port can land `POST /teams/{id}/behaviour-ratings/bulk` as a follow-up). No new capability, no migration. (closes #872, closes #867) =

= 4.1.2 — Behaviour discoverability — sub-ship B: coach + HoD dashboard "Behaviour pending" widget (closes #871, partial #867). Pulls the work to the coach instead of waiting for them to dig for it. New `behaviour_pending` `DataTableWidget` preset surfacing players the user is responsible for who haven't had a behaviour rating in the last 14 days (configurable via `tt_config.behaviour_staleness_days`). Three columns: Player (link to profile carrying `action=log-behaviour` so #870's hero popover can auto-open on landing — pre-#870 wiring of that param the link still works, the popover just doesn't auto-open), Team, and "Since" (days since last rating or "never"). Empty state is positive copy — "Up to date — all your players have a recent behaviour rating" — so users with no overdue players see reassurance, not blank space. **Scoping**: users with `tt_manage_players` (HoDs + admins) see all active players in the club; users with only `tt_rate_player_behaviour` (coaches) see only players on teams they coach via `QueryHelpers::get_teams_for_coach`. Limited to 10 rows; ordered with `never-rated` first, then oldest-rated-first. New `BehaviourPendingSource` in `src/Modules/PersonaDashboard/TableSources/`, registered via the existing `TableRowSourceRegistry` pattern. Wired into the coach template at row 6 and the HoD template at row 9 (HoD tile rows shifted from y=9 to y=11 to make room). (closes #871, partial #867) =

= 4.1.1 — Behaviour discoverability — sub-ship A: hero quick-record popovers on the player profile (closes #870, partial #867). Replaces the buried "Capture behaviour and potential" button that lived below the Identity + Academy panels on the Profile tab — the entry point pilot couldn't find — with two cap-gated inline buttons on the player hero next to the status pill. Click "Log behaviour" or "Set potential" opens a popover (desktop) or bottom sheet (mobile, slides up from `env(safe-area-inset-bottom)`) carrying the form fields. Scouts (no caps) see neither button; status pill stands alone. = 4.1.0 — Behaviour discoverability — sub-ship D: optional "Behaviour today" step in the new-evaluation wizard (closes #869, partial #867). First of four sub-ships under epic #867 fixing the discoverability gap on behaviour + potential recording — most coaches never find their way to the dedicated capture surface because the only entry point is buried on the player profile. This ship ties behaviour to the same activity-first evaluation flow coaches already use for ratings, so a coach finishing a session can record behaviour without context-switching. A new `BehaviourStep` sits between `RateActorsStep` and `ReviewStep` on the activity-first path; it renders one row per rateable player with a rating dropdown (5-10 from `tt_config`) plus optional notes input. Step is fully skippable — submitting all blank values writes zero behaviour rows. Auto-skipped via `notApplicableFor()` when the wizard is on the player-first path OR the current user lacks `tt_rate_player_behaviour` (so scouts never see it). `ReviewStep` displays a Behaviour summary alongside the evaluation rows that will be written; on submit it iterates the captured ratings and calls `PlayerBehaviourRatingsRepository::create()` once per non-null entry with `related_activity_id` set to the wizard's activity so the player-status calculator can attribute the rating to the same session. No new REST endpoint, no new migration — entirely client-side wizard wiring plus an existing repository call. Minor bump (epic = feature; SemVer per v4.0.0). (closes #869, partial #867) =

= 4.0.11 — Exports page gains six bulk-export use cases (closes #865). Pilot completeness audit flagged six obvious bulk exports missing entirely — added in one ship to round out the central Exports surface. **Player evaluations (flat)** — one row per evaluation with main-category averages; CSV companion to the multi-sheet evaluations workbook (`evaluations_xlsx`) for coaches who want a flat filter-in-Excel sheet. **Team roster + season stats** — one row per player on the chosen team, with date-bounded attendance count, total minutes played, and mean rating across the period. **Team activity history** — one row per activity for a team within the date range, with attendance count and average rating. **Coach / staff directory** — non-parent `tt_people` rows with email, phone, role and the comma-joined list of assigned teams. **KPI snapshot** — single-sheet XLSX with point-in-time KPIs (active players, total players, active teams, activities-in-period, evaluations-in-period, attendance rows / present / %, goals total / active / completed). For board reports. **Audit log** — admin-only CSV dump of `tt_audit_log` with date range + action contains-match + entity_type exact-match filters. All six follow the existing `ExporterInterface` pattern, register in `ExportModule::boot()`, surface as cards on `FrontendExportsView` with form-driven filters, and cap-gate per existing capability matrix. Multi-format ones (csv + xlsx) reuse the chip toggle introduced in v4.0.10. No schema migration. Brings the bulk-exports total from 8 to 14. (closes #865) =

= 4.0.10 — Players list / Attendance register / Goals list bulk exports now offer XLSX in addition to CSV (closes #864). Coaches asked for XLSX so they can pivot in Excel without re-saving, share with parents/board, and preserve number formatting (CSV loses leading zeros on jersey numbers and date-scrambles depending on locale). Three exporters declare `supportedFormats() = [ 'csv', 'xlsx' ]` instead of CSV-only; their labels drop the trailing "(CSV)" since they're now multi-format. The existing `XlsxRenderer` gains a recognition path for the `[ 'headers' => …, 'rows' => … ]` payload shape returned by the CSV exporters, so the same `collect()` output feeds both renderers without per-exporter branching. The Exports page (`FrontendExportsView`) replaces the per-card `'format' => 'CSV'` shape with a `'formats' => [ 'csv', 'xlsx' ]` list; multi-format cards render a chip toggle (`.tt-export-card__format-chip`, `:has(input:checked)` for selected state, hidden radio buttons for keyboard accessibility); single-format cards keep their static badge and emit a hidden input. The JS picks `format` out of the FormData so the fallback filename extension reflects the user's choice. No schema, REST contract, or capability change. (closes #864) =

= 4.0.9 — Exports page look & feel pass (closes #863). The v1 from #797 carried inline styles, no min-card-height, a format pill jammed into a tight flex header, and a 320px grid minimum that broke descriptions mid-phrase on narrow viewports. Pilot quote: *"look and feel is terrible."* Rebuild: extract the inline styles into a new dedicated stylesheet `assets/css/frontend-exports.css`, enqueued via an `enqueueAssets()` override on the view; introduce a `.tt-export-card` BEM class set (`__header`, `__title`, `__format`, `__desc`, `__form`, `__field`, `__footer`, `__msg`); position the format pill absolutely in the card's top-right so it never competes with the title; raise the desktop grid minimum to 360px and stack to a single column below 768px (mobile-first); set `min-height: 260px` on every card and `margin-top: auto` on the footer so all cards in a row visually align regardless of description length or field count. Date / select / number / text inputs all 100% width with 44px min-height, applied via the stylesheet — no inline width gymnastics. Error message styling switched from inline `style.color` to a `.tt-export-card__msg--error` modifier class so a future dark-mode pass can override centrally. (closes #863) =

= 4.0.8 — Exports page no longer 403s on every Export click (closes #862). The `/talenttrack/v1/exports/{key}` REST route was registered `'methods' => 'GET'`, but the inline JS in `FrontendExportsView` submits filters as a JSON body via POST. Result: every Export button on the central Exports page (#797) returned 403 / 405. Two-part fix: (1) route now accepts both GET and POST so direct-link integrations keep working while the page's own POST goes through; (2) the run() handler now merges `get_query_params()` AND `get_json_params()` into the filter bag before passing it to the exporter, so filters carried in the POST body actually reach the export — previously only GET querystring filters were read. Cap-gating in `ExportService::run()` is unchanged. (closes #862) =

= 4.0.7 — Player Compare layout + radar + trend chart fixed (closes #878). Three defects landed in one ship since they share the same view. **Layout — header column-stack**: the player-header row was column-stacking on desktop because `.tt-fcompare-cell` had no `display:flex`; the `tt-fcompare-headerplayer` child had `flex-direction: row` but no parent flex context. Added `display:flex; align-items:center` to the cell base; removed the redundant `.tt-fcompare-label` class from the header div (it inherited `display:block` from a sibling rule). **Radar — wrong player**: `renderChartScripts()` was indexing the radar dataset as `$radar_sets[0]` for every player slot — both columns rendered Player A's radar. Now reads `$radar_sets[$pid]` keyed by the actual player ID, and pulls the latest snapshot via `end($snap['datasets'])` instead of assuming `[0]`. **Trend — only main-category series, no overall**: `PlayerStatsService::getTrendSeries()` returned one line per main category; the compare view's trend was a tangle of 4-6 thin lines per player with no aggregate. Added a synthetic "Overall" series at index 0 — the per-date mean across all main-category points, computed in PHP, so the trend chart now leads with a clear aggregate line and keeps the per-category lines below. No schema change; pure presentation + service-layer aggregation. (closes #878) =

= 4.0.6 — Person detail page renders profile + teams as tables instead of lists (closes #876). Visually aligns with the established Team-detail + Player-detail pattern. The profile fields block (Role / Email / Phone / Status) was a `<dl class="tt-profile-dl">`; teams were a `<ul class="tt-stack">`. Both rebuilt as `<table class="tt-profile-table">` — same class the Player + Team detail pages use, so styling is shared. The Teams table gets a two-column layout (Team / Functional role) so the functional role gets its own column instead of a `&middot;`-separated trail. `frontend-player-detail.css` now enqueued from the Person detail view so the `.tt-profile-table` styles apply. No data-shape change; PeopleRepository unchanged. No mobile regression — the table layout is the same one Player/Team already use at 360px. (closes #876) =

= 4.0.5 — HoD Upcoming Activities widget shows today's activities again (closes #858). The widget used a time-inclusive `CONCAT(session_date, ' ', start_time) >= NOW()` filter that excluded any activity that had already started today, even if it hadn't ended — an HoD opening the dashboard at 09:00 on a day with an 08:00 training saw the widget empty. Pilot quote: *"the hod dashboard, the upcoming activities list does not show anything while there are multiple teams with upcoming, planned activities."* Fix: align with the coach hero's date-inclusive filter (`session_date >= today`). "Upcoming" now means "today or later", not "literally hasn't started yet this minute". `apply_demo_scope` unchanged. Sibling audit: the CONCAT pattern existed only here. (closes #858) =

= 4.0.4 — HoD Team Overview widget — two bugs fixed (closes #857). **Layout overrun**: clicking a team to expand its player list bled below the widget's grid cell because the shared `.tt-pd-widget { height: 100% }` rule locked the widget to the cell, and the inline-expand body had no overflow guard. New widget-specific `.tt-pd-widget-team_overview_grid { height: auto }` override lets the widget grow with content; other widgets keep the height-locked behaviour. **Drill-down scope drift**: the widget emitted `?tt_view=players&team_id={id}` but `FrontendListTable` consumes `?filter[team_id]={id}` and the REST controller silently dropped the raw `team_id` — HoDs landed on the full club roster instead of the clicked team. Two-character URL fix. Mobile rendering unchanged. (closes #857) =

= 4.0.3 — Three v3.110.121 rating-scale-flip leftovers fixed (closes #866). All three lived past the original 1-5 → 5-10 sweep because their literals weren't covered by the grep audit. **Bug A — behaviour floor unreachable**: `MethodologyResolver` shipped default carried `behaviour_floor_below = 3.0` (the old 1-5 midpoint). Under 5-10 a behaviour average below 3.0 is impossible, so the floor-veto never fired for fresh installs. Now reads the midpoint of the active scale from `tt_config.rating_min/max` (7.5 on 5-10). The methodology config form clamps to the active range too. Help text updated. **Bug B — pitch-fit colours**: `PitchSvg` rendered fit scores ≥ 4.0 as green (= 40% of max on 5-10, so weak fits showed strong). Now thresholds compute as `rating_max × 0.80` (strong) / `× 0.50` (mid). **Bug C — team-fit panel `/ 5`**: `PlayerTeamFitPanel` displayed `7.8 / 5`. Denominator now reads from `tt_config.rating_max`, so the coach sees `7.8 / 10`. No migration — all three changes are config-driven runtime reads. (closes #866) =

= 4.0.2 — Quick Action widget Dutch labels now render translated on Dutch installs (closes #805). Root cause was structural, not a missing .po entry: `ActionCardWidget` used `__($action['label_key'], 'talenttrack')` — a dynamic call that `wp i18n make-pot` cannot extract. The 8 labels (`+ New evaluation`, `+ New goal`, `+ New activity`, `+ Add player`, `+ Add team`, `+ New scout report`, `+ New trial`, `+ New test training`) had been marked obsolete in the .po and rendered as the English msgid. Fix: introduce a static `actionLabel($id)` switch with literal `__()` calls so msgmerge can extract the msgids; un-obsolete the existing Dutch translations in `nl_NL.po` and add `+ New test training` which was missing. (closes #805) =

= 4.0.1 — Frontend entry-link URL helper now canonicalises via `home_url($path)` on the REQUEST_URI fallback (closes #860). Pilot on Strato hit 404 on `?tt_view=wizard&slug=new-team-blueprint&team_id=4` clicked from the Team Blueprints list. Root cause: `RecordLink::dashboardUrl()` returned `esc_url_raw(REQUEST_URI)` as its last-resort fallback, which on Strato's setup produced a URL that `add_query_arg` couldn't extend cleanly — every entry link built through the helper failed the same way. Fix mirrors the v3.110.180 `wizardStepUrl()` pattern: extract the path manually (no esc_url_raw round-trip), wrap via `home_url($path)`. Affects ~15+ surfaces that build entry URLs through this helper (every "+ New X" / "Edit Y" link constructed off `RecordLink::dashboardUrl()`). No regression on installs where `dashboard_page_id` is correctly configured — steps 1 and 2 of the fallback chain are unchanged. (closes #860) =

= 4.0.0 — Versioning reset: adopt strict SemVer. Cosmetic-only — no breaking change, no schema migration, no behaviour change. The pre-4 `3.110.x` patch counter ran away because every PR bumped patch by reflex; the reset draws a line. Going forward: **major** for operator-visible breaking changes (DB column, REST contract, capability matrix), **minor** for new feature epics (e.g. Match Execution shipping), **patch** for bug fixes + small enhancements. PUC (Plugin Update Checker) handles `4.0.0 > 3.110.216` natively via semver comparison; no operator action required on upgrade. Migration numbering continues independently (next is 0121). (closes #877) =

= 3.110.216 — Match execution surface for assistant coaches: a mobile-first live-match view (`?tt_view=match-execution&activity_id=N`) that the assistant runs from a phone on the sideline. Hard-depends on Match Prep (#838) — refuses to launch without a prep row and points the user back to the prep wizard. Layout fits the 360×640 phone viewport without scrolling: header (40), inline score steppers (48), timer with start/pause (44), specific-goals counter list (48 per row, tap = +1, long-press = -1), bench list with bring-on arrows (40 per row), sticky bottom-bar action that cycles through the half/match lifecycle states (1e → half-time → 2e → finished). Adds `home_score` + `away_score` to `tt_activities` and `minutes_played` to `tt_attendance` for the end-of-match copy. JS includes a localStorage queue keyed `tt_match_exec_queue_<activity_id>` so taps survive sideline dead zones; the queue flushes on the next successful response (no full offline-first — initial page load still requires server). Out of scope per pilot direction: per-goal records (scorer/assist), yellow/red cards, multi-device sync, stoppage time, auto-substitution suggestions. (closes #847) =
